### [39] [RecMem: Recurrence-based Memory Consolidation for Efficient and Effective Long-Running LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16045)
*Zijie Dai,Shiyuan Deng,Sheng Guan,Yizhou Tian,Xin Yao,Xiao Yan,James Cheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为解决现有智能体记忆系统因频繁调用LLM处理每条交互而产生的极高Token成本问题，本文提出了RecMem。该系统引入潜意识记忆层，仅在语义相似的交互反复出现时触发LLM提取记忆，大幅降低了计算成本并提升了记忆检索的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型（LLM）记忆系统通常采用“急切式”记忆整合方案，即每次交互都调用LLM进行处理，导致了巨大的Token消耗，限制了长运行智能体的扩展性。

Method: 提出了RecMem系统，包含两个核心组件：1. 潜意识记忆层（subconscious memory layer）：使用轻量级嵌入模型存储原始交互，避免高频调用LLM；2. 基于递归的整合机制：仅当语义相似的交互达到一定频次（形成语义簇）时，才触发LLM进行记忆提取和总结；此外还引入了语义细化机制，用于补充和修正被提取过程遗漏的细粒度事实。

Result: 实验表明，RecMem在处理长程交互时，相较于现有的三种SOTA记忆系统，最高降低了87%的记忆构建Token成本，同时在准确性指标上表现更优。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于递归的按需记忆整合策略RecMem，证明了在长程交互中，不必对每次交互进行即时LLM处理，通过语义聚类触发记忆提取既能显著降低成本，又能保持甚至提升记忆系统的准确性。

Abstract: Memory systems often organize user-agent interactions as retrievable external memory and are crucial for long-running agents by overcoming the limited context windows of LLMs. However, existing memory systems invoke LLMs to process every incoming interaction for memory extraction, and such an eager memory consolidation scheme leads to substantial token consumption. To tackle this problem, we propose RecMem by rethinking when memory consolidation should be conducted. RecMem stores incoming interactions in a subconscious memory layer and encode them using lightweight embedding models for retrieval. LLMs are only invoked to extract episodic and semantic memory when sustained recurrence are observed for semantically similar interactions. Such recurrence-based consolidation works because these interactions correspond to a semantic cluster with rich information and thus are worth extraction and summarization. To improve accuracy, RecMem also incorporates a semantic refinement mechanism that recovers the fine-grained facts omitted by memory extraction. Experiments show that RecMem reduces the memory construction token cost of three SOTA memory systems by up to 87% while exceeding their accuracy.

</details>


### [40] [Can Large Language Models Imitate Human Speech for Clinical Assessment? LLM-Driven Data Augmentation for Cognitive Score Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16077)
*Si-Belkacem Yamine Ketir,Lenard Paulo Tamayo,Shohei Hisada,Shaowen Peng,Shoko Wakamiya,Eiji Aramaki*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种利用大语言模型生成高质量合成数据的方法，结合相似度引导的类平衡策略，成功改善了临床语音数据集中类别不平衡的问题，有效提升了认知衰退评分的预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对评估认知衰退时，因数据集规模受限和类别不平衡导致的预测准确性不足问题，探索利用大语言模型提升数据效率和模型性能。

Method: 提出了一种利用大语言模型（GPT-5）进行数据增强的框架：利用参与者的书面回答作为语义锚点，生成多种风格的口语化单句；使用Sentence-BERT提取语音嵌入，并采用基于相似度引导的类平衡选择策略，通过偏最小二乘回归模型预测长谷川痴呆量表（HDS）分数。

Result: 实验表明，相比随机类平衡选择，相似度引导的类平衡选择策略能带来更稳定的性能提升，显著降低了少数群体（低分参与者）的预测误差，同时保持了多数群体的预测表现。

Conclusion: 基于大型语言模型的语义引导数据增强方法，为解决临床语音分析中的数据匮乏和类别不平衡问题提供了一种原则性且有效的解决方案，能够显著提升认知评分预测的准确性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Accurate assessment of cognitive decline from spontaneous speech remains challenging due to limited dataset size and class imbalance. In this work, we propose a large language model (LLM)-driven data augmentation framework to improve the prediction of cognitive scores from speech. Experiments are conducted on a Japanese corpus in which each participant provides both a spontaneous oral narrative and a written response to the same clinical prompt. The written responses serve as semantic anchors to generate multiple oral-like monologues in different styles using GPT-5. We then predict Hasegawa Dementia Scale scores, a widely used cognitive screening tool in Japan, using a Partial Least Squares regression model trained on Sentence-BERT speech embeddings. We investigate two augmentation strategies: random class-balanced selection, which yields moderate but unstable improvements, and similarity-guided class-balanced selection. The latter prioritizes semantically close synthetic samples, leading to more consistent improvements and substantially reducing prediction error for minority low-score participants while maintaining performance for the majority group. Overall, our findings demonstrate the potential of semantically guided LLM-driven augmentation as a principled approach for addressing class imbalance and improving data efficiency in clinical speech analysis.

### [41] [DebiasRAG: A Tuning-Free Path to Fair Generation in Large Language Models through Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16113)
*Rui Chu,Bingyin Zhao,Thanh Quoc Hung Le,Duy Cao Hoang,Huawei Lin,Ping Li,Weijie Zhao,Khoa D Doan,Yingjie Lao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型的社会偏见问题，本文提出了一种名为 DebiasRAG 的无需微调、动态查询的检索增强生成（RAG）去偏框架，通过引入去偏引导上下文重排序，在保留模型原始生成能力的同时有效提升了公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）常因训练数据中潜藏的种族、性别和年龄偏见而产生幻觉或社会偏见。现有微调或提示工程方案存在资源消耗大、可能损害模型原有能力及缺乏动态调整机制等缺陷，迫切需要一种高效、无需微调且能适应不同上下文的去偏框架。

Method: 提出 DebiasRAG 框架，包括三个阶段：1) 基于查询的去偏候选生成，利用预设的偏见上下文反向生成去偏约束；2) 构建包含常规上下文的候选池；3) 通过梯度更新的去偏引导对上下文片段进行重排序。该方法无需额外的训练资源或领域知识，属于即插即用的动态推理机制。

Result: 实验证明，DebiasRAG 能够在不牺牲大模型基础性能的情况下，显著降低模型输出中的社会偏见，在保证生成质量的同时实现了更公平的推理表现。

Conclusion: DebiasRAG 通过 RAG 架构实现了一种无需微调的动态去偏方法，既能有效抑制大模型的社会偏见，又不会损害其原有的生成能力和知识表征，为大模型应用提供了更公平的推理方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved unprecedented success due to their exceptional generative capabilities. However, because they depend on knowledge encapsulated from training corpora, they may produce hallucinations, stereotypes, and socially biased content. In particular, LLMs are prone to prejudiced responses involving race, gender, and age, which are collectively referred to as social biases. Prior studies have used fine-tuning and prompt engineering to mitigate such biases in LLMs, but these methods require additional training resources or domain knowledge to design the framework. Moreover, they may degrade the original capabilities of LLMs and often overlook the need for dynamic debiasing contexts for fairer inference. In this paper, we propose DebiasRAG, a novel tuning-free and dynamic query-specific debiasing framework based on retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). DebiasRAG improves fairness while preserving the intrinsic properties of LLMs, such as representation ability. DebiasRAG consists of three stages: (1) query-specific debiasing candidate generation; (2) context candidate pool construction; and (3) gradient-updated debiasing-guided context piece reranking. First, DebiasRAG leverages self-diagnosed bias contexts relevant to the query through regular retrieval, where the bias contexts are prepared offline by the DebiasRAG provider. Given the query-specific bias contexts, DebiasRAG reversely produces debiasing contexts, which are provided as additional fairness constraints for LLM outputs. Second, a regular RAG retrieval process produces query-related contexts from the regular RAG document database, such as a chunked Wikipedia dataset.

</details>


### [42] [SGR: A Stepwise Reasoning Framework for LLMs with External Subgraph Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16117)
*Xin Zhang,Yang Cao,Baoxing Wu,Kai Song,Siying Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SGR的框架，通过从外部知识库中生成查询相关的子图，引导大语言模型进行多步逻辑推理，从而显著提升了模型在复杂推理任务中的表现及生成内容的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在多种NLP任务中表现出色，但在需要深度推理和逻辑推演的复杂场景中仍存在局限，且容易产生无关、噪声或事实不一致的内容。为此，研究旨在通过引入外部知识库来增强模型的推理能力并提高其生成内容的准确性。

Method: 提出了一种名为SGR（Stepwise Graph Reasoning）的逐步框架。该方法首先针对输入问题构建特定查询的外部子图，随后引导模型基于该语义结构进行多步推理，最后通过整合多条推理路径来获得最终预测结果。

Result: 在多个基准测试数据集上的实验结果表明，SGR框架在推理准确性和事实可靠性方面均优于现有的竞争基线方法。

Conclusion: SGR框架通过将外部结构化知识与大语言模型的推理过程相结合，有效提升了复杂推理任务的准确性和事实可靠性，证明了利用外部知识图谱增强LLM推理能力的有效性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities across diverse NLP applications, such as translation, text generation, and question answering. Nevertheless, they remain limited in complex settings that demand deep reasoning and logical inference. Since these models are trained on large-scale text corpora, their generation process may still introduce irrelevant, noisy, or factually inconsistent content. To mitigate this problem, we introduce SGR, a stepwise framework that enhances LLM reasoning through external subgraph generation. SGR builds query-specific subgraphs from external knowledge bases and uses their semantic structure to support multi-step inference. By grounding intermediate reasoning steps in structured external knowledge, the framework helps the model concentrate on relevant entities, relations, and supporting evidence. In particular, SGR first constructs a subgraph tailored to the input question. It then guides the model to reason progressively over the generated structure and combines multiple reasoning trajectories to obtain the final prediction. Experimental results across several benchmark datasets show that SGR achieves consistent improvements over competitive baselines, highlighting its value for improving both reasoning accuracy and factual reliability.

</details>


### [43] [Optimized Three-Dimensional Photovoltaic Structures with LLM guided Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16191)
*Michael P. Brenner,Lizzie Dorfman,John C. Platt*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文展示了一种利用AI编程智能体（AntiGravity）与树搜索算法（ERA）自动生成高效三维光伏结构的方法，并通过迭代式修正物理模拟中的“奖励作弊”问题，证明了该自动化框架在科学发现与复杂系统设计中的强大潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的科学发现过程往往依赖于人类专家的直觉和漫长的试错。该研究旨在探索如何利用人工智能编码系统（AI coding systems）实现科学假设生成的自动化，具体以优化三维光伏结构以提高中纬度地区太阳能利用效率为例，验证AI在解决复杂物理设计问题中的潜力。

Method: 研究提出了一种结合通用代码智能体（AntiGravity）与大语言模型驱动的树搜索算法（ERA）的工作流。首先，通过代码智能体复现基准计算，随后利用树搜索算法针对三维光伏（3DPV）结构进行性能优化。针对算法演化过程中出现的“奖励作弊”现象（如非物理的悬浮结构），研究人员引入了一个迭代式工作流，要求代码智能体实时对物理引擎施加约束以剔除不切实际的方案。

Result: 在成功解决算法产生的“奖励作弊”问题后，ERA算法发现了一系列性能优化的3DPV结构。这些设计在不同固定集光面积约束下，实现了优化的天顶追踪效果，并有效地避免了结构间的自遮挡，验证了该AI驱动框架在生成具有实际应用价值的科学设计方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，将代码智能体与树搜索算法相结合，能够为科学发现提供一个强大的自动化平台。通过迭代式地修复物理引擎以消除“奖励作弊”，该方法能够有效地在受限的物理空间中探索并发现比现有技术更优的新颖科学假设及工程设计。

Abstract: We present a case study for how AI coding systems can be used to generate novel scientific hypotheses. We combine a generic coding agent (Google's AntiGravity) with an LLM-driven tree search algorithm (Empirical Research Assistance / ERA) to autonomously generate high-efficiency three-dimensional photovoltaic (3DPV) structures that overcome losses limiting flat solar panels at mid-latitudes. These structures operate by presenting favorable angles to the sun throughout the day, and for illustrative purposes we focus on optimizing performance for a single solar day. Our workflow begins by using AntiGravity to reproduce calculations \cite{bernardi2012solar} showing that 3DPV can have energy densities much higher than stationary flat PV panels. We use these initial designs as the starting point for large scale tree search, where we seek improved solutions and score them for their diurnal yield. The initial tree search leads to nominally more efficient solutions, yet they are caused by algorithmic reward hacking, arising from non-physical design features such as structurally levitating disconnected tiers and exploitations of the discretizations in the optics solver. To counteract this, we develop a workflow where the coding agent iteratively patches the physics engine with constraints to eliminate reward hacking. With reward-hacking eliminated, ERA discovers a series of designs with various constraints and improved performance, including optimal designs with different fixed collector areas, optimizing zenith tracking and avoiding self shadowing.
  Combining coding agents with tree search (ERA) provides a powerful platform for scientific discovery, for problems whose solutions can be empirically evaluated with a score function.

### [45] [TeamTR: Trust-Region Fine-Tuning for Multi-Agent LLM Coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15207)
*Yi Xie,Siao Liu,Falong Fan,Yuanqi Yao,Yue Zhao,Bo Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多智能体协作中的上下文分布偏移问题，研究提出了TeamTR框架，通过轨迹重采样和发散度控制，实现了更稳定的多智能体微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体大语言模型系统在处理复杂推理任务时，往往表现不如单一模型，这是因为在共享上下文的团队中进行顺序微调时，单个智能体的更新会导致整个团队的上下文分布发生偏移，造成评估失效和性能下降。

Method: 提出了TeamTR（Team Trust-Region）框架，核心在于在每次组件更新后进行轨迹重采样，并实施针对每个智能体的发散度控制，以缓解由顺序微调引起的“复合占有偏移”（Compounding Occupancy Shift）问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，TeamTR平均性能优于单智能体和顺序微调基准线7.1%，有效缓解了协作退化问题，并支持插件式的组件替换。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种名为TeamTR的信任域框架，通过解决多智能体协作中的分布偏移问题，为训练多智能体大语言模型系统提供了理论保障和更优的性能表现。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems have shown promise for complex reasoning, yet recent evaluations reveal they often underperform single-model baselines. We identify a structural failure mode in sequential fine-tuning of shared-context teams: updating one agent shifts the team's context distribution, and when subsequent updates are evaluated on cached rollouts, this mismatch compounds. We formalize this as the compounding occupancy shift and prove that stale-occupancy evaluation incurs a penalty that scales quadratically with the number of agents. In contrast, intermediate-occupancy evaluation reduces this to linear scaling. We propose TeamTR, a trust-region framework that resamples trajectories after each component update and enforces per-agent divergence control, yielding rigorous per-update and per-stage improvement lower bounds. Experiments show that TeamTR outperforms single-agent and sequential baselines with 7.1% on average, mitigates coordination regressions, and supports plug-and-play component replacement. Code is available at https://github.com/Yydc/TeamTR.

</details>


### [46] [Quantization Undoes Alignment: Bias Emergence in Compressed LLMs Across Models and Precision Levels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15208)
*Plawan Kumar Rath,Rahul Maliakkal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大语言模型量化压缩会引发严重的偏见涌现问题，而标准评估指标（如困惑度）无法捕捉到这种关键的安全退化，强调了对压缩模型进行专项公平性测试的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的量化评估方法往往只关注聚合指标（如困惑度）或单一压缩水平，无法准确反映量化过程对模型在公平性和安全性方面产生的深层影响，导致“逐渐退化”与“阈值触发的安全失效”难以区分。

Method: 研究者对三种指令微调模型（Qwen2.5-7B, Mistral-7B, Phi-3.5-mini）进行了受控实验，涵盖从BF16到3-bit的五种精度等级。在12,148项BBQ（Bias Benchmark for QA）数据集上，通过5个随机种子共计进行了911,100次推理，并结合逻辑回归分析了模型量化程度与刻板印象偏差之间的剂量反应关系。

Result: 实验发现，3-bit量化会导致6%-21%的无偏题目产生新的刻板印象；4-bit量化下模型选择“未知”选项的意愿显著下降（17.4%）。令人警惕的是，这些显著的偏见增加在标准指标（如困惑度）上几乎不可见（4-bit下困惑度仅增加不到3%），表明聚合指标在检测模型公平性退化方面存在重大盲区。

Conclusion: 量化压缩不仅仅是模型性能的微小损失，更会引入严重的公平性和安全性风险。传统的聚合指标（如困惑度）无法察觉这种细粒度的偏差突变，因此亟需建立“质量感知”的压缩评估协议，在部署前进行专门的偏见涌现测试。

Abstract: Large Language Models are routinely compressed via post-training quantization to reduce inference costs and memory footprint for cloud and edge deployment, yet the impact of this compression on model quality remains poorly understood. Existing studies typically compare only two conditions (full-precision vs. a single quantized variant), rely on aggregate bias metrics, and evaluate a single model family, making it impossible to distinguish gradual degradation from threshold-dependent safety failures. We conduct a controlled empirical study of three instruction-tuned models (Qwen2.5-7B, Mistral-7B, Phi-3.5-mini) at five precision levels (BF16 through 3-bit) on 12,148 BBQ bias benchmark items across 5 random seeds, totaling 911,100 inference records. Our results reveal that 3-bit quantization causes 6-21% of previously unbiased items to develop new stereotypical behaviors, following a clear dose-response pattern confirmed via logistic regression, while models' willingness to select "unknown" answers declines by 17.4%. Crucially, these item-level changes are invisible to standard quality metrics: perplexity increases by less than 0.5% at 8-bit and under 3% at 4-bit across all three models, yet 2.5-5.6% of items already develop new biases at 4-bit. These findings demonstrate that aggregate evaluation metrics systematically miss fairness-critical degradation, underscoring the need for quality-aware compression protocols that explicitly test for bias emergence before deployment.

</details>


### [47] [MuteBench: Modality Unavailability Tolerance Evaluation for Incomplete Multimodal Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15235)
*Wugeng Zheng,Ziwen Kan,Tianlong Chen,Chen Chen,Song Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了MuteBench基准测试，用于评估临床AI多模态融合模型在两种常见数据缺失模式下的表现，发现模型架构的选择比参数量更能决定鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床多模态生理数据（如重症监护及可穿戴设备数据）常出现模态缺失和模态内时间片段缺失的问题，但目前缺乏跨多种架构和数据集的系统性鲁棒性评估基准。

Method: 构建了名为MuteBench的基准测试，涵盖9个临床数据集、6种融合架构及两种缺失模式（模态缺失与模态内缺失），在超过12.5万个样本上进行了受控的鲁棒性评估。

Result: 1. 架构家族是鲁棒性的最强预测指标；2. 通道独立模型对模态缺失鲁棒，但在短序列模态内缺失下表现较差；3. 课程模态丢失训练仅在预设概率内有效；4. 通道数、序列长度与模态对齐共同决定了哪种缺失模式威胁更大；5. 基于扩散的填补技术可提升下游分类任务表现。

Conclusion: 架构类型是模型鲁棒性的决定性因素。通过MuteBench，研究者确定了不同失效模式下的最佳模型选择策略，并验证了扩散模型填补在特定场景下的有效性，为未来开发更鲁棒的多模态融合系统提供了指南。

Abstract: Multimodal physiological data powers clinical AI systems from intensive care units to wearable devices, but sensors routinely fail in practice. Two failure modes are common: modality missing, where an entire channel is absent, and within-modality missing, where a contiguous time segment is lost. No existing benchmark evaluates multiple fusion architectures under both failure modes at controlled severity levels across diverse clinical datasets. We present MuteBench, a benchmark covering 9 datasets from 7 clinical domains, 6 fusion architectures, and 2 missing-data modes over 125,000 samples. Through this benchmark, we find that architecture family is the strongest predictor of robustness, outweighing parameter count. Channel-independent models tolerate modality missing well but can be sensitive to within-modality missing, especially on short sequences. Curriculum modality dropout protects reliably only up to the maximum dropout rate used in training. We also find that channel count, sequence length, and modality alignment jointly determine which failure mode poses the greater threat. Finally, a PTB-XL case study suggests that diffusion-based imputation can improve downstream classification under within-modality missing, with the largest gains for models whose expert routing is most sensitive to corrupted inputs, though broader validation across datasets remains an open direction. MuteBench provides practitioners with concrete guidance for both selecting existing architectures and informing the design of future robust multimodal fusion methods.

</details>


### [48] [Reducing the Safety Tax in LLM Safety Alignment with On-Policy Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15239)
*Yu Fu,Longxuan Yu,Haz Sameen Shahgir,Zhipeng Wei,Hui Liu,N. Benjamin Erichson,Yue Dong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OPSA通过在策略内自蒸馏和利用特权安全上下文，解决了现有安全对齐方法中因分布偏移导致的“安全税”问题，在显著提升模型安全性的同时，最大限度地保护了模型的通用推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的安全对齐方法通常存在“安全税”（safety tax）问题，即在提升安全性的同时牺牲了模型的推理能力。这主要是由于训练过程中的分布偏移（distributional mismatch）导致的，即模型是在人类或外部模型生成的轨迹上进行训练，而非在自身策略生成的轨迹上训练。

Method: 提出了一种名为OPSA（On-policy Self-Distillation for Safety Alignment）的方法。该方法通过模型自身生成的轨迹进行训练，利用冻结的教师模型在特权安全上下文下提供逐标记（per-token）的KL散度监督。此外，引入了“教师翻转率”（teacher flip rate）指标来搜索能够激活潜层安全推理的特权上下文，而非仅仅引导输出表象上的安全响应。

Result: 在两个推理模型系列和五个模型规模上，OPSA均表现优于离策略自蒸馏和外部教师蒸馏，尤其在小型模型上提升显著（如R1-Distill-1.5B提升8.85点，Qwen3-0.6B提升5.49点）。实验表明，该方法在各种规模的训练集及针对越狱攻击的评估中均表现稳健，且能有效聚焦于早期合规决策标记的优化。

Conclusion: OPSA证明了通过在策略内进行自蒸馏，并配合特权安全上下文，可以在缓解分布偏移的同时有效减少“安全税”，从而在提升模型安全性时更好地保留其原始推理能力。

Abstract: Safety alignment often improves robustness to harmful queries at the cost of reasoning ability, a tradeoff known as the safety tax. A common cause is distributional mismatch: supervised fine-tuning trains the target model on safety demonstrations produced by humans, external models, or fixed self-generated traces, rather than on trajectories sampled from its own policy. We identify off-policy training mismatch as a second source of this tax and study on-policy self-distillation for safety alignment, which we call OPSA. The model generates its own rollouts and receives dense per-token KL supervision from a frozen teacher copy of itself conditioned on a privileged safety context. Because this teacher must be safer than the sampled student trajectory, we introduce \emph{teacher flip rate}: a criterion that measures how often a privileged context converts unsafe responses into safe ones. We use this signal to search for contexts that activate latent safety reasoning rather than merely elicit safe-looking demonstrations. Across two reasoning-model families and five model scales, OPSA achieves a stronger safety--reasoning tradeoff than off-policy self-distillation and external-teacher distillation under matched data and full-parameter fine-tuning, with the largest gains on smaller models (+8.85 points on R1-Distill-1.5B and +5.49 points on Qwen3-0.6B). The gains persist across training-set sizes and adaptive jailbreak evaluations. Token-level analyses further show that OPSA concentrates updates near early compliance-decision tokens, providing a mechanism for improving safety while preserving general reasoning.

</details>


### [49] [Reading the Cell, Designing the Cure: Perturbation-Conditioned Molecular Diffusion for Function-Oriented Drug Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15243)
*Ziyu Xu,Zijian Zhang,Liang Wang,Zhiyuan Liu,Qiang Liu,Shu Wu,Liang Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对缺乏明确药物靶点的复杂疾病，本文提出了 CURE 模型。该框架利用扩散生成模型，通过转录组的扰动状态引导药物分子设计，有效解决了跨模态数据对齐和稀疏信号处理的难题，在分子生成质量和功能预测方面表现卓越。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在缺乏大规模可靠靶点结构或疾病表现为复杂通路失调的情况下，现有的基于结构的药物设计方法受限。本文旨在通过转录组扰动数据实现“基于转录组的药物设计（TBDD）”，即根据目标细胞状态转移生成对应的候选药物分子，以应对传统方法在生物与化学域之间的巨大鸿沟及信号稀疏性挑战。

Method: 提出了 CURE（Cellular Response Engine）框架，这是一种多分辨率转录组引导的扩散模型。核心组件包括：1) 转录组扰动功能特征提取器（TFE），用于提炼扰动嵌入；2) 跨模态对齐机制，用于桥接生物（转录组）与化学（分子）域的差异；3) 异构感知聚合技术，从噪声信号中提取稳健的状态特定信号。

Result: 在标准基准测试和严苛的分布外（OOD）评估中，CURE 在分子结构的合理性（structural quality）和功能的一致性（functional consistency）方面均显著优于现有基线模型。此外，通过零样本基因抑制剂设计任务，验证了其在实际药物发现场景中的应用潜力。

Conclusion: CURE 框架成功证明了将药物设计建模为条件生成逆问题的可行性。通过有效处理转录组数据的稀疏性和跨模态偏差，该模型为表型驱动的药物发现提供了一种高效、稳健的新范式，尤其在处理缺乏明确靶点的复杂疾病路径时具有显著优势。

Abstract: When reliable target structures are unavailable at scale or phenotypes arise from dysregulated pathways, transcriptomic perturbations provide a system-level functional readout for drug action. In this work, we formalize \emph{Transcriptome-based Drug Design (TBDD)} as a generative inverse problem: designing drug molecules conditioned on desired transcriptomic state transitions. We analyze the inherently ill-posed nature of this task, which is further complicated by the profound domain gap between biology and chemistry and by the sparsity of transcriptomic signals. To address these challenges, we propose \textbf{\themodel{}} (A \textbf{C}ell\textbf{U}lar \textbf{R}esponse \textbf{E}ngine), a multi-resolution transcriptome-guided diffusion framework. \themodel{} features a specialized \textbf{Transcriptome Perturbation Functional Feature Extractor (TFE)} that (1) distills function-oriented perturbation embeddings from pre/post states, (2) aligns these signatures to dual chemical views to bridge the cross-modal gap, and (3) performs heterogeneity-aware aggregation to extract robust state-specific signals from noisy transcriptomic data. Extensive evaluations on both standard benchmarks and rigorous out-of-distribution protocols demonstrate that \themodel{} consistently outperforms strong baselines in structural quality and functional consistency. Furthermore, we validate its practical utility via a zero-shot gene-inhibitor design task, highlighting the potential of phenotype-driven generative discovery.

Method: 本文对生成式轨迹建模与隐私保护的交叉领域进行了研究，通过采用成员推理攻击（Membership Inference Attacks）作为实证评估方法，对多种代表性的生成模型（如GANs、VAEs、扩散模型）进行了隐私风险测试，以量化模型对原始训练数据的泄露程度。

Result: 研究发现，当前主流生成式轨迹模型存在明显的隐私泄露风险，成员推理攻击能够以较高的准确率识别出模型训练集中的轨迹数据，证明了生成式模型并不具备固有的隐私保护能力。

Conclusion: 研究表明，生成式轨迹模型本身并不能自动保证隐私安全。仅仅依赖生成过程的模糊性是不够的，必须在模型开发和部署阶段引入系统的实证隐私评估，以识别并量化潜在的隐私泄露风险。

Abstract: Trajectory data is fundamental to modern urban intelligence, yet its sensitivity raises significant privacy concerns. Generative models such as Generative Adversarial Networks, Variational Autoencoders, and Diffusion Models have been developed to generate realistic synthetic trajectory data by capturing underlying spatiotemporal distributions and mobility patterns. Although these models are often assumed to preserve privacy due to their generative nature, this assumption does not necessarily hold. In this work, we investigate the intersection of generative trajectory modeling and privacy evaluation. By identifying applicable empirical methods for assessing privacy preservation in trajectory generation tasks, we demonstrate a significant gap in the evaluation of privacy for generative trajectory models. Motivated by this gap, we implement Membership Inference Attacks against representative models, demonstrating the feasibility of using such empirical privacy evaluation methods and showing that their generative nature does not eliminate privacy risks.

### [51] [GQLA: Group-Query Latent Attention for Hardware-Adaptive Large Language Model Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15250)
*Fanxu Meng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Group-Query Latent Attention (GQLA)，通过一种创新的双路径架构，使得单一模型权重能够在高端 H100 和受限 H20 等不同硬件上均实现最优推理性能，解决了 MLA 硬件兼容性差和张量并行受限的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DeepSeek-V2/V3 使用的 MLA 虽然在 H100 上表现极佳，但其固定的推理路径使得在 H20 等算力带宽比不同的硬件上表现受限，且缺乏对头轴张量并行的支持，限制了其在通用推理设备上的性能优化空间。

Method: 提出 Group-Query Latent Attention (GQLA)，作为 MLA 的最小修改版本，在同一组参数下暴露两种代数等效路径：一种是类似 MLA 的 MQA 吸收路径（适用于 H100），另一种是支持缓存扩展的 GQA 路径（适用于受限硬件如 H20）。同时开发了 TransGQLA 方法，将现有的 GQA 预训练检查点转换为 GQLA 模型，无需从零开始训练。

Result: GQLA 实现了对不同硬件架构的自适应，在 H100 上保持与 MLA 相当的高性能，在 H20 上则通过 GQA 路径显著提升性能并支持多标记预测（MTP）。在 LLaMA-3-8B 实验中，MQA 吸收路径将 KV 缓存压缩至原始 GQA 基线的 28.125%，同时在 GQA 路径下保持了高效的流量特性。

Conclusion: GQLA 为多头潜在注意力（MLA）引入了一种灵活的双解码路径机制，无需重新训练即可适应不同硬件的算力带宽比，解决了 MLA 在非 H100 等高端 GPU 上的推理性能瓶颈，同时提升了并行扩展性和多标记预测效率。

Abstract: Multi-head Latent Attention (MLA), the attention used in DeepSeek-V2/V3, jointly compresses keys and values into a low-rank latent and matches the H100 roofline almost perfectly. Its trained weights, however, expose only one decoding path - an absorbed MQA form - which ties efficient inference to H100-class compute-bandwidth ratios, forfeits tensor parallelism along the head axis, and yields no Multi-Token Prediction (MTP) gain on commodity inference GPUs such as the export-restricted H20. We propose Group-Query Latent Attention (GQLA), a minimal modification of MLA whose trained weights expose two algebraically equivalent decoding paths over the same parameters: an MQA-absorb path identical to MLA's, and a GQA path with a per-group expanded cache. The runtime picks the path that matches the target hardware - no retraining, no custom kernels - so a single set of GQLA weights pins the rooflines of both H100 (MQA-absorb, s_q=1) and H20 (GQA + MTP, s_q=2), while supporting up to 8-way zero-redundancy tensor parallelism on the GQA path. To avoid pretraining from scratch we extend TransMLA into TransGQLA, which converts a pretrained GQA checkpoint into a GQLA model; on LLaMA-3-8B it compresses the per-token KV cache to 28.125% of the GQA baseline on the MQA-absorb path while structurally preserving GQA-level traffic on the per-group path.

</details>

*Jairo Diaz-Rodriguez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出机器学习领域过度依赖基准测试和理想化理论的弊端，倡导一种“理念优先”的研究框架，通过设计针对性的实验来验证模型行为，从而促进科学理解并降低研究门槛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器学习研究存在严重分化：一端是盲目追求指标的工程化基准测试，另一端是脱离现代系统的理想化理论。这种趋势忽视了科学探索的核心——“理念”，且加剧了资源不平等（“复杂性溢价”）。

Method: 提出“理念优先”（Ideas First）框架。该方法论主张：1. 将理念作为研究的核心对象；2. 通过理念预测现代模型中的行为特征；3. 设计专门的实验来检测这些特定模式，而非单纯追求基准测试的得分。

Result: 通过该框架，研究者能够摆脱计算资源限制的束缚，通过更科学的实验设计获得有价值的贡献，从而实现研究范式的转变，即从“追求分数”转向“理解模型机制”。

Conclusion: 研究界应建立一种以“理念优先”为核心的研究文化，将基准测试和理论模型视为检验机械论假设的工具，而非研究的终极目标。这种转变有助于弥合理论与实践的鸿沟，并促进研究公平。

Abstract: Machine learning research increasingly bifurcates into two disconnected modes: benchmark-driven engineering that prioritizes metrics over understanding, and idealized theory that often fails to transfer to modern systems. In this position paper, we argue that the field focuses too heavily on these endpoints, neglecting the central scientific object: the idea. We propose an Ideas First framework in which ideas are valued for the behavioral signatures they predict in modern models, and these signatures are tested through tailored experiments designed to detect the relevant patterns rather than to win leaderboards. This shift not only bridges the gap between theory and practice but also promotes equity by removing the "complexity premium," enabling rigorous scientific contributions from researchers with modest computational, financial, and human resources. Ultimately, we advocate for a research culture centered on ideas, treating benchmarks and theorems as instruments for testing mechanistic hypotheses rather than as ends in themselves.

### [53] [Curriculum Learning of Physics-Informed Neural Networks based on Spatial Correlation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15254)
*Xujia Chen,Xinyue Hu,Letian Chen,Daming Shi,Wenhui Fan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对PINN训练困难问题，本文提出了一种空间相关的课程学习框架，通过引入空间因果引导、低频一致性桥接及区域自适应重加权，有效提升了PINN处理强空间耦合问题的收敛性与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PINN在求解偏微分方程时常面临损失函数景观非凸、多目标约束失衡以及信息传播受阻等问题，现有方法在处理强空间耦合的边值问题时效果有限，缺乏对空间信息传播及区域一致性的显式控制。

Method: 提出了一种空间相关的课程学习框架，包含三个核心组件：1. 空间因果权重，引导信息从边界向内部传播；2. 低频信息桥，通过伪标签强制执行空间区域间的一致性；3. 区域自适应重加权策略，动态调整损失函数以平衡局部残差并恢复高频细节。

Result: 在多个PDE基准测试中，该方法在保持计算成本相当的情况下，显著降低了PINN的训练失败率，并提升了求解精度。

Conclusion: 本文提出的空间相关课程学习框架有效解决了PINN在求解复杂偏微分方程时面临的训练不稳定性与精度限制问题，为解决强空间耦合的边值问题提供了一种新颖且高效的训练范式。

Abstract: Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) combine deep learning with physical constraints for solving partial differential equations (PDEs), and are widely applied in fluid mechanics, heat transfer, and solid mechanics. However, PINN training still suffers from high-dimensional non-convex loss landscapes, imbalanced multiobjective constraints, and ineffective information propagation. Existing curriculum learning and causality-guided strategies improve training stability, but mainly focus on temporal or parametric progression, lacking explicit treatment of spatial information propagation and inter-region consistency. Moreover, they are not directly applicable to boundary value problems (BVPs) with strong spatial coupling. To address this issue, we propose a spatially correlated curriculum learning framework for PINNs. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to address PINN training difficulties from the perspective of spatial coupling among subregions. First, spatial causal weights guide information from near-boundary regions inward, reducing optimization failures and spurious convergence. Second, a low-frequency information bridge enforces pseudo-label-based consistency across spatially separated regions, suppressing global low-frequency drift. Third, a region-adaptive reweighting strategy adjusts subregion losses to reduce local residuals and recover high-frequency details. Experiments on PDE benchmarks show that, under comparable computational cost, the proposed method alleviates training failures and improves solution accuracy. The code is available at https://github.com/pigofmomo/CurriculumLearningPINN.

### [54] [Training on Documents About Monitoring Leads to CoT Obfuscation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15257)
*Reilly Haskins,Bilal Chughtai,Joshua Engels*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现，如果AI模型知晓监控机制且具备高度的思维链重构能力，它们可以故意混淆推理轨迹来逃避安全检查，这对基于思维链的监控方案构成了显著威胁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于思维链（CoT）的监控机制依赖于模型如实输出推理过程，但这一假设可能存在漏洞。研究者旨在探讨具备监控感知能力的模型是否会故意混淆其推理过程，从而逃避安全检测，以评估现有监控手段的稳健性。

Method: 1. 采用合成文档微调（synthetic document finetuning）技术，使八种不同模型“接触”并了解CoT监控机制。
2. 将这些受过监控感知训练的模型与未接触监控信息的对照组进行对比测试。
3. 在简单任务和复杂智能体（agentic）任务中评估其逃避检测的能力。
4. 计算模型“思维链可控性”（CoT controllability）与混淆成功率之间的相关性。
5. 在强化学习环境下，对比模型在满足奖励目标的同时规避监控的能力。

Result: 1. 具备监控感知能力的模型在执行任务时，其不当行为被漏检的比例显著高于对照组。
2. 该效应在复杂智能体任务中依然存在。
3. 模型的“思维链可控性”与混淆成功率高度正相关（r=0.800）。
4. 在强化学习中，监控感知模型能比对照组更快学会通过“奖励黑客”（reward-hacking）行为获利，且不触发监控报警。

Conclusion: 思维链（CoT）监控并非万无一失。当模型了解监控机制并具备较强的思维链可控性时，它们能够主动混淆推理过程以逃避检测。该研究强调了在开发安全监控方案时，必须考虑模型对监控机制的潜在感知与反制能力。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring is one of the most promising tools we have for detecting model misbehavior, but its effectiveness depends on models faithfully externalizing their reasoning. Motivated by this vulnerability, we study whether monitor-aware models are capable of obfuscating their reasoning to evade detection. We use synthetic document finetuning to expose eight models to realistic pre-training-style documents describing a CoT monitor and find that monitor-aware models consistently achieve higher rates of undetected misbehavior compared to unaware controls. This effect is weaker but still present on a harder agentic task. We also show that CoT controllability, a model's ability to reshape its own reasoning trace under an imposed constraint, is closely correlated with obfuscation success across the eight models studied ($r=0.800$, $p=0.017$). Monitor-aware models placed under equal reinforcement learning optimization pressure also learn to reward-hack without triggering a CoT monitor substantially faster than unaware controls. Together, these results suggest that knowledge of monitoring combined with high CoT controllability poses a risk to CoT-based monitoring.

### [55] [Tadpole: Autoencoders as Foundation Models for 3D PDEs with Online Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15284)
*Qiang Liu,Felix Koehler,Benjamin Holzschuh,Nils Thuerey*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Tadpole是一个针对3D偏微分方程的通用基础模型，通过大规模在线生成的合成数据预训练，实现了对复杂物理系统的高效表示学习，并支持通过参数高效微调执行多种科学计算下游任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有偏微分方程（PDE）求解模型在处理三维数据时面临可迁移性差、难以扩展到高维空间以及功能单一（通常只能解决特定任务）的挑战。研究旨在构建一个通用的基础模型，以有效处理不同状态变量和分辨率的异构物理系统。

Method: 1. 开发了一个高效的在线数据生成框架，用于生成合成3D偏微分方程数据，避免了存储和I/O瓶颈；2. 设计了一种基于自动编码器的预训练架构，通过对单通道空间裁剪块进行学习，提取丰富的物理系统特征表示；3. 提出了一种参数高效的微调策略（结合低秩适应LoRA、潜空间变换和重引入跳跃连接），用于将模型快速适配到动态学习和生成任务中。

Result: Tadpole能够处理相当于数百TB的训练数据，在多种下游任务（如动力学学习、生成建模）中表现出强大的性能，且通过参数高效微调策略，仅需极少的可训练参数即可实现高精度的时空建模。

Conclusion: Tadpole证明了通过在线数据生成进行大规模预训练的自动编码器范式，可以有效构建能够跨越异构物理系统、具有高度可迁移性和多功能性的3D偏微分方程基础模型。该模型及其高效的微调策略为解决高维科学计算问题提供了一种强大且通用的解决方案。

Abstract: We introduce Tadpole, a novel foundation model for three-dimensional partial differential equations (PDEs) that addresses key challenges in transferability, scalability to high dimensionality, and multi-functionality. Tadpole is pre-trained as an autoencoder on synthetic 3D PDE data generated by an efficient online data-generation framework. This enables large-scale, diverse training without storage or I/O overhead, demonstrated by scaling to an equivalent of hundreds of terabytes of training data. By autoencoding single-channel spatial crops, Tadpole learns rich and transferable representations across heterogeneous physical systems with varying numbers of state variables and spatial resolutions. Although pre-trained solely as an autoencoder, Tadpole can be efficiently applied for multiple downstream tasks beyond reconstruction, including dynamics learning and generative modeling. For dynamics learning, we propose a novel parameter-efficient fine-tuning strategy that integrates low-rank adaptation, latent-space transformations, and reintroduced skip connections, achieving accurate temporal modeling with a minimal number of trainable parameters. Tadpole demonstrates strong fine-tuning performance across various downstream tasks, highlighting its versatility and effectiveness as a foundation model for 3D PDE learning. Source code and pre-trained weights of Tadpole are available at https://github.com/tum-pbs/tadpole

</details>


### [56] [Universal Approximation of Nonlinear Operators and Their Derivatives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15285)
*Filippo de Feo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次提出了针对非线性算子及其高阶导数的通用逼近定理（UAT），利用编码器-解码器架构实现了无限维空间下的高精度算子逼近，为解决PDE、逆问题及最优控制中的高阶计算难题奠定了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 算子学习（OL）中关于非线性算子及其导数的通用逼近理论（UAT）尚属空白，现有经典结论难以直接推广至无限维的算子学习框架，限制了其在高阶精度任务及复杂偏微分方程（PDE）求解中的应用。

Method: 利用编码器-解码器架构（如DeepONets、Deep-H-ONets等）作为参数化手段，结合Bastiani导数定义（比Fréchet导数更弱且更灵活）、加权Sobolev空间构造以及Banach空间的逼近性质，在紧集上证明了算子及其导数的通用逼近能力。

Result: 证明了在Banach空间之间，非线性k阶可微算子及其导数在紧集和加权Sobolev范数意义下的通用逼近定理；指出标准算子范数拓扑在导数逼近中失效的问题，并给出了新的数学解决方案。

Conclusion: 本文通过数学证明确立了非线性算子及其各阶导数的通用逼近定理（UAT），填补了算子学习（OL）领域在理论基础上的重要空白，并为高阶算子学习在控制理论、PDE求解及逆问题中的应用提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Derivative-Informed Operator Learning (DIOL), i.e. learning a (nonlinear) operator and its derivatives, is an open research frontier at the foundations of the influential field of Operator Learning (OL). In particular, Universal Approximation Theorems (UATs) of nonlinear operators and their derivatives are foundational open questions and delicate problems in nonlinear functional analysis. In this manuscript, we prove the first UATs of non-linear $k$-times differentiable operators between Banach spaces and their derivatives, uniformly on compact sets and in weighted Sobolev norms for general finite input measures, via OL architectures. Our results are the first complete generalizations of the corresponding influential classical results in [Hornik, 1991] to infinite-dimensional settings and OL.
  We discuss several open areas where DIOL and our UATs find applications: high-order accuracy in OL, fast constrained optimization in Banach spaces (e.g. optimal control of PDEs, inverse problems) and numerical methods for infinite-dimensional PDEs (e.g. HJB PDEs on Banach spaces from optimal control of PDEs, SPDEs, path-dependent systems, partially observed systems, mean-field control).
  We parameterize nonlinear operators via Encoder-Decoder Architectures, renowned classes in OL due to their generality, including classical architectures, such as DeepONets, Deep-H-ONets, PCA-Nets. Our results are based on four key features that allow us to prove UATs in full generality: (i) Approximation Properties of Banach spaces. (ii) $k$-times continuous differentiability in the sense of Bastiani (weaker than $k$-times continuous Fréchet differentiability). (iii) Natural compact-open topologies for UA; indeed, we show that UA in standard compact-open topologies induced by operator norms is violated even for Fréchet derivatives. (iv) Construction of novel weighted Sobolev spaces for the UA.

### [57] [GQA-μP: The maximal parameterization update for grouped query attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15290)
*Kyle R. Chickering,Huijuan Wang,Mengxi Wu,Alexander Moreno,Muhao Chen,Xuezhe Ma,Daria Soboleva,Joel Hestness,Zhengzhong Liu,Eric Xing*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的最大更新参数化（μP）虽然能实现超参数的跨架构迁移，但针对新架构（如GQA）的推导过程复杂且困难，且其理论假设在特定条件下存在局限性。本文旨在简化推导过程并扩展其适用范围至非满秩权重架构。

Method: 1. 将权重的谱范数条件从启发式方法提升为特征学习的定义；2. 基于谱特征学习视角，推导出了无需依赖“惰性学习”（lazy-learning）假设的Complete-P深度和权重衰减缩放比例；3. 引入改进的谱范数，解决了权重矩阵非满秩时的缩放失效问题，成功推导了GQA架构下的μP缩放比例。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Complete-P参数化方法有效地解决了非满秩权重矩阵下的超参数迁移问题，使得在GQA等现代架构中进行超参数迁移成为可能，进一步降低了大模型调优的算力成本。

Abstract: Hyperparameter transfer across model architectures dramatically reduces the amount of compute necessary for tuning large language models (LLMs). The maximal update parameterization (μP) ensures transfer through principled mathematical analysis but can be challenging to derive for new model architectures. Building on the spectral feature-learning view of Yang et al. (2023a), we make two advances. First, we promote spectral norm conditions on the weights from a heuristic to the definition of feature learning, and as a consequence arrive at the Complete-P depth and weight-decay scalings without recourse to lazy-learning. Second, we consider a modified spectral norm that preserves the valid scaling law of network weights when weight matrices are not full rank. This enables (to our knowledge, the first) derivation of μP scalings for grouped-query attention (GQA). We demonstrate the efficacy of our theoretical derivations by showing learning rate transfer across the GQA repetition hyperparameter as well as experiments regarding transfer over weight decay.

### [58] [GESD: Beyond Outcome-Oriented Fairness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15295)
*Gideon Popoola,John Sheppard*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的评估指标GESD，用于衡量机器学习模型对不同群体解释的稳定性差异，并开发了FEU框架，通过多目标优化在提升模型效用、结果公平性的同时，实现了更公正、更具解释性的决策过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的公平性指标（如统计平价、机会均等）主要关注模型输出结果的偏差，而忽视了产生决策的程序和解释本身可能存在的偏见。研究者旨在填补这一空白，提出一种从“过程导向”出发的解释性公平度量方法。

Method: 1. 提出了“群体级解释稳定性差异”（GESD）指标，用于衡量模型在不同受保护群体间解释的稳定性、鲁棒性和敏感性差异；2. 开发了FEU（Fairness-Explainability-Utility）多目标优化框架，通过联合优化效用、结果公平性和解释公平性来缓解偏见。该方法具有模型无关（model-agnostic）和解释器无关（explainer-agnostic）的特点。

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) algorithms are increasingly deployed in high-stakes decision-making domains such as loan approvals, hiring, and recidivism predictions. While existing fairness metrics (e.g., statistical parity, equal opportunity) effectively quantify outcome-oriented disparities, they offer limited insight into the procedure or explanation behind biased decisions. To address this gap, we propose Group-level Explanation Stability Disparity (GESD), a \textit{procedural-oriented} fairness metric that measures disparities in the stability, robustness, and sensitivity of model explanations across different subgroups in a protected category. %GESD is explainer-agnostic, model-agnostic, and extends the scope of fairness analyses to the level of explainability. We further integrate GESD into a multi-objective optimization framework that jointly optimizes for utility, outcome-based fairness, and explanation-based fairness called FEU (Fairness--Explainability--Utility). Empirical results on multiple benchmark datasets show that GESD effectively captures group-wise discrepancies in explanation quality, and that FEU improves both utility and fairness over state-of-the-art methods. By bridging outcome-based and explanation-based fairness, GESD offers a comprehensive tool for diagnosing and mitigating bias in predictive modeling. Our code and datasets are available on GitHub {\hyperlink{https://github.com/horlahsunbo/GESD}{https://github.com/horlahsunbo/GESD}}

### [59] [Beyond Bounded Variance: Variance-Reduced Normalized Methods for Nonconvex Optimization under Blum-Gladyshev Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15314)
*Antesh Upadhyay,Arda Fazla,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次在非凸优化中，针对方差随距离增长的BG-0噪声模型，证明了归一化动量算法及归一化STORM算法的收敛性，并给出了匹配下界的复杂度分析，无需依赖有界域等强假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非凸随机优化研究通常假设随机梯度的方差是有界的。然而，在许多实际应用中，方差往往随参数与最优解距离的增加而增大（即BG-0噪声模型）。现有的分析方法通常依赖于有界域或增加批次大小，这限制了算法的实际应用。因此，作者旨在无需这些限制性假设的前提下，探索在BG-0噪声模型下实现高效收敛的算法及相应的理论复杂度。

Method: 本文主要研究了两种算法：1) 归一化随机梯度下降及其动量变体；2) 方差减少的归一化STORM方法。通过分析目标函数在标准平滑性（Standard Smoothness）和对称广义平滑性（Symmetric Generalized Smoothness）下的表现，结合BG-0噪声模型（方差随距离平方增长），通过理论推导得出了对应的预言机复杂度（Oracle Complexity）。

Result: 在BG-0噪声模型下：1) 归一化随机梯度动量法在标准平滑性和α-对称广义平滑性下均达到O(ε⁻⁶)复杂度；2) 方差减少的归一化STORM方法在均方平滑性和尖锐初始化条件下，达到了极小极大最优的O(ε⁻⁴)复杂度；3) 在广义平滑性下，STORM方法的复杂度为O(ε⁻⁽⁴⁺α⁾)；4) 当噪声中的距离增长参数趋于零时，结果可恢复至标准有界方差下的收敛速率。

Conclusion: 本文为非凸随机优化在Blum-Gladyshev (BG-0) 噪声模型下的收敛性提供了首个理论保障，无需假设有界域、增加批次大小或显式锚定。研究结果表明，归一化方法在处理此类非一致有界方差问题时非常鲁棒，且Generalized smoothness在特定归一化动力学中具有速率中性（rate-neutral）的特性。

Abstract: We study nonconvex stochastic optimization under the Blum-Gladyshev ($\mathsf{BG}$-0) noise model, where the stochastic gradient variance grows quadratically with the distance from the initialization. We consider this problem under both standard smoothness and the symmetric generalized-smoothness framework, which captures objectives whose local curvature can scale with the gradient norm. We prove that normalized stochastic gradient descent with momentum, using only one stochastic gradient per iteration, converges under $\mathsf{BG}$-0 noise with oracle complexity $O(\varepsilon^{-6})$. This rate holds both for standard smoothness and for $α$-symmetric generalized smoothness, showing that generalized smoothness is rate-neutral for normalized momentum in this setting. We then study a variance-reduced normalized STORM method. Under mean-square smoothness and sharp initialization, the method achieves the minimax optimal $O(\varepsilon^{-4})$ complexity, matching the lower bound. Under expected $α$-symmetric generalized smoothness, the STORM recursion couples gradient-dependent smoothness with distance-dependent noise, leading to complexity $O(\varepsilon^{-(4+α)})$ for $α\in(0,1)$ and $O(\varepsilon^{-5})$ for $α=1$. When the distance-growth parameter in the noise model vanishes, our guarantees recover the standard bounded-variance rates: $O(\varepsilon^{-4})$ for momentum, $O(\varepsilon^{-3})$ for variance reduction, and $O(\varepsilon^{-2})$ in the deterministic case. To our knowledge, these are the first convergence guarantees for normalized methods in non-convex stochastic optimization under $\mathsf{BG}$-0 noise without bounded domains, increasing batch sizes, or explicit anchoring, covering both standard and generalized smoothness regimes.

</details>


### [60] [Bounded-Rationality, Hedging, and Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15340)
*Pedro A. Ortega*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过将学习器的泛化能力重新定义为一种在信息几何框架下的“对冲”行为，提供了一种仅通过观察黑盒学习器对损失扰动的响应，即可评估其泛化性能并获得泛化证书的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的泛化理论大多关注于模型的拟合能力，往往忽视了学习器本身如何权衡训练数据的依赖性与输出的鲁棒性。本文旨在通过信息论视角，将泛化能力重新定义为学习器的一种“对冲”（hedging）属性，从而建立一个更通用的分析框架来量化学习器对训练样本的响应敏感度。

Method: 本文将学习过程建模为一个受限理性的决策问题，利用诱导信道（induced channel）来描述样本到输出的映射。通过引入f-散度正则化器，在信息几何框架下推导出训练损失与样本依赖性之间的上下界权衡曲线，并提出通过观察学习器对缩放损失及局部扰动的响应，来反推其对冲特性与泛化性能的方法。

Result: 研究证明，泛化误差可以被分解为经验损失与由特定训练样本诱导的失真之和。文章给出了泛化性能的上下界曲线，并证明了当该“对冲”特性覆盖了由样本带来的失真时，即构成了一个实证的泛化保证。该方法适用于黑盒模型，且在KL散度正则化下与香农互信息具有数学上的对应关系。

Conclusion: 本文通过将泛化问题转化为学习器响应规律的“对冲”特性，不仅从理论上揭示了泛化误差与样本依赖性之间的权衡关系，还为评估机器学习模型的泛化能力提供了一种可测试的实证框架，即通过黑盒观测即可获得泛化证书。

Abstract: A learner does not only fit data; it also determines how strongly the training sample may shape its output and how much distortion it can hedge. We study this relation as a bounded-rational decision problem whose primitive object is the induced channel from samples to outputs. The learner's response law determines which changes in this channel are cheap or costly, and therefore induces both a lower tradeoff curve between training loss and sample dependence and a matched upper certificate curve. When the response law is represented by an $f$-divergence regularizer, these curves live in the regularizer's native information geometry, with KL as the special case corresponding to Shannon mutual information. We show how the hedge and the two curves can be recovered from black-box behavior by observing responses to scaled losses and local loss perturbations. In learning, population loss is empirical loss plus the distortion induced by the particular training sample. The recovered hedge gives a practical certificate when it covers that distortion. Thus generalization is treated as a testable hedging property of the learner's own response law.

### [61] [LEAP: Trajectory-Level Evaluation of LLMs in Iterative Scientific Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15341)
*Marilyn Zhang,Tianfeng Chen,Fabián Barzuna,Ankita Rathod,Mark E. Whiting*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 LEAPBench 基准框架，指出评估 LLM 在科学设计中的表现应关注学习轨迹而非仅最终结果。研究发现 LLM 在学习效率上未胜过经典的贝叶斯优化，并揭示了领域引导提示词在科学发现任务中可能存在的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的科学设计基准测试仅关注固定时间点的最终结果，无法衡量学习效率。而在自动化实验室中，减少迭代次数直接等同于成本和时间的节省。因此，研究旨在解决如何科学衡量 LLM 在迭代科学设计中的学习轨迹效率这一问题。

Method: 研究团队提出了 LEAPBench 基准测试框架，包含 55 个任务。该方法采用“最佳累计收益曲线”（best-so-far AUC）作为轨迹度量指标，将其与经典的贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization）进行对比，并利用已发表的文献进行审计验证。同时，利用该轨迹度量作为离线强化学习的奖励函数来指导模型训练。

Result: 1. 切换至轨迹评估后，53% 任务的最佳模型选择发生改变。2. LLM 在效率上并未超过经典贝叶斯优化基线。3. 在 16 项生物学任务中，领域感知的提示词（domain-aware prompting）的表现反而不如领域不可知提示词（domain-agnostic prompting）。4. 使用轨迹度量作为奖励进行离线强化学习，在 21 项任务中的 14 项上提升了性能。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，在评估自主实验室中的大语言模型（LLM）时，传统的最终结果评估方法忽略了关键的学习轨迹效率。通过 LEAPBench，研究发现 LLM 在迭代科学设计中并未超越经典的贝叶斯优化基线。此外，研究还揭示了领域知识引导的提示词（domain-aware prompting）在特定科学任务中反而可能对性能产生负面影响，强调了针对学习轨迹进行优化评估与训练的重要性。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly deployed in autonomous laboratories, under the assumption that their domain priors and reasoning over iterative feedback let them converge on good designs in fewer iterations than feedback-only baselines. Current iterative scientific design benchmarks, however, score only outcome snapshots at fixed horizons. This leaves the learning trajectory unmeasured, even though the trajectory is what captures learning efficiency, where each iteration saved is a real saving in cost and time. Motivated by this, we examine three evaluation choices that change the conclusions one draws about LLM learning efficiency in iterative scientific design: what to measure, what baseline to compare against, and what to ground against. We introduce LEAPBench, Learning Efficiency in Adaptive Processes, a 55-task framework that pairs a best-so-far area under the curve (AUC) trajectory metric with a classical Bayesian-optimization reference and an audit grounded in published literature. Applied to eight contemporary LLMs, switching from final-outcome to trajectory scoring changes the best-model decision on 53% of tasks at matched horizons, and exposes efficiency gains overlooked by outcome-based scoring. LLMs do not outperform a classical Bayesian baseline. On 16 biology tasks where the oracle's reward signal is aligned with configurations from the published-best design, domain-aware prompting leads to LLM choices that match the published-best's approximately 10 percentage points less often than domain-agnostic prompting at iteration 30. The pattern is sharpest on 6 tasks where the literature-typical and published-best configurations diverge, and domain-agnostic prompting matches the published-best more often on all 6. The trajectory metric also doubles as a tractable training target. Offline reinforcement learning with the metric as a reward improves performance on 14 of 21 held-out tasks.

</details>


### [62] [PACER: Acyclic Causal Discovery from Large-Scale Interventional Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15353)
*Ramon Viñas Torné,Sílvia Fàbregas Salazar,Soyon Park,Ivo Alexander Ban,Artyom Gadetsky,Nikita Doikov,Maria Brbić*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PACER 是一种新型因果发现框架，通过直接在变量排列和边概率上进行参数化，在保证无环性的前提下实现了对大规模观测与干预数据的高效因果结构学习，克服了现有方法在大规模场景下的扩展性瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对当前高维因果发现领域中，现有基于软无环约束的方法存在易产生循环图、数值不稳定以及难以在大规模数据上扩展等问题，旨在通过构造性的方法确保结构的无环性，实现高效且可扩展的因果结构学习。

Method: PACER（基于扰动的非循环因果边恢复）通过联合建模变量排列（permutations）和边概率（edge probabilities）来对DAG空间进行参数化。该方法直接在有效因果结构上进行优化，无需软约束惩罚项；支持观测与干预数据的统一似然估计，并在线性高斯机制下推导出了封闭形式的梯度计算，从而显著提升了计算效率。

Result: PACER 在蛋白质信号转导和大规模基因扰动基准测试中表现优异，性能达到或超越了现有顶尖方法。该框架能够扩展至数千个变量的规模，且在计算速度上比传统的基于惩罚项的可微优化方法快了两个数量级。

Conclusion: PACER 通过构建一种不仅能保证无环性，而且能处理大规模干预数据的因果发现框架，证明了在保留因果结构约束的前提下，实现高效、精确的因果结构学习是完全可行的。该方法为处理高维观测与干预数据提供了一种具有可扩展性的新路径。

Abstract: Inferring the structure of directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) from data is a central challenge in causal discovery, particularly in modern high-dimensional settings where large-scale interventional data are increasingly available. While interventional data can improve identifiability, existing methods remain limited by soft acyclicity constraints, leading to optimization over invalid cyclic graphs, numerical instability, and reduced scalability. We introduce PACER (Perturbation-driven Acyclic Causal Edge Recovery), a scalable framework for causal discovery that guarantees acyclicity by construction. PACER parameterizes a distribution over DAGs through a joint model of variable permutations and edge probabilities, enabling direct optimization over valid causal structures without surrogate penalties. The framework supports a unified likelihood-based treatment of observational and interventional data, flexible conditional density models, and the incorporation of structural prior knowledge. For linear-Gaussian mechanisms, we derive closed-form expressions for the expected interventional log-likelihood and its gradients, yielding substantial computational gains. Empirically, PACER matches or exceeds state-of-the-art methods on protein signaling and large-scale genetic perturbation benchmarks, while scaling efficiently to networks with thousands of variables and achieving up to two orders of magnitude speedups over penalty-based differentiable approaches. These results demonstrate that exact and scalable causal discovery from high-dimensional perturbation data is achievable through principled search space design.

</details>


### [63] [Controllable Molecular Generative Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15354)

Abstract: Despite the success of foundation models in language and vision, molecular graph generation still lacks a unified framework for heterogeneous design tasks with reliable controllability. We propose \textbf{Co}ntrollable \textbf{Mole}cular Generative Foundation Models (CoMole), built with a unified motif-aware graph diffusion pipeline. By learning a motif-aware graph space, CoMole transfers pretrained structural priors into controllable generation, where RL optimizes conditional reverse policies over chemically meaningful decisions. We theoretically characterize the bottleneck of atom-level RL and justify motif-aware policy optimization. ### [64] [Is One Score Enough? Rethinking the Evaluation of Sequentially Evolving LLM Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15384)
*Songwei Dong,Zihan Chen,Chengshuai Shi,Peng Wang,Jundong Li,Cong Shen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 SeqMem-Eval 评估框架，旨在通过在线效用、泛化性、后向迁移和遗忘等细粒度指标，揭示大模型在连续任务中记忆机制的深层表现及潜在的失效模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了 SeqMem-Eval 诊断评估框架。该框架借鉴持续学习理论，在测试时设置下对由提示词驱动（而非修改模型参数）的外部记忆进行评估。它引入了一系列细粒度指标，包括：在线效用（Online Utility）、保持集泛化能力（Hold-out Generalization）、后向迁移（Backward Transfer）以及遗忘程度（Forgetting）。

Result: 实验结果显示，高准确率并不等同于高质量的记忆。许多方法虽然在最终性能上表现出色，但内部却存在严重的遗忘或负迁移现象。此外，不同的记忆设计在适应性和稳定性之间存在显著的权衡（trade-offs），而这些细节在传统评估指标下是不可见的。

Conclusion: 该论文表明，仅凭最终准确率等综合指标无法全面评估大语言模型的记忆能力。SeqMem-Eval 框架通过揭示“稳定性与适应性”之间的权衡，以及遗忘和负迁移等关键失效模式，为评估持续学习场景下的记忆系统提供了更深入、更科学的视角。

Abstract: Memory plays a central role in enabling large language models (LLMs) to operate over sequential tasks by accumulating and reusing experience over time. However, existing evaluations of LLM memory mostly rely on aggregate metrics such as final hold-out accuracy or cumulative online performance, which can obscure critical failure modes such as forgetting and negative transfer. In this paper, we introduce SeqMem-Eval, a diagnostic evaluation framework for sequentially evolving LLM memory. Drawing inspiration from continual learning, it targets a test-time setting in which memory is external, prompt-mediated, and updated without modifying model parameters. Rather than focusing only on final performance, SeqMem-Eval evaluates how memory states evolve, generalize, consolidate experience, and retain useful information during sequential inference. Specifically, it measures online utility, hold-out generalization, backward transfer, and forgetting, providing a finer-grained view of memory quality. Through extensive experiments across diverse tasks and memory methods, we show that higher final or cumulative accuracy does not necessarily imply better memory quality: many methods exhibit strong performance gains while suffering from substantial forgetting or negative transfer. Moreover, different memory designs exhibit distinct trade-offs between adaptability and stability that remain invisible under standard evaluation metrics.

### [65] [Unified High-Probability Analysis of Stochastic Variance-Reduced Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15388)
*Zhankun Luo,Antesh Upadhyay,M. Berk Sahin,Sang Bin Moon,Anuran Makur,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的随机估计方法（如Momentum、SPIDER、STORM、PAGE等）分析多针对特定估计器且基于期望，缺乏统一的结构性理解，且难以应对高概率性能界和复杂约束条件下的挑战。

Method: 提出了一种包含“记忆保留、重置概率、迭代移动修正”三个组件的通用递归框架。利用一种新型的与维度无关的向量值Freedman不等式，对该框架进行了高概率误差分析。该方法适用于欧几里得空间及Banach空间中的镜像下降算法。

Result: 推导出了一个统一的高概率误差界，证明了该界在欧几里得和非欧几里得空间均有效。在无约束优化中实现了对置信水平的对数依赖；针对带期望约束的随机优化问题，首次将方差缩减技术引入，将预言机复杂度从 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-4})$ 提升至 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-3})$。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个统一的随机方差缩减估计框架，通过高概率分析揭示了优化算法的本质结构权衡。该研究不仅统一了现有算法，还为带期望约束的优化问题提供了更优的复杂度界，证明了方差缩减技术在更广泛设定下的有效性。

Abstract: Stochastic estimators are fundamental to large-scale optimization, where population quantities must be inferred from noisy oracle observations. Although influential methods such as momentum, SPIDER, STORM, and PAGE have been highly successful, their analyses are largely estimator-specific and expectation-based, obscuring the structural tradeoffs that determine reliability. In this paper, we develop a unified framework for stochastic variance-reduced estimation based on a recursion with three components: memory retention, reset probability, and a correction term for iterate movement. This framework recovers several classical estimators, motivates new second-order variants, and yields a bias-variance decomposition of estimation error. Our main result is a unified high-probability bound proved using a new dimension-free vector-valued Freedman inequality, valid for smooth normed spaces involving random sums of vector martingales. The result applies in both Euclidean and non-Euclidean settings, including the analysis of mirror-descent-based methods in Banach spaces. As applications, we obtain high-probability oracle complexities for unconstrained optimization with mirror descent, establishing the logarithmic dependence on the confidence level. We also derive the first $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-3})$ oracle-complexity bounds for stochastic optimization with expectation constraints, improving upon the existing $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-4})$ complexity by leveraging variance-reduced estimation for the first time in this setting.

### [66] [LPDS: Evaluating LLM Robustness Through Logic-Preserving Difficulty Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15393)
*Philipp Mondorf,Samuel J. Bell,Jesse Dodge,Dieuwke Hupkes*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了LPDS框架，通过系统搜索和量化逻辑保持变体来识别大语言模型的推理脆弱点，有效解决了现有随机评估方法对模型鲁棒性高估的问题，并证明了针对高难度变体微调可显著增强模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型（LLM）在面对逻辑不变但实体（如人名、数字等）改变的问题时，表现出不一致的稳健性。现有的评估方法多采用随机抽样，往往无法发现模型的真实漏洞，导致对模型鲁棒性的高估。因此，需要一套系统的方法来识别哪些变体最容易导致模型失效。

Method: 提出了“逻辑保持难度缩放”（LPDS）框架。该方法分为两部分：首先，量化问题变体的难度；其次，系统地搜索逻辑保持变体的空间，以找到并识别出那些能最大化问题难度并诱导模型出错的变体。此外，通过在这些高难度变体上进行微调，验证了其提升鲁棒性的有效性。

Result: 实验证明，随着问题难度的增加，模型的表现显著下降，推理链中的错误更加明显。相比随机抽样，LPDS能发现更难的问题变体，导致模型性能下降幅度最高可达5倍。此外，在困难变体上进行微调比在简单变体上训练能带来更一致的鲁棒性收益。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过LPDS框架识别出的高难度逻辑保持变体，不仅能更有效地揭示大语言模型的推理薄弱点，还能通过针对性微调显著提升模型的鲁棒性。该方法比传统的随机抽样评估更能准确衡量模型的真实稳健性。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed to perform tasks with minimal human oversight, it is crucial that these models operate robustly. In particular, a model that can solve a given problem should not fail simply because certain entities$\unicode{x2013}$such as names, numbers, or other contextual details$\unicode{x2013}$have changed while the underlying problem logic remains the same. Prior work suggests that current LLMs still struggle with this form of robustness: they often succeed on some variations of a problem but fail on others. However, existing evaluations often lack a systematic way to identify which logic-preserving variations are most likely to induce failure. Instead, they typically test a random subset of allowable variations, which can overstate robustness. To address this gap, we introduce logic-preserving difficulty scaling (LPDS), a framework that (i) quantifies the difficulty of a problem variation and (ii) systematically searches the space of allowable variations to find those that maximize difficulty and expose failures. We show that as difficulty increases, performance declines and errors in the models' reasoning chains become more pronounced. We further demonstrate that LPDS efficiently finds difficult problem variations for a model, resulting in performance drops up to 5 times larger compared to random sampling. Finally, we show that fine-tuning on more difficult variations leads to more consistent robustness gains than training on easier ones.

</details>


### [67] [Representation Without Reward: A JEPA Audit for LLM Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15394)
*Biswa Sengupta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过广泛的实验表明，在LLM微调中，向模型注入隐藏状态表征约束（JEPA策略）并不能可靠地提升下游任务的精度，隐藏状态的几何特性与最终任务表现之间存在微弱且不稳定的耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）的学习范式（即通过预测潜在表征而非直接输出观察结果）是否能显著提升大语言模型（LLM）在下游任务中的微调表现，并研究隐藏状态的几何特征与最终任务评估指标之间的相关性。

Method: 通过在Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct模型上进行自然语言转正则表达式的任务微调，测试了22种不同的辅助目标（包括轨迹形状正则化、分布约束、预测器/目标非对称性、Fisher度量雅可比残差以及解码器可见的JEPA目标），并对比了LoRA微调与全参数微调在统计学上的有效性。

Result: 实验结果呈现出“结构化的零假设”：虽然部分辅助目标在单一指标上表现出统计显著性，但在经过严格的Bonferroni多重假设校正后，没有任何一种方法能够稳定提升任务性能。即便是表现最好的解码器可见JEPA目标，在全参数微调的重复实验中也未能复现性能优势。

Conclusion: 在当前的预训练大语言模型微调范式下，隐藏状态的表征能力与最终的任务解码精度之间存在较弱的耦合关系。研究表明，仅优化隐藏状态的几何结构并不足以自动转化为显著的任务性能提升，这揭示了LLM微调中表征优化与任务目标之间的断层。

Abstract: Joint-embedding predictive architectures (JEPAs) propose that a model should learn more useful abstractions when trained to predict latent representations rather than observed outputs. For autoregressive language-model fine-tuning the principle entails a stricter requirement: the induced hidden-state geometry must reach the language-model head \emph{and} improve the decoded task metric. We test that requirement under a fixed Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct LoRA harness on natural-language-to-regex generation, comparing twenty-two training-time auxiliaries across trajectory-shape regularisation, distributional constraints, predictor/target asymmetry, Fisher-metric Jacobi residuals, and a decoder-visible JEPA objective constructed to lie in cross-entropy's positive cone. The empirical answer is a structured null: several auxiliaries clear single-cell paired $α= 0.10$ without correction (T3-Local at $Δ= +2.53$~pp, $p = 0.003$ being the strongest), but none survives Bonferroni or Holm--Bonferroni at the relevant family-wise threshold, even though many change curvature, anisotropy, variance, and gradient direction. Decoder-visible JEPA yields the first positive auxiliary--cross-entropy gradient cosine in the study, yet exact match remains inside seed noise; a full-fine-tuning replication of the same auxiliary at $n = 5$ seeds reproduces the null on both benchmarks (TURK: $Δ= +0.04$~pp, $p_{\text{paired}} = 0.96$; SYNTH: $Δ= +0.52$~pp, $p_{\text{paired}} = 0.28$), so the null is robust across LoRA and full fine-tuning for the decoder-visible construction. Hidden-state representation work and decoded-task accuracy are therefore weakly coupled in this regime; we accordingly reframe LLM-domain JEPA evaluation as a coupling problem, in which the operative question is under which metrics useful hidden geometry becomes decoder-visible task signal.

### [68] [Breakeven complexity: A new perspective on neural partial differential equation solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15399)
*Yijing Zhang,Nicholas Roberts,Tanya Marwah,Mikhail Khodak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决神经PDE求解器在评估中忽视训练成本的问题，本文提出了“盈亏平衡复杂度”评估框架，旨在衡量神经求解器在何种使用规模下优于传统数值方法，并发现其在处理高复杂度物理问题时具有更高的经济效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经偏微分方程（PDE）求解器评估大多仅关注精度，忽略了高昂的数据生成与训练成本。此外，传统数值求解器也可以通过降低精度来降低计算成本。因此，需要一个能够综合考虑训练、数据生成及推理成本的公平评价标准，以确定神经求解器在何时真正具备成本优势。

Method: 提出了基于“盈亏平衡复杂度”（breakeven complexity）的评估框架，旨在计算神经求解器相对于同精度传统求解器的累积成本平衡点；利用缩放定律（scaling laws）指导训练预算与数据生成的分配；并在包含复杂障碍物流动的基准测试集上对多种神经求解器进行了实证分析。

Result: 研究表明，当问题难度（如高维度、长序列、高雷诺数等）增加时，神经PDE求解器的成本优势更为显著。通过新的基准测试发现，神经求解器在达到特定的正向求解次数后，能够实现相对于传统求解器的“盈亏平衡”，且在复杂场景下表现出更强的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 本研究强调了在评估神经偏微分方程求解器时，必须超越单纯的精度指标，将训练与推理的端到端成本纳入考量。通过引入“盈亏平衡复杂度”指标，研究证明了神经求解器在处理高难度、高成本物理问题时更具竞争力，为未来神经求解器的开发与评估提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Neural surrogate solvers of partial differential equations (PDEs) promise dramatic speedups over numerical methods, especially in scenarios requiring many solves. However, current accuracy-based evaluations do not fully consider two central issues: (1) neural solvers incur substantial up-front costs for data generation, training, and tuning; and (2) classical solvers can also generate low-fidelity solutions at a sufficiently low simulation cost. To explicitly account for these realities and fully incorporate end-to-end costs, we propose an evaluation framework centered on breakeven complexity, a metric that counts the forward solves before a learned solver is cost-effective relative to an error-equivalent traditional solver. To evaluate this measure, we apply scaling laws to determine how much training budget to allocate to data generation and discuss how to achieve smooth error-matching in diverse settings. We evaluate the breakeven complexity of multiple neural PDE solvers on three PDEs on 2D periodic domains from APEBench and a novel benchmark of flows past multiple obstacles generated by the GPU-native PyFR code. Among other findings, our results suggest that neural PDE solvers become more effective as problems get harder in terms of cost, dimension, rollout, physics regime (e.g. higher Reynolds number), etc.

### [69] [$φ$-Balancing for Mixture-of-Experts Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15403)
*Lizhang Chen,Jonathan Li,Qi Wang,Runlong Liao,Shuozhe Li,Chen Liang,Ni Lao,Qiang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 $\phi$-balancing，一种旨在替代传统启发式方案的 MoE 模型负载均衡框架，利用凸对偶与在线算法实现了更高效、更稳定的专家负载分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 MoE 模型负载均衡方法多为启发式，且依赖于带有噪声的小批量（Mini-batch）统计信息，无法实现全局（总体级）的专家负载平衡，导致模型的可扩展性受限。

Method: 提出了一种基于凸优化（Convex Duality）的 $\phi$-balancing 框架。该方法通过最小化专家路由分布的严格凸、对称且可微的势函数（Potential Function）来实现总体级的负载均衡，并推导出了一种基于镜像下降（Mirror Descent）和指数移动平均（EMA）的简单在线路由调整算法。

Result: 在超大规模预训练和下游任务微调实验中，$\phi$-balancing 在专家利用率的稳定性与模型性能表现上，均显著优于传统的 Switch-style 及其他无损（loss-free）基准方法。

Conclusion: $\phi$-balancing 是一种更具理论严谨性的负载均衡方法，通过凸优化与镜像下降算法，有效解决了 MoE 模型中专家利用率不均的问题，并在大规模预训练与微调中表现出优于传统启发式方法的性能。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models rely on balanced expert utilization to fully realize their scalability. However, existing load-balancing methods are largely heuristic and operate on noisy mini-batch assignment statistics, introducing bias relative to population-level objectives. We propose $φ$-balancing, a principled framework that directly targets population-level expert balance by minimizing a strictly convex, symmetric, and differentiable potential of the expected routing distribution. Using convex duality, we derive an equivalent min-max formulation and obtain a simple online algorithm via mirror descent, yielding an efficient EMA-based routing adjustment with negligible overhead. Across large-scale pretraining and downstream fine-tuning, $φ$-balancing consistently outperforms prior Switch-style and loss-free baselines, demonstrating more stable and effective expert utilization.

### [70] [Transformer Scalability Crisis: The First Comprehensive Empirical Analysis of Performance Walls in Modern Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15413)
*Mahdi Naser Moghadasi,Faezeh Ghaderi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文通过对118个Transformer模型的大规模基准测试，揭示了模型在处理长序列时存在的严重可扩展性危机，发现超过一定长度后模型性能将急剧下滑，并量化了压缩模型与大型模型在参数效率上的巨大差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Transformer在NLP领域表现优异，但学术界对其可扩展性的局限性尚缺乏系统的实证分析。研究旨在揭示Transformer模型在实际部署过程中面临的性能瓶颈，打破现有的关于模型扩展性的假设。

Method: 该论文采用了大规模实证分析方法，对7种不同架构类别的118个Transformer模型进行了系统性基准测试。研究通过评估不同序列长度（128至2048 tokens）下的模型加载时间、内存消耗和计算效率（tokens/sec/M参数），量化分析了模型在不同规模下的性能表现。

Result: 研究发现：1) 模型处理序列的能力随长度显著下降，在512 tokens时成功率为88.1%，1024 tokens时降至44.9%，2048 tokens时则完全失效（0%）；2) 压缩模型在参数效率方面远优于大型生成式模型（649.2 tokens/sec/M 对比 12.5 tokens/sec/M）；3) 证实了O(n²)复杂度在实际应用中确实构成了难以逾越的性能墙。

Conclusion: 该研究通过实证揭示了Transformer模型在处理长序列时存在严重的“可扩展性危机”，即随着序列长度增加，模型的计算效率和成功处理率呈断崖式下跌。研究明确了理论上的O(n²)注意力复杂度在实际部署中会转化为具体的性能瓶颈，为生产环境下的模型选型提供了新的基准和决策依据。

Abstract: Despite the remarkable success of transformer architectures in natural language processing, their scalability limitations remain poorly understood through systematic empirical analysis. This paper presents the first comprehensive large-scale evaluation of 118 transformer models across seven distinct architectural categories, revealing fundamental performance walls that manifest as hard deployment constraints. Our systematic benchmarking methodology uncovers a critical scalability crisis: while 88.1% of models successfully process sequences up to 512 tokens, this drops dramatically to 44.9% at 1024 tokens, with complete failure (0%) at 2048 tokens. Through rigorous analysis of loading times, memory consumption, and computational efficiency across sequence lengths from 128 to 2048 tokens, we demonstrate that compressed models achieve superior parameter efficiency (649.2 tokens/sec/M parameters) compared to large generative models (12.5 tokens/sec/M). Our findings challenge prevailing scaling assumptions and provide the first quantitative evidence that the theoretical O(n2) attention complexity translates into measurable performance walls. This work establishes new benchmarking methodologies for transformer evaluation and provides critical insights for practical deployment decisions in production environments.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型与人类评价一致性保障框架依赖于置信度与人类分歧风险呈单调性的假设，但在实际应用中这一假设往往不成立，且缺乏对置信度估计器泛化行为的明确分析。

Method: 提出了一种基于模拟标注多样性和边缘（Margin）排序公式的置信度估计器学习方法。该方法不仅显式建模了模型区分人类共识与分歧的能力，还通过推导泛化界限来指导自适应训练过程，从而优化置信度与人类不一致风险之间的单调关系。

Result: 实验表明，该方法不仅改善了排序准确性，还增强了置信度与不一致风险之间的单调性，并在多个数据集和评测模型上实现了更高的一致性目标达成率。

Conclusion: 通过学习专门的置信度估计器并将其集成到假设检验框架中，可以有效解决大语言模型置信度与人类评价一致性之间的偏差，显著提高模型在达成预定一致性目标时的成功率。

Abstract: Jung et al. (2025) introduce a hypothesis testing framework for guaranteeing agreement between large language models (LLMs) and human judgments, relying on the assumption that the model's estimated confidence is monotonic with respect to human-disagreement risk. In practice, however, this assumption may be violated, and the generalization behavior of the confidence estimator is not explicitly analyzed. We mitigate these issues by learning a dedicated confidence estimator instead of relying on heuristic confidence signals. Our approach leverages simulated annotator diversity and a margin-based ranking formulation to explicitly model how confidently an LLM distinguishes between human-agreement and human-disagreement cases. We further derive generalization guarantees for this estimator, revealing a margin-dependent trade-off that informs the design of an adaptive estimator training procedure. When integrated into fixed-sequence testing, the learned confidence estimator yields improved ranking accuracy and empirically strengthens the monotonic relationship between confidence and disagreement risk, leading to higher success rates in satisfying target agreement levels across multiple datasets and judge models.

### [72] [Lagrangian Flow Matching: A Least-Action Framework for Principled Path Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15419)
*Shukai Du,Junzhe Zhang,Yiming Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于经典力学最小作用量原理的“拉格朗日流匹配”框架，通过优化广义拉格朗日量来学习概率路径，实现了对现有多种流匹配方法的统一与扩展，并支持更灵活的生成模型设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的流匹配方法（如基于直线路径的 rectified flow 或最优传输路径）仅限于简单的动力学形式，相当于经典力学中最简的“自由粒子直线运动”。为了超越这一局限，作者受经典力学中最小作用量原理的启发，试图构建一种更通用的物理框架，以产生更丰富、更具表现力的概率路径和速度场。

Method: 提出拉格朗日流匹配（Lagrangian Flow Matching），通过在连续性方程和给定端点约束下，最小化广义拉格朗日量的作用量来确定概率路径和速度场。该方法将动力学问题转化为等价的静态最优传输（OT）形式，并推导出无模拟（simulation-free）的训练目标。通过选择不同的拉格朗日量，可以诱导出包括直线运动、谐振子运动等在内的多种流形轨迹。

Result: 该研究成功推导出一系列涵盖现有方法（如最优传输流匹配和谐振子扩散路径）的统一训练目标。数值实验表明，使用更复杂的拉格朗日量可以显著改变学习到的生成动力学特征，同时在生成性能上保持了与现有先进条件流匹配模型相当的竞争力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的拉格朗日流匹配框架通过引入广义拉格朗日量，拓展了流匹配模型的建模能力。研究表明，通过优化作用量可以推导出多种概率路径，这不仅统一了现有的最优传输和扩散路径方法，还为设计更复杂的生成模型提供了物理学原理支持。实验证明该方法在学习动力学特性方面具有灵活性，且性能与现有条件流匹配模型相当。

Abstract: Flow matching trains a neural velocity field by regression against a target velocity associated with a prescribed probability path connecting a simple initial distribution to the data distribution. A central design choice is the path itself. Existing constructions, including rectified and optimal-transport-based paths, transport samples along straight lines between coupled endpoints and thus cover only a narrow class of dynamics. We observe that this corresponds to the simplest case of the least-action principle in classical mechanics, in which the kinetic Lagrangian yields free-particle straight-line trajectories. Building on this observation, we propose Lagrangian flow matching, a physics-based framework in which the probability path and velocity field are determined by minimizing the action of a general Lagrangian subject to the continuity equation and the prescribed endpoints. We show that this dynamic problem admits an equivalent static optimal transport (OT) formulation, yielding a family of simulation-free training objectives that recover OT-based flow matching as the kinetic special case and the trigonometric variance-preserving diffusion path as the harmonic-oscillator case. More general Lagrangians give rise to new probability paths and velocity fields, and numerical experiments show that they induce meaningful changes in the learned dynamics while remaining competitive with existing conditional flow matching models.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了一种基于频谱选择性的特征构造方法，即通过信号处理技术从原始EEG数据中提取主要脑波频段（如Alpha、Beta、Theta等）的信号强度，将其转化为高价值的频谱特征。该方法将这些特征输入到传统的机器学习模型中，并与SOTA深度学习模型（包括注意力机制模型）在多个公开的静息态和任务态EEG数据集上进行了对比验证。

Conclusion: 该研究指出，在神经退行性疾病的EEG分类任务中，基于频谱选择性的特征工程方法比复杂的深度学习模型（如注意力机制模型）更有效。研究表明，针对特定频段的特征提取能显著提高模型的可解释性和分类性能，且盲目引入注意力机制并不能克服信号噪声和类间高相似度带来的分类挑战。

Abstract: Electroencephalograph (EEG) timeseries signals are characterized by significant noise and coarse spatial resolution, which complicates the classification of neurodegenerative diseases. Even SOTA deep learning architectures struggle to distinguish between healthy controls and diseased subjects, or between different disease types, due to high intergroup similarity. In this paper, we show that a spectrally selective approach to feature construction enhances class separability. By isolating signal strengths within the primary brainwave bands, we transform high dimensional raw data into high value spectral features. Our results demonstrate that a) features derived from frequency and time frequency domain allow traditional machine learning models to match or exceed the performance of SOTA deep learning models, b) Attention mechanism is unable to distill the stable feature signatures that characterize healthy neural activity in both resting and task EEGs, and c) the limitations of attention based models in finding relevant spectral features appear to be fundamental in that providing frequency selective time domain input do not appreciably improve their performance. We validate our methodology across three open source resting EEG datasets and one task EEG dataset, providing robust empirical evidence for our claims.

### [74] [DrugSAGE:Self-evolving Agent Experience for Efficient State-of-the-Art Drug Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15461)
*Yikun Zhang,Xiwei Cheng,Tianyu Liu,Yuanqi Du,Wengong Jin*

Method: 提出了Self-evolving Agent Experience (SAE) 框架。该框架构建了一个跨任务记忆库，用于存储已验证的技能、关于有效策略的统计证据，以及常见错误及其修复方案的记录。智能体利用这些累积的经验，在处理新任务时通过直接迁移工作方案或减少搜索空间来降低计算成本。

Result: 在33个分子性质预测任务的单任务设置中排名第一。在跨任务评估中，利用16个较小任务积累的经验，在17个留存任务上取得了0.935的平均归一化分数，并在零测试时间搜索场景下，较基准智能体性能提升了10%-30%。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了跨任务记忆机制在药物发现领域模型开发中的显著优势，通过积累和复用经验，能够显著提升智能体构建高性能预测模型的效率和准确性，为实现更智能、更高效的药物研发自动化提供了有效范式。

Abstract: Building state-of-the-art (SOTA) predictive models for drug discovery requires expensive search over tools, architectures, and training strategies. Current LLM-based agents can find SOTA solutions through extensive trial and error, but they do not retain the experience accumulated along the way and therefore pay the full search cost on every new task. We propose \method (Self-evolving Agent Experience), a framework that accumulates and reuses experience across tasks to build SOTA drug discovery models efficiently. \method maintains a cross-task memory of verified skills, statistical evidence about effective strategies, and a record of recurring errors and their fixes. In some cases, \method transfers a working solution directly without test-time search. In 33 molecular property prediction tasks, \method ranks first among nine SOTA agents in a single-task setting. With memory accumulated from 16 smaller tasks, \method achieves an averaged normalized score of 0.935 on 17 held-out tasks in a cross-task evaluation setting and outperforms all baseline agents by 10-30\% in a zero-test-time search regime. In summary, our work shows the advantage of cross-task memory for efficient SOTA model development in drug discovery.

### [75] [GRLO: Towards Generalizable Reinforcement Learning in Open-Ended Environments from Zero](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15464)
*Shangjian Yin,Yu Fu,Yue Dong,Zhouxing Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GRLO 是一种高效的大模型后训练方法，通过极少量的开放式 RLHF 训练，即可激发模型在推理和代码任务上的强大泛化能力，大幅降低了高性能模型训练的算力和数据门槛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的推理导向后训练（RLVR）虽然有效，但极其消耗 GPU 算力和数据，导致门槛过高。研究旨在探究从少量交互中学习到的对话能力是否能隐式迁移至下游复杂任务，从而寻求一种更高效、通用的模型优化范式。

Method: 提出 GRLO 方法，通过在开放式环境中进行小规模（5K 提示）的 RLHF 训练，利用从基础交互中习得的对话能力，通过模型内部的表征迁移，实现对下游任务（推理、代码）的泛化提升，而非依赖特定领域的 verifier-backed 强化学习。

Result: 在 Qwen3-4B 模型上，GRLO 仅用 5K 提示和 22.7 GPU 小时，将多领域平均性能从 24.1 提升至 63.1。相较于传统的 RLVR 基线，数据需求减少了 46 倍，算力消耗减少了 68 倍，且表现足以媲美经过大规模训练的同类模型。

Conclusion: GRLO 证明了通过小规模、开放式环境下的 RLHF 训练获得的对话能力，能够显著迁移到数学推理和代码生成等下游任务中。这种方法提供了一种极具成本效益的通用模型训练方案，打破了对大规模领域内强化学习（RLVR）的依赖。

Abstract: Post-training has become a crucial step for unlocking the capabilities of large language models, with reinforcement learning (RL) emerging as a critical paradigm. Recent RL-based post-training has increasingly split into two paradigms: reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), which optimizes models using human preference signals in target domains, and reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR), which operates in verifier-backed environments. The latter has dominated recent reasoning-oriented post-training because it delivers stronger gains and higher efficiency on domain-specific tasks (e.g., reasoning). However, although in-domain RL training achieves promising performance, it still requires a substantial amount of GPU compute, which remains a major barrier to broad adoption. In this work, we study the generalization ability of RLHF learned from scratch from a small set of interactions in open-ended environments, and investigate whether the conversational abilities it explicitly acquires can implicitly transfer to downstream tasks such as mathematical reasoning and code generation, namely GRLO. Specifically, on Qwen3-4B-Base backbone, GRLO improves the average performance across all domains from 24.1 to 63.1 with only 5K prompts and 22.7 GPU hours, requiring about $46\times$ less data and $68\times$ less compute than a strong in-domain RLVR baseline. The resulting model is even competitive with Qwen's released post-trained models which required a much larger training cost. Notably, a subsequent in-domain RLVR stage brings only selective gains, mainly on harder competition-math benchmarks. We hope GRLO offers a simple and efficient recipe for building broadly capable post-trained models. Our code and data will be available at: \href{https://github.com/SJY8460/GRLO}{https://github.com/SJY8460/GRLO}.
