We introduce NormWear-2, a world model that encodes both multivariate physiological signals and clinical intervention variables into a shared latent space and models their joint temporal evolution as a dynamical system. Our approach combines inference from prior pre-trained knowledge (intuition) with instant non-parametric latent state transition adaptation (insight), enabling coherent forecasting across multiple temporal scales, conditioned on heterogeneous clinical interventions. During the pretraining phase, we find that chaos-theoretic balancing of dynamical regime diversity yields more robust representations, with a smaller balanced corpus outperforming one twice its size and capturing bifurcation regimes. ### [77] [Learning Normalized Energy Models for Linear Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15487)

Motivation: 现有的基于生成扩散模型的图像逆问题解决方法存在两个主要缺陷：一是先验概率密度以隐式形式存在，缺乏可解释性；二是依赖似然估计的近似方法，导致采样过程中引入了不可控的偏差。

Method: 提出了一种结合降噪训练与协方差正则化项的能量模型。该模型能够计算归一化的后验概率密度，并支持：1. 基于能量引导的实时自适应采样；2. 用于消除采样偏差的无偏Metropolis-Hastings校正；3. 通过贝叶斯法则进行退化算子的盲估计。

Result: 在ImageNet、CelebA和AFHQ等多个数据集及图像修复（inpainting）、去模糊（deblurring）等任务上进行了验证。结果显示，该方法在保持扩散模型高效采样能力的同时，性能优于或媲美现有的主流基准模型。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于能量的模型，通过显式概率建模克服了生成扩散模型在逆问题处理中的局限性。该方法不仅提升了图像重建质量，还通过引入自适应采样和无偏校正等机制，增强了模型在处理复杂线性逆问题时的灵活性和可靠性，为生成模型在图像恢复任务中的应用提供了更严谨的统计框架。

Abstract: Generative diffusion models can provide powerful prior probability models for inverse problems in imaging, but existing implementations suffer from two key limitations: $(i)$ the prior density is represented implicitly, and $(ii)$ they rely on likelihood approximations that introduce sampling biases. We address these challenges by introducing a new energy-based model trained for denoising with a covariance-based regularization term that enforces consistency across different measurement conditions. The trained model can compute normalized posterior densities for diverse linear inverse problems, without additional retraining or fine tuning. In addition to preserving the sampling capabilities of diffusion models, this enables previously unavailable capabilities: energy-guided adaptive sampling that adjusts schedules on-the-fly, unbiased Metropolis-Hastings correction steps, and blind estimation of the degradation operator via Bayes rule. We validate the method on multiple datasets (ImageNet, CelebA, AFHQ) and tasks (inpainting, deblurring), demonstrating competitive or superior performance to established baselines.

</details>


### [78] [Ghosted Layers: Unconstrained Activation Alignment for Recovering Layer-Pruned LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15491)
*Vincent-Daniel Yun,Junhyuk Jo,Sai Praneeth Karimireddy,Sunwoo Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型层剪枝导致的性能退化问题，本文提出“Ghosted Layers”技术，通过计算最优线性算子对齐被剪枝后的激活分布，无需重新训练即可显著提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）的层剪枝会导致剩余层的输入隐藏状态分布发生偏移，与该层预训练时的分布不匹配，从而引发严重的性能下降。现有的解决方法通常局限于有限的算子空间，难以实现最优对齐。

Method: 本文提出了一种无需训练的恢复模块“Ghosted Layers”。该方法将层剪枝后的激活对齐问题建模为线性算子优化问题，利用少量校准数据集，通过闭式解（Closed-form solution）计算出一个最优线性算子，用于重建被剪除层导致的激活分布差异，从而修正后续层的输入偏差。

Result: 在多个大模型主干和剪枝策略上的实验表明，该方法在保持层剪枝推理效率优势的同时，在准确率和困惑度（Perplexity）指标上均优于现有的无需训练的基准方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的“Ghosted Layers”方法通过数学推导找到了层剪枝中激活对齐问题的闭式最优解，在无需额外训练的情况下，有效弥补了层剪枝带来的性能损失，是一种高效且具有理论支撑的LLM压缩辅助技术。

Abstract: Layer pruning removes entire Transformer decoder blocks from large language models, but introduces a mismatch between the hidden state received by the next surviving layer and the distribution it was trained to process, leading to significant performance degradation. We propose Ghosted Layers, a training-free recovery module that addresses this issue by solving a boundary activation alignment problem. Our method derives a closed-form optimal linear operator from a small calibration set to reconstruct the activation discrepancy introduced by the pruned layers. We show that this solution corresponds to the unconstrained optimum of the alignment objective, whereas existing methods are restricted to constrained solutions over limited operator subspaces. Experiments across multiple LLM backbones and pruning strategies demonstrate that our method consistently improves accuracy and perplexity over prior training-free baselines, while preserving the efficiency gains of layer pruning.

### [79] [Learning with Conflicts of Interest](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15504)
*Nischal Aryal,Arash Termehchy,Ali Vakilian,Marianne Winslett*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于博弈论的框架，通过在用户端引入防御机制，解决机器学习系统与用户之间因利益冲突导致的偏见与操纵问题，确保用户能安全地利用AI系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器学习系统常因所有者利益与用户利益不一致而产生偏见或操纵性内容，且系统所有者缺乏通过自身协议缓解这些偏差的动力。因此，需要一种从用户角度出发的框架，在保护用户免受不利信息影响的同时，保留系统带来的技术便利。

Method: 采用博弈论方法建模机器学习系统（信息提供者）与用户之间的利益冲突，并设计了可扩展的算法，通过优化决策过程，在最大化有用信息获取的同时，最小化有害偏见和操纵行为的影响，并提供了理论保证。

Result: 成功构建了一个通用的博弈论交互模型，并验证了所提出的算法在处理信息操纵问题上的有效性，在具备理论保障的前提下，显著提升了用户在面对机器学习系统时的决策质量。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种博弈论框架，能够在不对系统所有者施加外部强制约束的前提下，通过用户侧的防御机制有效减轻机器学习系统带来的偏差和操纵风险，从而在系统效率与用户利益保护之间达成平衡。

Abstract: Financial, social, and political factors often prevent the interests of the owners of ML systems and services and their users from being perfectly aligned. ML systems often produce biased information that can influence users to make decisions that are not in their best interest. Current solution approaches require ML systems to implement protocols to mitigate their biases. However, ML system owners usually do not have any incentive to implement these protocols and often argue that it limits their freedom of expression or business. We believe that a successful solution to this problem must recognize the conflict of interest between the ML systems and their users, and use this information to protect users against information that adversely influences their decisions while allowing users to safely benefit from these systems. To this end, we propose a game-theoretic framework that models the interaction between ML systems and users with conflicts of interest. We present scalable algorithms with theoretical guarantees that maximize the amount of desired information and actions and minimize the amount of biased and manipulative actions in interaction with ML systems.

### [80] [STS: Efficient Sparse Attention with Speculative Token Sparsity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15508)
*Ceyu Xu,Jiangnan Yu,Yongji Wu,Yuan Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: STS 是一种无需重训练的稀疏注意力加速方案，通过在推测解码过程中复用草稿模型的注意力分数来动态剪枝目标模型的计算，在处理长序列任务时显著提升了推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型推理中的注意力机制具有二次时间复杂度，这在处理超长上下文（multi-million tokens）的智能体应用时导致了严重的内存和计算瓶颈。

Method: 提出了一种名为 STS 的稀疏注意力机制，它集成于推测解码（Speculative Decoding）框架中。通过利用草稿模型（draft model）的注意力分数动态构建针对特定 Token 和 Attention Head 的稀疏掩码（sparsity mask），从而在大型目标模型中裁剪冗余的注意力计算。

Result: 在 NarrativeQA 基准测试中，STS 实现了 2.67 倍的推理加速，在保持约 90% 稀疏度的同时，精度损失几乎可以忽略不计，并在稀疏性与精度的权衡方面优于现有技术。

Conclusion: STS 证明了在不进行模型重训练的情况下，利用小型草稿模型引导大型目标模型的稀疏注意力计算是一种高效的推理加速策略，为超长序列推理提供了新的性能基准。

Abstract: The quadratic complexity of attention imposes severe memory and computational bottlenecks on Large Language Model (LLM) inference. This challenge is particularly acute for emerging agentic applications that require processing multi-million token sequences. We propose STS, a sparse attention mechanism that requires no model retraining. STS leverages the key insight that tokens identified as important by a smaller draft model are highly predictive of important tokens for a larger target model. By integrating into speculative decoding frameworks, STS repurposes the draft model's attention scores to dynamically construct a token-and-head-wise sparsity mask. This mask effectively prunes the expensive attention computation in the target LLM. Our evaluation shows that STS achieves a 2.67x speedup operating at approximately 90% sparsity on representative benchmark NarrativeQA, maintaining negligible accuracy degradation compared to dense attention. STS establishes a new state-of-the-art on the sparsity-accuracy trade-off, outperforming prior techniques by enabling higher sparsity levels for a given accuracy budget.

### [81] [parallelcbf: A composable safety-filter and auditability framework for tensor-parallel reinforcement learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15509)
*Yijun Lu,Zilei Yang,Yuyin Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ParallelCBF 是首个统一了并行无人机仿真、CBF 安全过滤、BC-to-RL 训练管线及自动化操作审计功能的开源框架，旨在解决机器人研究中安全约束训练缺乏统一基准和审计标准的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管现有工具分别提供了大规模并行模拟、约束强化学习基准和 CBF 合成工具，但缺乏一个统一的框架来支持端到端的安全约束训练。此外，现有的实验缺乏系统化的可审计性，容易导致训练过程中的隐蔽性失效或结果不可复现。

Method: 该框架通过四层可组合 API 集成了以下核心功能：(1) 基于张量并行的无人机环境；(2) 硬门控制屏障函数 (CBF) 安全过滤器；(3) 分片的行为克隆到强化学习 (BC-to-RL) 训练流程；(4) 一流的操作可审计性工具，包括预注册、看门狗注册表、故障取证及数据集审计。此外，该框架还提供了双屏障 CBF 的参考实现及属性驱动的安全不变性测试。

Result: ParallelCBF 实现了 1.67 秒完成 39 项属性驱动的安全不变性测试；支持了 31,415 个片段的行为克隆数据集采集；并成功展示了框架的审计层如何通过自动监测预注册的收敛标准，在训练阶段中止不合格任务，有效防止了退化模型权重的传播。

Conclusion: ParallelCBF 填补了机器人研究中缺乏端到端安全约束训练框架的空白。作者强调，通过内置的审计层（auditability layer）实现可复现性和安全性，是未来经验机器人研究中必不可少的架构特性。

Abstract: While Isaac Lab provides massive parallel UAV simulation, OmniSafe and safe-control-gym provide constrained-RL benchmarks, and CBFKit provides control-barrier-function synthesis tooling, no existing framework unifies these capabilities for end-to-end safety-constrained training. ParallelCBF is the first framework to unify (i)~tensor-parallel UAV environments, (ii)~hard-gate CBF safety filters, (iii)~sharded BC-to-RL pipelines, and (iv)~first-class operational auditability -- pre-registration, watchdog registries, failure forensics, and dataset audits as composable APIs rather than user-implemented scripts. We release ParallelCBF v0.1.0 under Apache~2.0 with a four-layer composable API, a CPU PyTorch reference implementation of a dual-barrier (squared / linear-predictive) CBF, property-based safety invariance tests across vectorized batch sizes that complete in 1.67~s for the full 39-test suite, and a 31{,}415-episode behavior-cloning collection campaign whose curriculum mix, per-bucket yields, and dataset SHA-256 are auditable through the framework's own \texttt{ops} primitives. We report a representative end-to-end pipeline execution in which the framework's auditability layer halted a downstream training stage that did not meet pre-registered convergence criteria, preventing silent propagation of a degraded checkpoint -- an architectural property we argue is necessary, not merely useful, for reproducible empirical robotics research. The framework is installable via \texttt{pip install parallelcbf}; source and release artifacts are available at https://github.com/xiaoyang-123-cell/ParallelCBF.

</details>


### [82] [On the Fragility of Data Attribution When Learning Is Distributed](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15520)
*Xian Gao,Bo Hui,Min-Te Sun,Wei-Shinn Ku*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了机器学习数据归因方法存在安全漏洞，证明了恶意参与者可以通过注入精心构造的合成数据来操纵归因结果，从而虚增自身贡献，且不会影响模型性能或触发防御报警。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器学习数据归因方法通常假设归因值能够忠实地反映参与者的贡献，但这一假设在恶意参与者面前可能失效。研究动机旨在揭示这种假设的脆弱性，证明单一参与者可以在不降低模型性能的前提下，通过操纵手段显著夸大自己的贡献度（归因值）。

Method: 研究者提出了一种“归因优先攻击（Attribution-first attack）”。该方法利用潜在优化（Latent optimization）技术，在分布式训练过程中注入微小的合成数据批次；这些数据不仅能保持模型的全局效用（精度），还能利用非独立同分布（Non-IID）的标签覆盖特性及评估器的敏感性，从而在不被几何防御手段察觉的情况下提升自身的归因权重。

Result: 实验结果表明，该攻击在多种数据集、模型架构及边缘效用评估器上均表现稳健。攻击者不仅成功增加了自身的归因占比，还能够重塑良性参与者之间的相对归因结构，且整个过程不会造成精度损失，也能绕过现有的基于几何特性的防御机制。

Conclusion: 数据归因方法本身构成了一个新的攻击面。该研究强调了开发“归因鲁棒”且具备“激励兼容性”的评分机制的紧迫性，以防止恶意参与者操纵归因结果。

Abstract: Data attribution has become an important component of pricing, auditing, and governance in machine learning pipelines, yet most attribution methods implicitly assume that attribution values faithfully reflect participants' contributions. We show that this assumption can fail: a single participant in a standard distributed training workflow can substantially inflate its measured attribution value while preserving global utility. Our attribution-first attack uses latent optimization to inject small synthetic batches that preserve utility while exploiting non-IID label coverage and evaluator sensitivities. Across datasets, models, and multiple marginal-utility evaluators, the attack consistently increases the adversary's attribution value and reshapes the relative attribution structure among benign clients without degrading accuracy or triggering geometry-based defenses. These results show that attribution itself forms a new attack surface and motivate the development of attribution-robust and incentive-compatible scoring mechanisms.

</details>


### [83] [DeltaPrompts: Escaping the Zero-Delta Trap in Multimodal Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15532)
*Jaehun Jung,Hyunwoo Kim,Brandon Cui,Ximing Lu,David Acuna,Prithviraj Ammanabrolu,Yejin Choi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了VLM蒸馏中普遍存在的数据冗余问题，通过提出DeltaPrompts方法，主动筛选并合成能体现师生模型能力差异的训练数据，成功突破了模型性能的提升瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态模型蒸馏方法多依赖启发式选择或现成数据集，存在大量对学生模型学习无贡献的“零散度”冗余数据（占比高达69%），导致学生模型的性能提升在数据规模扩大后迅速陷入饱和。

Method: 研究提出了“DeltaPrompts”方法：首先识别现有数据集中的“零散度”（zero-delta）提示词（即师生模型预测分布一致），然后构建一个分阶段的合成流水线，利用现有数据作为种子，主动生成并筛选能够暴露教师与学生模型功能性差距（即高答案散度）的提示词，最终形成包含20万条高价值推理问题的训练数据集。

Result: 使用DeltaPrompts在三种典型场景下进行训练，均取得了显著性能提升。在涵盖图表、文档及感知推理的10个基准测试中，即便是在Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking等已高度优化的模型基础上，DeltaPrompts仍能实现最高15%的相对性能提升。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了从基于启发式的提示词生成转向基于模型差异（Delta）的主动数据合成，是提升轻量化多模态大模型（VLM）推理能力的关键。通过聚焦于教师与学生模型存在能力差距的“高散度”数据，可以显著打破性能饱和瓶颈。

Abstract: Distillation enables compact Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to obtain strong reasoning capabilities, yet the prompts driving this process are typically chosen via simple heuristics or aggregated from off-the-shelf datasets. We reveal a critical inefficiency in this approach: up to 69% of the prompts in standard chart / document reasoning datasets are effectively zero-delta, meaning the teacher and student already induce the exact same answer distribution. Training on these prompts provides minimal learning signal, causing student improvement to rapidly saturate regardless of data scale. To escape the zero-delta trap, we return to first principles: distillation fundamentally minimizes distributional divergence, and thus a prompt is valuable only if it exposes a functional capability gap between the teacher and student. We quantify this gap through answer divergence ($Δ$), demonstrating that non-zero divergence is critical for effective scaling. Building on this insight, we propose a staged synthesis pipeline that repurposes existing datasets as seeds, actively targeting student failure modes to produce better prompts. The result is DeltaPrompts, a diverse dataset of 200k synthetic, high-divergence reasoning problems. We evaluate DeltaPrompts across three distinct settings: on-policy distillation with the target teacher-student pair, transfer to a novel model family without regenerating the data, and off-policy fine-tuning of a non-reasoning model. Across all scenarios, DeltaPrompts drives substantial gains, yielding up to 15% relative improvement even on top of a highly-optimized reasoning model (e.g., Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking) -- averaged over 10 benchmarks spanning chart, document and perception-centric reasoning.

</details>


### [84] [CTF4Nuclear: Common Task Framework for Nuclear Fission and Fusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15549)
*Stefano Riva,Carolina Introini,Antonio Cammi,Dean Price,Alexey Yermakov,Yue Zhao,Philippe M. Wyder,Judah Goldfeder,Jan Williams,Amy Sara Rude,Matteo Tomasetto,Joe Germany,Joseph Bakarji,Georg Maierhofer,Miles Cranmer,J. Nathan Kutz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核反应堆的复杂多物理场模拟计算成本高昂，传统物理建模方法存在难以克服的简化误差，而现有的机器学习方法缺乏标准化的评估手段，难以满足核工程这一安全关键领域对模型可靠性和透明度的严格要求。

Method: 本文引入了一个通用的任务框架（Common Task Framework, CTF），该框架整合了多个核能及相关领域的系统数据集，并包含12种评估指标及一种基于稀疏测量的系统监测新范式，用于对机器学习基准模型进行系统性对比与评估。

Result: 研究通过该框架对多种机器学习基准模型进行了基准测试，揭示了现有方法在处理核工程复杂系统时的具体局限性，并强调了在隐蔽测试集上进行标准化评估的必要性。

Conclusion: 通过建立标准化的评估框架（CTF），本文为核工程领域中机器学习模型的可重复性、严谨性和性能评估设定了新标杆，有助于推动数据驱动方法在核能安全关键领域的稳健应用。

Abstract: The demand for clean energy is ever increasing, with new nuclear technologies presenting a complementary solution to renewable energies. However, designing and operating these systems is exceptionally difficult, given the complexity of the physical phenomena that interact to form the system dynamics. While high-fidelity simulations help to understand the non-linear, multi-physics interactions within a reactor, they are computationally expensive and rarely suitable for real-time applications. Furthermore, model-based approaches are inherently sensitive to simplifying assumptions required to derive their governing equations and parameters, leading to inevitable discrepancies with real-world measurements. In contrast, Machine Learning (ML) methods have the potential to generate reliable surrogate models which may be able to quickly predict the system's behaviour. However, the number of data-driven methods that can potentially be used for this task is large and diverse. In a safety-critical setting such as nuclear engineering, a fair comparison of different ML methods, and a clear understanding of their advantages and limitations, is of paramount importance. To address this, we introduce a Common Task Framework (CTF) for ML in nuclear engineering, building upon previous efforts in dynamical systems and seismology. This CTF considers a curated set of datasets from different nuclear and nuclear-adjacent systems. The CTF evaluates the performance of a method on 12 established metrics, alongside a new paradigm focused on system monitoring from sparse measurements only. We illustrate the framework by benchmarking standard ML baselines against these datasets, revealing current method limitations. Our vision is to replace ad hoc comparisons with standardized evaluations on hidden test sets, raising the bar for rigour and reproducibility in scientific ML for the nuclear industry.

### [85] [VSPO: Vector-Steered Policy Optimization for Behavioral Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15604)
*Xuechen Zhang,Zijian Huang,Kai Yang,Weijia Zhang,Jiasi Chen,Samet Oymak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了矢量引导策略优化（VSPO），通过利用行为引导向量来控制模型的采样强度，有效缓解了多目标优化中的奖励稀疏问题，在提升语言模型特定行为表现的同时确保了推理任务的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代语言模型微调中，常面临主任务准确性与次要行为偏好（如简洁度、专业性等）的权衡。当理想行为在基础模型中出现频率极低时，会产生严重的“稀疏行为奖励瓶颈”。现有的奖励塑形或蒸馏方法往往难以在保持任务精度的同时有效平衡这些行为偏好。

Method: 提出矢量引导策略优化（VSPO）。该方法在 GRPO 的基础上，利用目标行为的引导向量对模型采样过程进行干预，产生不同强度（intensity）的响应。其本质是一个在线（on-policy）潜空间自我蒸馏过程，通过改变采样强度来上采样稀疏的理想行为，从而增加样本多样性并加速策略优化过程。

Result: 理论上，在 Bandit 抽象模型下，VSPO 在引导分布与目标行为对齐时，表现出比奖励塑形（Reward-shaped GRPO）更好的迭代复杂性。实验上，在 MATH 和 MMLU-Pro 等推理基准上，VSPO 在解释专业性、自信度、鲁棒性及简洁度四个维度的行为控制上表现出色，且在任务准确率上优于或持平现有的奖励塑形、教师蒸馏及基于引导的基准方法。

Conclusion: VSPO 是一种高效且具有理论支撑的策略优化框架，通过引入行为引导向量（steering vector）并结合 GRPO，成功解决了多目标优化中的奖励稀疏问题。该方法在提升模型对特定行为的控制力（如专业性、自信度等）的同时，能够保持甚至提升任务性能，证明了其在复杂语言模型微调任务中的优越性与广泛适用性。

Abstract: Modern language models often need to optimize a primary accuracy objective while also accommodating secondary behavioral preferences, such as verbosity, agreeableness, or the level of technical expertise in its response. In practice, a base model may exhibit a desired behavior very rarely or not at all. Thus, endowing the model with a target behavior creates a sparse behavioral reward bottleneck. To address such multi-objective problems, we introduce Vector-Steered Policy Optimization (VSPO) which employs a steering vector associated with the target behavior to control the behavior intensity of the generated rollouts. VSPO is obtained by modifying GRPO to sample rollouts with varying steering intensities. This process can be interpreted as an on-policy latent self-distillation procedure where the model internalizes its steering vector. By varying steering intensities, VSPO upsamples rare behaviors and enriches rollout diversity, which alleviates the sparse reward issue and provably accelerates the policy optimization. Through comprehensive theory and experiments, we establish that VSPO has favorable properties compared to vanilla reward shaping and other alternative approaches. Specifically, under a bandit abstraction, VSPO provably achieves better iteration complexity than reward-shaped GRPO when the steering-induced distributions are sufficiently aligned with the target behavior. We evaluate VSPO across multiple reasoning benchmarks, including MATH and MMLU-Pro, for four target behaviors: explanation expertise, confidence expression, robustness to misleading context, and response verbosity. Our results show that VSPO consistently improves the control along target behavior while maintaining or improving task accuracy compared with reward shaping, teacher-trace distillation, and guidance-based baselines.

</details>


### [86] [CrystalBoltz: End-to-End Protein Structure Determination via Experiment-Guided Diffusion for X-Ray Crystallography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15564)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的蛋白质结构生成模型难以直接整合晶体学实验数据，导致结构解析（尤其是相位恢复）仍然依赖于耗时的人工精修和复杂的计算流程，需要一种能直接结合实验测量与结构预测的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为CrystalBoltz的生成式框架，将晶体学精修建模为原子结构的贝叶斯推断问题；利用预训练的蛋白质结构生成模型作为先验，直接对实验测量的结构因子幅度进行后验采样，随后进行原子坐标和B因子的精修。

Result: 在多个蛋白质晶体学数据集上，CrystalBoltz在结构坐标均方根偏差（RMSD）和R因子指标上均优于基准方法，同时将计算运行时间缩短了约33倍。

Conclusion: CrystalBoltz通过将生成式模型与贝叶斯推断相结合，成功将实验测量数据直接融入结构预测流程，实现了更高效、更精确的蛋白质结构解析，证明了生成式先验在解决晶体学相位问题中的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Generative models trained on public databases of protein structures, most of which have been determined by X-ray crystallography, now provide powerful priors for structure prediction. However, they are not readily conditioned on the measurements from a new crystallographic experiment, limiting their use for X-ray structure determination. In crystallography, the measured structure-factor amplitudes do not by themselves determine an electron density map or atomic structure because the associated phases are unobserved and must be inferred. Structure determination therefore remains an inverse problem in which candidate models must be both structurally plausible and consistent with measured diffraction data, often requiring substantial manual refinement by human experts. Emerging methods aim to incorporate experimental information more directly into predictive and refinement workflows. We present CrystalBoltz, a generative framework that casts crystallographic refinement as Bayesian inference over atomic structures and operates directly on structure-factor amplitudes. CrystalBoltz moves from unguided generation with a pre-trained prior over protein structures to experiment-guided posterior sampling, followed by atomic coordinate and B-factor refinement. Across multiple protein crystallography datasets, CrystalBoltz attains lower coordinate RMSD and lower R-factors than the strongest baselines considered, while reducing runtime by a factor of 33 relative to existing experimentally guided refinement.

To this end, we introduce universal horizon models (UHM), a generalization of GHM that directly predicts future states under arbitrary horizons. Experimental results on 100 challenging OGBench tasks demonstrate that the proposed method outperforms competitive baselines, particularly on tasks with highly suboptimal datasets and those requiring long-horizon reasoning. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 推导出的“对偶滤波器”算法在结构上与解码器专用 Transformer 的层结构高度一致。数值实验对比了最优控制解与已训练 Transformer 的注意力权重，结果揭示了在模型嵌入维度受限时，Transformer 能够隐式地捕捉并利用数据的非马尔可夫依赖性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功地通过最优控制理论为解码器专用 Transformer 的推理架构提供了理论基础，证明了 Transformer 的层结构可以视为一种最优推理过程的实现。实验表明，当嵌入维度不足时，Transformer 会隐式地利用序列的非马尔可夫结构来提升性能。

Abstract: Decoder-only transformers compute the conditional probability of the next token from a sequence of past observations. This paper derives, from first principles, inference architectures that solve the same prediction problem - and in doing so, recovers transformer-like layer operations as a consequence of optimal control theory. The framework is developed for two model classes: a nonlinear model of discrete-valued processes, directly motivated by the transformer, and a linear Gaussian model as a tractable baseline. For both model classes, the prediction objective is reformulated as an optimal control problem whose solution yields an explicit inference algorithm, the dual filter, with a layer structure that mirrors the layer structure of a decoder-only transformer. Numerical experiments provide a comparison of the optimal control to attention weights from a trained transformer. These experiments reveal that when the embedding dimension is insufficient, the transformer implicitly exploits non-Markovian structure.

### [91] [Position: Zeroth-Order Optimization in Deep Learning Is Underexplored, Not Underpowered](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15622)
*Sijia Liu,Yicheng Lang,Soumyadeep Pal,Changsheng Wang,Yancheng Huang,Chongyu Fan,James Diffenderfer,Bhavya Kailkhura,Yihua Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文反驳了零阶优化（ZO）无法扩展的观点，指出其局限性源于研究范式的局限，并提出了从子空间优化、系统集成及评估方法等角度进行创新的新框架，从而为在大规模资源受限场景下应用ZO优化铺平了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了六项核心改进立场：1. 通过方差控制、方差-查询权衡和方向导数视角重新评估可行性边界；2. 探索子空间和谱方法以实现方差缩减和良好的查询缩放；3. 利用ZO的前向传播特性作为系统优势，以提升通信效率和流水线友好性；4. 去除评估中的任务混淆，重新定义评估指标。

Result: 论文指出通过采用子空间优化、谱分析和系统感知的实现方式，可以大幅降低ZO优化的方差，并在资源受限环境下实现与一阶方法（梯度下降）更具竞争力的表现，为大规模ZO学习提供了理论和系统实现上的新路径。

Conclusion: 零阶优化（ZO）并非天生不可扩展，其局限性主要源于当前的开发范式。通过改变以估计量为中心的设计，转向子空间和谱方法，并结合系统级优势，ZO优化能够成为大规模、资源受限及黑盒学习场景下的高效替代方案。

Abstract: Zeroth-order (ZO) optimization, learning from finite differences of function evaluations without backpropagation, has recently regained attention in deep learning due to its memory efficiency and applicability to gray- or black-box pipelines. Yet, ZO methods are often dismissed as fundamentally unscalable because of estimator variance and unfavorable query complexity. We argue that this conclusion might be misguided: ZO optimization is underexplored, not underpowered. We show that many perceived limitations stem from myopic development practices, most notably full-space, element-wise, estimator-centric designs. We articulate six positions spanning the algorithmic, systems, and evaluation stack. First, we revisit the feasibility boundaries of estimator-centric ZO methods through variance control, variance-query tradeoffs, and directional-derivative lenses. Then, we identify three underexplored opportunities: (i) subspace and spectral views of ZO that enable interpretable variance reduction with graceful query scaling, (ii) the forward-only nature of ZO as a systems advantage for communication-efficient, pipeline-friendly, and resource-constrained training, and (iii) the need to de-obfuscate ZO evaluations from task complexity. We strongly advocate rethinking ZO optimization around its unique strengths and acting accordingly, opening a viable path toward large-scale, system-aware, and resource-efficient learning with ZO optimization.

### [92] [Layer Equivalence Is Not a Property of Layers Alone: How You Test Redundancy Changes What You Find](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16234)
*Gabriel Garcia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文指出在Transformer模型剪枝中，“替换”与“交换”是两种不同的等价性度量方式，且两者差异显著。研究建议在进行剪枝操作前，应综合评估这两种指标，而非仅依赖其中之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者指出目前在Transformer层压缩研究中，存在混淆“替换”和“交换”两种不同等价性测试的问题。这两种方法在评估层可剪枝性时可能存在显著差距，导致剪枝决策的准确性受影响，因此作者旨在明确这两者的差异并提出更稳健的评估流程。

Method: 通过在Pythia、Qwen3-8B和Llama-3.1-8B等不同架构和规模的模型上，测量“替换”与“交换”这两种协议在训练轨迹中的表现，对比它们在预测层移除安全性方面的差异。该诊断方法仅需未标记数据的正向传播即可实现。

Result: 在训练过程中，替换与交换之间的差距会随模型收敛而扩大。实验发现不同模型表现各异：在Qwen3-8B中，基于交换的剪枝远比基于替换的剪枝安全；而在Llama-3.1-8B中，两者在剪枝成本上表现相当，说明指标间的差异并不总是直接对应于移除效果。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在Transformer模型剪枝过程中，“替换（Replacement）”和“交换（Interchange）”两种衡量层等价性的指标并不等同。研究者在评估模型压缩潜力时，不能单纯依赖其中一种，建议在进行层移除或合并前，应同时对两种swap-KL指标进行诊断，以确保剪枝的安全性。

Abstract: When researchers ask whether two transformer layers are "equivalent" for compression, they often conflate distinct tests. Replacement asks whether one layer's map can substitute for another's in place; interchange asks whether two layers approximately commute when their positions are swapped. Both are output-grounded swap-KL probes, but they need not agree: on pretrained transformers the protocol gap can change which layers look safe to prune by several-fold under the same evaluator, especially when replacement distances are high.
  We measure both protocols across checkpoints and architectures. On a Pythia training trajectory (410M and 1.4B), the replacement-interchange gap grows from initialization to convergence. Under one matched WikiText-2 contract at 8B scale, Qwen3-8B enters a divergent regime: interchange-guided removal is several-fold safer than replacement-guided at the same layer budgets, while Llama-3.1-8B ties the two protocols for pruning cost even though interchange KL is lower, showing metric gaps need not map one-to-one to removal. Before layer removal or merging, score both swap-KLs on the target checkpoint; the diagnostic requires only unlabeled forward passes.

</details>


### [93] [IO-SVD: Input-Output Whitened SVD for Adaptive-Rank LLM Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15626)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）虽然性能强大，但高昂的存储和计算成本限制了其在资源受限及延迟敏感场景的应用。现有的基于SVD的后训练压缩方法存在缺乏双向白化、秩分配不合理及损失感知能力弱等问题，导致高压缩率下模型性能下降严重。

Method: 1. 提出IO-SVD方法，通过KL散度感知构建输入输出双向白化空间；2. 利用二阶KL损失展开构建输出侧敏感度指标；3. 引入高效的异构秩分配策略，基于一阶校准损失进行组件剪枝；4. 改进混合SVD-量化技术，通过损失感知重映射优化低秩因子的8-bit量化过程。

Result: 在多种LLM和VLM系列模型上进行了广泛实验，结果表明IO-SVD在实现显著模型压缩和推理加速的同时，将模型性能损耗降至最低。

Conclusion: IO-SVD通过创新的双向白化空间构建、异构秩分配以及结合量化的混合压缩策略，有效解决了大模型在资源受限环境下的部署难题，实现了模型压缩与推理加速的平衡。

Abstract: Large language models deliver strong performance across language and reasoning tasks, but their storage and compute costs remain major barriers to deployment in resource-constrained and latency-sensitive settings. SVD-based post-training compression offers a hardware-agnostic way to reduce model size and improve inference efficiency through low-rank factorization. However, existing methods often rely on input-only whitening spaces, homogeneous rank allocation, or loss-agnostic allocation heuristics, limiting their ability to preserve model quality under aggressive compression. We propose Input-Output Whitened SVD (IO-SVD), a post-training compression method that forms a KL-aware double-sided whitening space for model weights. Using a second-order expansion of the KL loss over the top-K token probabilities, IO-SVD constructs an output-side metric that captures predictive sensitivity, while input whitening captures activation statistics. We further introduce an efficient heterogeneous rank-allocation strategy that scores whitened singular components using first-order calibration loss estimates and prunes the least sensitive components under a global budget. Inspired by prior work that combines SVD truncation with quantization, we improve hybrid SVD-quantization compression through loss-aware remapping, which selects low-rank factor rows for 8-bit quantization based on the predicted loss change incurred by quantizing them. Extensive experiments across diverse LLM and VLM families, and inference-time analysis shows that IO-SVD compresses LLMs with minimal performance degradation while delivering practical inference speedups. Code is available at https://github.com/mint-vu/IO-SVD.git

</details>


### [94] [Sharp Spectral Thresholds for Logit Fixed Points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15651)
*Tongxi Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究针对Softmax反馈系统的稳定性问题，推导出了一个新的锐利判据（β\|ΠWΠ\|<2），证明了此类系统比传统理论所认为的更加稳健，并准确界定了系统发生相变的临界点，填补了以往在奖励响应机制研究中的理论缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统理论在评估Softmax反馈系统稳定性时过于保守，导致无法识别真实的稳定边界，错失了大量稳定运行的机制区域，且未能准确刻画系统从稳定走向分叉的本质转折点。因此，作者旨在建立一个更精准的数学判据，以弥补这一理论空白。

Method: 通过数学推导，证明了有限维仿射Logit系统在稳定性方面的锐利欧几里得阈值（即β\|ΠWΠ\|<2），取代了以往基于“单位尺度响应”的过于保守的条件。该方法不仅考虑了系统的随机性，还准确捕捉了系统在奖励响应性增强后的动态变化。

Result: 提出了一个新的、与维度无关的稳定性阈值，显著扩大了Softmax反馈系统的认证稳定边界。该结果证明了即便在系统对奖励变得更具响应性时，其依然能够保持全局可预测性，从而准确界定了系统发生定性相变的真实临界点。

Conclusion: 该论文纠正了传统上对Softmax反馈系统稳定性的过度保守估计，揭示了一个更广阔的稳定区域，并精确识别了系统发生分叉（相变）的数学临界点。该成果为理解强化学习、博弈动力学等领域中的自强化系统提供了更强有力的稳定性保障。

Abstract: Softmax feedback systems are a common mathematical core of entropy-regularized reinforcement learning, logit game dynamics, population choice, and mean-field variational updates. Their central stability question is simple: when does a self-reinforcing softmax system produce a unique and globally predictable outcome? Classical theory gives a conservative answer. By treating softmax as a unit-scale response, it certifies stability only in a strongly randomized regime.
  We prove that the classical approach misses an entire stable regime and does not identify the point at which the qualitative change truly occurs. For finite-dimensional affine logit systems, the sharp dimension-free Euclidean threshold is $$β\|ΠWΠ\|_{\mathcal T\to\mathcal T}<2,$$ rather than the previously used condition, which certifies stability only while the softmax system remains safely over-regularized. Our theorem fills the previously missing pre-bifurcation regime, extending stability guarantees for affine softmax feedback systems to reward-responsive yet globally predictable systems. It enlarges the certified stability boundary for these systems and identifies where the model genuinely undergoes a phase transition.

### [95] [On the Power of Adaptivity for $\varepsilon$-Best Arm Identification in Linear Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15663)
*Arnab Maiti,Yunbei Xu,Kevin Jamieson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了线性强盗问题中 $\varepsilon$-最优臂识别的样本复杂度，明确了非自适应算法的界限，并证明了虽然在许多常见情况下自适应采样带来的收益有限，但在特定结构下，自适应采样可实现多项式级别的显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨线性强盗算法中 $\varepsilon$-最优臂识别问题的最小极大样本复杂度，特别是分析自适应采样相比于非自适应采样在不同动作集下究竟能带来多大的性能提升（即存在多项式级差距的结构性条件）。

Method: 1. 提出了一种非自适应固定设计算法，并推导了其最优样本复杂度下界。
2. 对比了多种自然动作集（超立方体、$\ell_2$球、m-集合等）下的自适应与非自适应采样效率。
3. 构造了特定动作集，并设计了基于自适应算法的 $\ell_2$-范数估计子程序，以展示自适应带来的多项式级样本复杂度优势。

Result: 1. 确定了非自适应固定设计算法的样本复杂度为 $\mathcal{O}\!\left(\frac{d\log(1/δ)}{\varepsilon^2}+\frac{w(\mathcal{X})^2}{\varepsilon^2}\right)$。
2. 证明了对于超立方体等自然动作集，自适应仅能实现对数级别的改进。
3. 证明了存在特定的动作集，使得自适应采样能够相比非自适应方法实现多项式级别的样本复杂度改进，并提供了一种高效的自适应 $\ell_2$-范数估计算法。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了线性强盗算法中自适应采样与非自适应采样在 $\varepsilon$-最优臂识别任务上的性能边界。研究证明了对于许多自然动作集，自适应采样仅能带来对数级别的提升，但也首次构造了能够实现多项式级别性能优势的特殊动作集，这依赖于高效的自适应 $\ell_2$-范数估计方法。

Abstract: We study the minimax sample complexity of $\varepsilon$-best arm identification in linear bandits. Given a compact action set $\mathcal{X}$ that spans $\mathbb{R}^d$ and an unknown reward vector $θ\in\mathbb{R}^d$, the goal is to output an arm $\widehat{x}\in\mathcal{X}$ such that $\langle \widehat{x},θ\rangle \ge \max_{x\in\mathcal{X}} \langle x,θ\rangle - \varepsilon$ with probability at least $1-δ$, using as few samples as possible.
  First, we present a non-adaptive fixed-design method with sample complexity $\mathcal{O}\!\left(\frac{d\log(1/δ)}{\varepsilon^2}+\frac{w(\mathcal{X})^2}{\varepsilon^2}\right)$, where $w(\mathcal{X})$ is a Gaussian width term dependent on $\mathcal{X}$, and we prove a matching lower bound $Ω\!\left(\frac{d\log(1/δ)}{\varepsilon^2}+\frac{w(\mathcal{X})^2}{\varepsilon^2}\right)$ for all non-adaptive fixed-design methods.
  We then turn to adaptive sampling. We raise an important structural question: beyond the canonical basis, are there structured action sets for which adaptivity yields only logarithmic-factor improvements over the optimal non-adaptive rate? We answer in the affirmative for several natural action sets, namely the hypercube, the $\ell_2$ ball, $m$-sets, and multi-task multi-armed bandits.
  Finally, we provide the first construction of an action set $\mathcal{X}$ for which adaptivity yields a polynomial-factor improvement over every non-adaptive algorithm. A key ingredient behind this separation is an $\ell_2$-norm estimation subroutine: we design an adaptive algorithm that uses $\mathcal{O}\!\left(\frac{d\log(1/δ)}{\varepsilon^2}\right)$ samples from the unit $\ell_2$ ball in $\mathbb{R}^d$ and outputs an estimate $\widehat r$ satisfying $|\widehat r-\|θ\|_2|\le \varepsilon$ with probability at least $1-δ$, where $θ$ is the unknown reward vector.

### [96] [Interaction-Aware Influence Functions for Group Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15675)
*Jaeseung Heo,Kyeongheung Yun,Youngbin Choi,Sehyun Hwang,Jungseul Ok,Dongwoo Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对传统影响函数无法捕捉训练样本间交互作用的局限，本论文提出了一种二阶交互感知影响函数，通过引入成对交互项，有效提升了对数据删除影响的预测精度及数据选择的质量，特别是在大模型指令微调场景下表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的影响函数通过简单累加个体样本的影响来估计一组样本的影响，这种方法忽略了数据样本之间复杂的联合作用（如冗余或互补性），导致在评估群体影响时存在偏差。因此，研究者旨在开发一种能捕捉样本间交互作用的方法，以更准确地评估数据对模型训练的贡献。

Method: 作者提出了一种交互感知影响函数（Interaction-aware Influence Function），通过对目标函数进行二阶泰勒展开，在传统的一阶影响函数基础上增加了一个成对交互项（pairwise interaction term）。该项利用海森矩阵（Hessian matrix）或其近似，量化了两个样本对模型参数影响的一致性，从而捕捉样本间的冗余或互补关系。

Result: 在六个数据集-模型对的实验中，该方法在跟踪“留组删除”（leave-group-out retraining）任务上的表现显著优于一阶影响函数。在Llama-3.1-8B的指令微调数据选择任务中，该方法在七个下游任务中的五个任务上超过了现有的影响函数和表征相似度基线，且在标准影响函数表现不如随机选择的情况下仍能保持优势。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的交互感知影响函数成功捕捉了训练数据之间的联合影响，能够更准确地反映数据组的删除效果，并在大模型指令微调场景下展现了优于传统方法的筛选能力，为理解模型行为和优化数据选择提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Influence functions approximate how removing a training example changes a quantity of interest, called the target function, such as a held-out loss. To estimate the influence of a group of examples, the standard practice is to sum the individual influences of its members. However, this sum does not capture how examples jointly affect the target: a pair of examples may be redundant or complementary, but the sum cannot distinguish these cases. We propose an interaction-aware influence function that characterizes how interactions between examples influence the target. By expanding the target to second order around the trained parameters, we obtain an estimator that augments the standard sum with a pairwise interaction term that captures the alignment between two examples' effects on the target. We empirically evaluate our estimator in two settings. First, on six dataset-model pairs spanning logistic regression, MLPs, and ResNet-9, our estimator tracks leave-group-out retraining substantially better than first-order influence across all settings. Second, when used as a greedy selection rule for instruction-tuning data on Llama-3.1-8B, it beats prior influence-based and representation-similarity baselines on five of seven downstream tasks, in a regime where standard influence-based selection underperforms random selection.

### [97] [FRWKV+: Adaptive Periodic-Position Branch Interaction for Frequency-Space Linear Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15690)
*Qingyuan Yang,Dongyue Chen,Da Teng,Junhua Xiao,Jiaji Pan,Shizhuo Deng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FRWKV+ 是一种改进的轻量级时间序列预测模型，通过引入跨分支门控和自适应信任机制，实现了频率域分支间的高效交互及周期性信息的智能选取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的轻量级频率域时间序列预测模型存在两个核心挑战：一是频率域复数的实部和虚部流之间缺乏有效的信息交换；二是周期性位置提示仅在数据集和预测视界可靠时才有用，缺乏灵活的筛选机制。

Method: 1. 引入跨分支门控（Cross-branch Gates）：在实部和虚部频率流之间交换压缩上下文，实现两者的相互调节。
2. 开发自适应相位门（Adaptive PhaseGate）：提取周期性位置上下文并生成符号修正信号。
3. 实施自适应信任机制（Adaptive Trust Mechanism）：在样本、变量和通道级别动态控制修正强度，确保仅在可靠时引入周期性信息，从而在提高精度的同时保持高效性。

Result: 在严格匹配的 FRWKV 系列消融实验中，FRWKV+ 实现了最高的 MSE 胜出率，并在特定的周期性场景中表现出显著的性能增益，验证了所提机制的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 FRWKV+ 模型通过引入跨分支门控机制和自适应相位门机制，有效解决了频率域预测中实部与虚部信息交互不足以及周期性位置信息利用不当的问题，显著提升了长序列时间序列预测的性能与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Long-term time series forecasting is essential for decision making in energy, finance, transportation, and healthcare systems. Recent lightweight forecasting models improve efficiency by operating in transformed or linearized spaces, but two challenges remain in frequency-space forecasting. The real and imaginary streams of complex spectra contain complementary information that is often weakly exchanged, and periodic-position cues can help recurring patterns only when they are reliable for the current dataset and prediction horizon. To address these challenges, we propose FRWKV+, an enhanced FRWKV forecasting model for selective periodic-position branch interaction. FRWKV+ first introduces cross-branch gates that exchange compact contexts between the real and imaginary frequency streams, allowing each stream to modulate the other. It then uses the Adaptive PhaseGate mechanism to extract periodic-position context and generate signed corrections to these gates. An adaptive trust mechanism controls the correction strength at the sample, variable, and channel levels, so periodic-position information is admitted as a reliable correction signal while preserving the efficiency of the FRWKV backbone. External benchmark tables report a separately labeled FRWKV-family selected system for manuscript-level comparison, while mechanism-level claims are based on strict matched-seed FRWKV-family ablations and representative component-level ablations. Under this matched protocol, FRWKV+ achieves the largest MSE winner coverage among the family variants and provides clear gains in selected periodic regimes. Component analysis further supports the usefulness of periodic-position context, signed correction, and adaptive trust in these regimes, while revealing boundary cases where simpler correction rules remain preferable.

</details>


### [98] [SEED: Targeted Data Selection by Weighted Independent Set](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15691)
*Yuan Zhang,Lifeng Guo,Junwen Pan,Chang Liu,Wenzhao Zheng,Kuan Cheng,Kurt Keutzer,Shanghang Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SEED 提出了一种基于图论的稳健数据选择框架，通过节点价值校准和局部尺度归一化，从大规模数据中筛选出高质量、高多样性的子集，显著提升了模型训练性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模数据集中的数据质量参差不齐且存在冗余，导致模型训练效率低下。现有数据选择方法在处理梯度噪声及跨域分布带来的图结构不平衡问题时表现不佳，难以平衡样本质量与多样性。

Method: SEED 将数据选择建模为相似度图上的加权独立集（WIS）问题。针对原有方法的不足，提出了两个关键改进：一是“节点价值校准”，通过限制影响力估计至双侧显著子空间，滤除噪声信号；二是“局部尺度归一化”，通过根据局部邻域密度调整边阈值，解决跨域分布带来的结构不平衡问题。

Result: 构建了精简多模态数据集 Honeybee-Remake-SEED-200K。实验表明，SEED 在指令微调、视觉指令微调及语义分割等多个任务上均优于现有的先进数据选择方法。

Conclusion: SEED 通过将数据选择建模为加权独立集问题，并结合节点价值校准和局部尺度归一化技术，成功解决了在大规模语料中筛选高质量、多样化样本的难题，为模型训练提供了一种高效的数据精简范式。

Abstract: Data selection seeks to identify a compact yet informative subset from large-scale training corpora, balancing sample quality against collection diversity. We formulate this problem as a Weighted Independent Set (WIS) on a similarity graph, where nodes represent data samples weighted by influence, and edges connect semantically redundant pairs. This formulation naturally yields subsets that are simultaneously high-quality and diverse. However, two challenges arise in practice: naive node weights fail to distinguish informative signals from gradient noise, and edge construction under heterogeneous domain distributions produces structurally imbalanced graphs that bias selection toward sparse regions. To address these issues, we introduce two principled refinements from a unified graph perspective: (1) \textit{node value calibration} that restricts influence estimation to the bilateral salient subspace to ground node importance in task-relevant signals rather than surface-level statistics; (2) \textit{local scale normalization} that adapts edge thresholds to local neighborhood density, mitigating graph imbalance induced by cross-domain distribution shifts. Together, these components yield a robust and scalable data selection pipeline dubbed SEED. We further construct \texttt{Honeybee-Remake-SEED-200K}, a compact multimodal dataset curated by SEED. Extensive experiments show that SEED consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods on instruction tuning, visual instruction tuning, and semantic segmentation across diverse model families.

### [99] [Tighter Regret Bounds for Contextual Action-Set Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15692)
*Zijun Chen,Zihan Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了动作集合随情节变化的强化学习问题，通过将MVP算法扩展至此框架，实现了近乎最优的极小极大遗憾界及依赖于间隙的性能提升，为处理具有限制性动作空间的强化学习提供了理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多实际的强化学习场景中，动作的选择往往受到环境或任务上下文（context）的限制。然而，现有的强化学习理论主要集中在静态动作空间。为了解决具有情节依赖动作限制（episode-dependent admissible action sets）的强化学习问题，作者试图探究如何优化遗憾界并验证算法在不同上下文分布下的性能。

Method: 本文将MVP（Minimax Value-aware Planning）算法扩展到具有情节依赖动作限制的设置中，采用基于价值的迭代方法，通过构建模型估计和置信区间，结合乐观原则应对动作集合的变化。在分析中使用了遗憾分解技术、极小极大优化理论以及针对不同间隙条件的变体界限推导。

Result: 1. 对于对抗性上下文，证明了 $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{SAH^3K\log L})$ 的极小极大遗憾界；2. 对于随机上下文，遗憾界可优化为 $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{SAH^3K})$；3. 在固定上下文分布下，实现了 $\widetilde{O}(SAH^3/\epsilon^2)$ 的样本复杂度；4. 推导出一种依赖于间隙（gap-dependent）的遗憾界，在子优性间隙较大时，该界显著优于极小极大率。

Conclusion: 本文证明了MVP算法在具有情节依赖动作限制的强化学习框架下具有强大的理论保障，能够实现接近最优的极小极大遗憾界，并提供了针对特定问题的依赖于间隙的改进遗憾界。

Abstract: We study episodic reinforcement learning with fixed reward and transition functions, but with episode-dependent admissible action sets that are observed at the start of each episode. Performance is measured by cumulative regret against the episode-wise optimal value, $\sum_{k=1}^K [V^{*,M^k} - V^{π^k,M^k}]$, where $M^k$ represents the action context in the $k$-th episode. We show that the MVP algorithm naturally extends to this framework and enjoys strong theoretical guarantees. In particular, we establish a minimax regret bound of $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{SAH^3K\log L})$ for adversarial contexts, where $L$ denotes the number of possible contexts. This result implies a regret bound of $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{SAH^3K})$ for stochastic contexts. We further translate the stochastic regret guarantee into a sample complexity bound of $\widetilde{O}(SAH^3/ε^2)$ for a fixed context distribution.
  In addition, we derive a gap-dependent regret bound of \[ \widetilde O\left( \inf_{p\in [0,1)} \left( \frac{1}{Δ_{\min}^{p}} + pKΔ_{\min}^{p} \right)\log K \cdot \mathrm{poly}(S,A,H) \right), \] where $Δ_{\min}^{p}$ is the global $p$-trimmed positive-gap floor over suboptimal $(h,s,a)$ triples. This bound can substantially improve upon the minimax rate when the relevant suboptimality gaps are large.

### [100] [Going Beyond the Edge: Distributed Inference of Transformer Models on Ultra-Low-Power Wireless Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15694)
*Alexander Gräfe,Ding Huo,Vincent de Bakker,Johannes Berger,Marco Zimmerling,Sebastian Trimpe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CATS 是一种用于超低功耗 IoT 设备的分布式 Transformer 推理框架，通过协同设计通信协议（SomeGather）与训练策略，使多设备协同运行超大模型成为可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer 模型在物联网（IoT）应用中日益重要，但其高昂的算力和内存需求超过了单个超低功耗 IoT 设备的承载极限。本研究旨在通过分布式计算解决这一矛盾。

Method: 1. 提出 SomeGather 通信原语：通过剪枝技术选择性地广播激活列，降低通信带宽与内存占用。
2. 模型并行划分：设计了基于 SomeGather 的分布式模型划分策略。
3. 训练阶段的消息丢弃（Message-dropout）：模拟无线通信中的丢包现象，增强模型对通信不确定性的鲁棒性。

Result: 在实机实验中，CATS 支持多达 16 台设备协同工作，能够运行比单台设备极限大 14 倍的 Transformer 模型，且在保证模型准确率的同时有效应对了无线通信的不可靠性。

Conclusion: CATS 成功在超低功耗无线设备集群上实现了分布式 Transformer 推理，证明了通过协同设计划分、通信与训练策略，可以将大型模型部署在资源受限的 IoT 环境中，突破了单设备的算力与内存瓶颈。

Abstract: Transformer models are rapidly becoming a cornerstone of modern Internet of Things (IoT) applications, yet their computational and memory demands far exceed the capabilities of a single typical ultra-low-power IoT device. We present CATS, a framework for distributed transformer inference on ultra-low-power wireless devices, enabling multiple devices to collaboratively execute models far larger than what a single device can sustain. At its core, CATS is a communication-aware distributed transformer inference scheme co-designed across transformer partitioning, wireless communication and training. It employs SomeGather, a new pruned communication primitive that selectively broadcasts activation columns to reduce communication bandwidth and RAM usage without sacrificing model accuracy. Building on SomeGather, we design a partitioning method that exploits this primitive for efficient model parallelism. To cope with unreliable wireless communication, CATS employs message-dropout during training, which mimics packet losses and yields models that are robust to message loss during inference. In real-world experiments, we show that CATS brings distributed transformer inference to ultra-low-power wireless devices for the first time, with deployments on up to 16 devices that collaboratively execute transformer models up to 14 times larger than what a single device can run.

</details>


### [101] [AGOP-IxG: A Gradient Covariance Filter for Local Feature Attribution on Tabular Data, with a Controlled Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15700)
*Raj Kiran Gupta Katakam*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 AGOP-IxG 的新型表格数据归因方法，通过梯度外积矩阵运算实现了比传统方法（如 SHAP）快几个数量级的推理速度，并在合成基准测试中展示了更高的特征归因保真度。

Method: 提出了一种名为 AGOP-IxG 的方法，该方法通过将样本的梯度与预先计算的 Top-K 秩截断平均梯度外积矩阵（Average Gradient Outer Product matrix）相乘来获取特征归因。研究通过构建三种具有已知解析或数值解的合成表格任务，对比了 AGOP-IxG 与 SHAP、Integrated Gradients、InputXGradient 和 LIME 的表现，并利用 ROAR 协议在真实数据集上评估了全局忠实度。

Conclusion: AGOP-IxG 是一种高效且在局部归因上具有高保真度的特征归因方法。尽管它在全局特征排序任务上与其他主流方法表现相当，但在需要快速、准确的样本级解释场景（如 AutoML 生产环境）中，它表现出显著的计算效率优势。

Abstract: Automated machine learning pipelines increasingly produce models whose predictions must be explained to end users, auditors, and downstream decision systems. The most widely used feature attribution methods (SHAP, Integrated Gradients, LIME) are typically chosen by convention rather than measured fidelity, because rigorous evaluation is impeded by the absence of ground-truth attribution on real data. We propose AGOP-IxG, a fast per-sample attribution method for tabular classifiers that pre-multiplies the per-sample gradient by a top-$K$ rank-truncated Average Gradient Outer Product matrix, and evaluate it against four widely-used baselines on a controlled tabular benchmark designed for AutoML practitioners. In Part 1, we construct three synthetic multi-class tabular tasks (linear, sparse nonlinear, interaction-based) where ground-truth attribution per sample is analytically or numerically derivable, and compare five methods: AGOP-IxG, SHAP (DeepExplainer), Integrated Gradients, InputXGradient, and LIME. AGOP-IxG leads on Spearman rank correlation and noise feature mass on all three synthetic datasets, and on top-$k$ precision on the interaction dataset. Across all settings, AGOP-IxG is approximately $350\times$ to $1{,}650\times$ faster than SHAP. ### [104] [A Unified Perturbation Framework for Analyzing Leaderboard Stability and Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15761)
*Hosna Oyarhoseini,Jimmy Lin,Amir-Hossein Karimi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了当前大模型排行榜（如 LMArena）极度缺乏鲁棒性，少于1%的针对性数据扰动即可导致排名剧烈波动，并提出了一种基于影响函数的分析框架用于审计及模拟排名操纵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型排行榜（如 LMArena）虽然是评估模型性能的核心工具，但其排名的稳健性缺乏深入研究。研究旨在揭示排行榜在面对少量数据扰动时的脆弱性，并提供一种量化的审计工具来评估其稳定性。

Method: 提出了一种基于影响函数（Influence-based approximation）的统一扰动框架，用于分析 Bradley-Terry 模型构建的排行榜。该方法系统地研究了“删除（Drop）”、“添加（Add）”和“翻转（Flip）”等三种比赛层面的扰动，以及玩家（模型）移除操作，并考察其对排行榜 Top-k 成员稳定性、Kendall's tau 相关性以及置信区间不确定性的影响。

Result: 研究发现当前的排行榜在面对微小扰动（小于1%的针对性修改）时极其脆弱，能够轻易改变排名榜首、降低 Kendall's tau 指标并扭曲置信区间。此外，所提出的影响函数分析法不仅能用于审计，还能以极高的效率操纵排名（促进或贬低特定模型），其效率远超现有的基准算法。

Conclusion: 现有的排行榜体系存在显著的鲁棒性缺陷，极易受到少量扰动的影响。研究强调了在评估大模型时引入更严谨的鲁棒性审计工具的必要性，以防止评价结果被恶意操纵或因数据波动而产生误导。

Abstract: Evaluation leaderboards such as LMArena play a central role in benchmarking large language models by aggregating pairwise human preferences into model rankings, yet the robustness of these rankings remains poorly understood. We present a unified perturbation framework for analyzing Bradley-Terry leaderboards under structured data modifications using influence-based approximations. Our framework studies three match-level perturbations -- Drop, Add, and Flip -- together with player removal, and evaluates their effects on top-k membership, global ranking consistency via Kendall's tau, and confidence-interval-based uncertainty. Across Chatbot Arena and six additional pairwise-comparison datasets, we show that modern leaderboards are non-robust across all three objectives: sub-1% targeted perturbations can change the top-ranked model, degrade Kendall's tau, and alter confidence intervals. Beyond robustness auditing, we show that the same influence scores enable efficient targeted perturbations, promoting or demoting specific models and reducing target-model uncertainty with fewer actions than previous manipulation and active-sampling baselines. By summarizing these effects with normalized dataset-level robustness scores, our framework provides a practical and helpful tool for auditing leaderboard stability and motivating more robust evaluation protocols.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一类结合“经验回放（Replay-based training）”与“序贯不变性对齐（Sequential invariance alignment）”的持续学习新方法。该方法旨在通过捕捉跨领域不变的因果机制，在保持先前知识的同时，提取出对新领域具有强鲁棒性的表征。

Result: 在视觉、医学、制造和生态学等领域的六个基准数据集和真实世界数据集上的实验表明，该方法在未见目标域的泛化性能上持续优于现有的持续学习基线方法。消融实验也验证了将传统域不变表示学习方法直接用于序贯学习的效果十分有限。

Conclusion: 本文是首个将域不变表示学习应用于持续学习领域的工作。研究表明，通过显式地对齐不同领域间的结构不变性，可以显著提升模型在未见领域上的泛化能力，克服传统持续学习方法因关注领域特定线索而导致的“捷径学习”问题。

Abstract: Continual learning (CL) aims to train models sequentially over multiple domains without forgetting previously learned knowledge. However, existing CL methods optimize for in-domain performance and are therefore prone to learning spurious, domain-specific cues (``shortcut learning''), which limits generalization to unseen domains after deployment. In this paper, we address this limitation through continual learning of domain-invariant representation. We introduce a broad class of CL methods that sequentially learn representations capturing invariant structures across domains. Our methods are motivated by the observation that such invariant structures often preserve the underlying causal mechanisms, which can reduce the risk of overfitting to domain-specific cues and thus offer better out-of-domain generalization. Our proposed CL methods combine replay-based training with a tailored sequential invariance alignment to learn -- and preserve -- invariant structures over time. We evaluate our methods under a deployment-oriented protocol that measures performance on unseen target domains. Across six benchmark and real-world datasets spanning vision, medicine, manufacturing, and ecology, our methods consistently outperform existing CL baselines in terms of generalization to unseen target domains. As an ablation, we further show that naïve extensions of sequential training with existing domain-invariant representation learning (DIRL) methods provide only limited benefits. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to develop domain-invariant representation methods for CL.

### [106] [AOT-POT: Adaptive Operator Transformation for Large-Scale PDE Pre-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15793)
*Qitan Lv,Hong Wang,Zhongkai Hao,Wen Wu,Xuenan Xu,Bowen Zhou,Feng Wu,Chao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多 PDE 预训练中算子异构带来的建模难题，AOT-POT 通过自适应算子变换机制，将多样化的 PDE 算子动态转化为统一易学的形式，在极低参数代价下显著提升了模型的精度与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 PDE 预训练研究过分依赖增加模型容量（Scaling），忽略了不同 PDE 算子本身的结构差异和复杂性，导致模型难以高效统一建模异构算子。受经典数值分析启发，作者旨在寻找一种方法将多样化的算子转化为更简单的对齐形式。

Method: 提出 AOT-POT 框架，通过引入多并行流隐藏表示，在子层前后进行自适应聚合与重分布，并利用 Sinkhorn 投影的双随机矩阵进行流混合，从而在输入依赖的基础上动态将复杂的 PDE 算子转化为统一的、易于建模的形式。

Result: 在 12 个 PDE 基准测试中达到 SOTA 水平，参数量仅增加 3%，相对 L2 误差平均降低 40.9%（最高达 77.6%）。在微调阶段，领域内任务 L2 误差降低最高达 92%，未见过的领域外任务最高降低 89%。

Conclusion: AOT-POT 证明了通过自适应算子变换（而非单纯增加模型参数）来统一异构 PDE 算子，是构建高效通用科学机器学习基础模型的关键方向。该方法在处理多 PDE 任务时具有极高的泛化能力和迁移潜力。

Abstract: Pre-training neural operators on diverse partial differential equation (PDE) datasets has emerged as a promising direction for building general-purpose surrogate models in scientific machine learning. However, the inherent complexity and structural diversity of PDE solution operators make multi-PDE pre-training fundamentally challenging. Existing methods mainly address this by increasing model capacity, while leaving the target solution operators unchanged. Inspired by classical numerical analysis, we instead propose to transform complex and diverse solution operators into simpler, better-aligned forms that are easier to model jointly. Since the optimal transformation varies across PDE types, it must be adaptive and input-dependent, allowing a single neural operator to approximate an entire family of operators. We instantiate this idea as AOT-POT (adaptive operator-transformation for pre-training operator transformer), which expands hidden representations into multiple parallel streams, adaptively aggregates and redistributes them before and after each sub-layer, and mixes streams through Sinkhorn-projected doubly stochastic matrices for stable training. These mechanisms together reshape diverse solution operators into a unified form that can be effectively modeled by a single architecture. Empirically, AOT-POT achieves state-of-the-art performance on 12 PDE benchmarks with only 3\% additional parameters, reducing relative L2 error by up to 77.6\% (40.9\% on average). Fine-tuning AOT-POT further reduces L2 error by up to 92\% on in-domain PDEs and 89\% on out-of-domain PDEs (unseen types during pre-training), demonstrating that adaptive operator transformation is an effective and complementary direction for advancing PDE foundation models beyond simply scaling model capacity.

</details>


### [107] [Practical Validity Conditions for Byzantine-Tolerant Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15887)
*Mélanie Cambus,Darya Melnyk,Tijana Milentijević,Stefan Schmid*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对拜占庭容错联邦学习，本文提出了最小包围球（MEB）有效性条件，解决了传统凸性条件在实际应用中的局限性，并为多种经典聚合规则提供了理论保证，为构建更鲁棒的聚合机制提供了实用框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的拜占庭容错联邦学习中的凸有效性（Convex validity）条件虽然理论保证强，但存在维度依赖的弹性问题，且排除了许多实际有效的聚合规则，无法良好适配现代联邦学习系统。因此，需要探索更具普适性和实践价值的有效性条件。

Method: 1. 提出了最小包围球（MEB）及其乘法松弛版本（c-MEB）有效性条件；2. 推导了满足c-MEB条件的最优聚合规则（MinMax-MEB）；3. 证明了最小直径平均（Minimum-diameter averaging）、中心点（Medoid）和几何中位数（Geometric median）等标准聚合器的MEB有效性；4. 对比分析了MEB有效性与既有凸性、框性等有效性条件的关系。

Result: 1. 证明了精确的MEB有效性具有有限的弹性，但c-MEB在多数诚实节点下是可实现的；2. 给出了c < sqrt(2)边界下的最优MinMax-MEB聚合规则；3. 建立了MEB有效性与现有多种几何有效性条件（如凸性、框性）的系统性映射关系。

Conclusion: 本文建立了最小包围球（MEB）有效性条件，证明了其松弛版本（c-MEB）在多数诚实节点（n>2t）的条件下是可实现的，并为多种现有聚合规则提供了统一的几何解释，从而弥合了分布式计算理论与拜占庭鲁棒聚合规则之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: Robust aggregation is the core operation in Byzantine-tolerant federated learning. To ensure the quality of aggregation independently of data distribution or attacks, validity conditions are needed. They provide geometric guarantees of where the output of the aggregation must lie. The widespread convex validity requires the output to lie in the convex hull of the honest vectors. Although this guarantee is strong in theory, it is poorly suited to modern federated learning systems, as it has dimension-dependent resilience and excludes many practical aggregation rules.
  We introduce the minimum enclosing ball (MEB) validity condition for robust aggregation, as well as its multiplicative relaxation, $c$-MEB validity, where $c$ is a constant. We show that exact MEB validity still suffers from limited resilience, while relaxed $c$-MEB validity is achievable if a majority of clients is honest, i.e. $n>2t$. We give an optimal MinMax-MEB rule for the relaxed condition with the bound $c<\sqrt{2}$ and prove explicit relaxed-MEB guarantees for standard aggregators including minimum-diameter averaging, medoid and geometric median. Finally, we relate MEB validity to convex, relaxed-convex and box validity studied in prior literature, thus providing a systematic map of geometric validity conditions for Byzantine-robust aggregation. Our results show that relaxed MEB validity connects validity conditions in distributed computing and Byzantine-tolerant aggregation rules, and offers a practical alternative to convex validity.

</details>


### [108] [LoCO: Low-rank Compositional Rotation Fine-tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15916)
*An Nguyen,Jaesik Choi,Anh Tong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LoCO 是一种新型参数高效微调（PEFT）方法，通过利用低秩斜对称矩阵构建可并行计算的组合旋转，在保持模型预训练几何结构（正交性）的同时，实现了高效且高性能的模型适配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的参数高效微调方法（如 LoRA）虽然实现了参数高效性，但在模型微调过程中难以有效保持预训练表示的几何结构。为了解决这一问题，研究者旨在引入一种既能保持正交性又具有低计算复杂度的微调机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为“低秩组合正交微调”（LoCO）的方法。该方法通过低秩斜对称矩阵构建正交变换，并利用组合旋转链（compositional rotation chains）来实现。此外，作者提出了一种近似方案，实现了组合旋转的完全并行计算，从而在保持正交约束的同时，将计算复杂度控制在较低水平。

Result: LoCO 在扩散模型（Diffusion Transformers）、视觉模型（Vision Transformers）和大语言模型等多种领域进行了实验。结果表明，LoCO 在性能上优于或足以媲美现有的正交与非正交微调方法。

Conclusion: LoCO 是一种高效且强大的参数高效微调（PEFT）方法。通过保持正交性，它能更好地保留预训练模型的几何结构，在多种任务中表现出优于或媲美现有主流微调技术的性能，为大模型适配提供了一种新的高效选择。

Abstract: Parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) has emerged as an critical technique for adapting large-scale foundation models across natural language processing and computer vision. While existing methods such as low-rank adaptations achieve parameter efficiency via low-rank weight updates, they are limited in their ability to preserve the geometric structure of pretrained representations. We introduce Low-rank Compositional Orthogonal fine-tuning (LoCO), a novel PEFT method that constructs orthogonal transformations through low-rank skew-symmetric matrices and compositional rotation chains. We propose an approximation scheme that enables fully parallel computation of compositional rotations, making the approach practical for high-dimensional feature spaces. Our method maintains low computational complexity while maintaining orthogonality with controlled approximation error. We validate LoCO across diverse domains, including diffusion transformer fine-tuning, vision transformer adaptation, and language model adaptation. Our method demonstrates superior or competitive performance compared to both existing orthogonal and non-orthogonal methods.

</details>


### [109] [Entropy-Based Characterisation of the Polarised Regime in Latent Variable Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15965)
*Peter Clapham,Lisa Bonheme,Marek Grzes*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于均值表示熵的通用信息论准则，用于识别变分自编码器（VAE）中的潜变量极化状态，并论证了所谓的“维度塌陷”实际上是尺度问题，被动维度在特定条件下仍保有信息价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有识别VAE主动维度的方法通常依赖于高斯先验，适用范围受限。研究者希望通过更通用的信息论视角，探究VAE潜空间中主动、被动及混合维度的极化机制，并厘清“维度塌陷”的深层含义。

Method: 提出了一种基于均值表示熵的信息论分类方法来识别极化状态，通过熵-方差界将其与KL最小化耦合，并结合方差表示信号对主动/被动维度进行分类。在多种模型（β-VAE、可辨识VAE等）上进行了实证评估。

Result: 实证结果表明，该熵准则能够一致地在多种变分模型中识别出极化现象。研究发现被动维度并非完全无用，通过合适的归一化处理，它们仍能对下游任务产生微小但显著的提升。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了VAE中潜变量极化现象的本质，提出基于均值表示熵的分类标准，并指出“塌陷”（collapse）更多是尺度问题而非信息彻底丢失，被动维度在适当归一化后仍具备潜在的下游任务价值。

Abstract: Variational Autoencoders (VAEs) often exhibit a polarised regime in which latent variables separate into active, passive, and mixed subsets. Existing criteria for identifying active dimensions depend on a Gaussian prior, limiting their applicability to variational models and specific priors. We propose a simple information-theoretic classification of the polarised regime based on the entropy of the mean representation. We show theoretically how this entropy couples to KL minimisation through entropy--variance bounds, and we relate the resulting criterion to Bonheme's active/passive conditions. We also clarify a key limitation: entropy of the mean alone cannot reliably distinguish active from mixed dimensions without additional signals from the variance representation. Empirically, we evaluate the entropy criterion on $β$-VAEs, identifiable VAEs, Least-Volume Autoencoders, and L2-regularised autoencoders, and find that it consistently recovers a polarised regime when such a regime is present across the model classes studied. Finally, we show that passive dimensions can yield small but consistent improvements on downstream tasks when latent codes are appropriately normalised, suggesting that collapse is often a matter of scale rather than absolute information removal.

Method: 提出了一种名为 CT-AGD（曲率调节加速梯度下降）的通用加速框架。该方法利用有限差分商显式捕获目标函数的局部曲率信息，并引入了针对随机小批量（mini-batch）训练中噪声和偏差的启发式调节策略，从而加速一阶梯度下降法的收敛过程。

Conclusion: CT-AGD 是一种高效的优化算法，能够通过捕捉局部曲率信息，在保持与主流一阶优化器相似的计算成本下，显著提升深度学习模型的训练速度，且无需牺牲模型精度。

Abstract: In this paper, we present CT-AGD (Curvature-Tuned Accelerated Gradient Descent), an optimization method for non-convex optimization problems in deep learning training tasks. CT-AGD is a general boosting procedure that accelerates first-order methods by explicitly capturing the local curvature using finite-difference quotients, and the development of heuristics aimed at mitigating noise and bias introduced by stochastic mini-batch training. CT-AGD has a comparable storage and computational overhead as adaptive gradient methods such as Adam. Our extensive experiments demonstrate that CT-AGD achieves the same level of accuracy as the baseline first-order methods, yet reduces the required training epochs by 33% on average.

### [111] [Mind Dreamer: Untethering Imagination via Active Latent Intervention on Latent Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16030)
*Shaojun Xu,Xiaoling Zhou,Yihan Lin,Yapeng Meng,Xinglong Ji,Luping Shi,Rong Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Mind Dreamer (MD) 是一种新型 MBRL 框架，通过对抗性生成的“潜在跳跃”取代传统基于历史的初始化，配合中继值函数实现跨空间断裂的价值与不确定性传播，从而在复杂稀疏奖励任务中显著提升了学习效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于模型强化学习 (MBRL) 存在“历史绑定”问题，即想象过程通常从观测到的状态开始初始化，导致世界模型对环境流形的发现速度远超策略在稀疏奖励下的优化速度，从而限制了采样效率。

Method: 1. 提出主动潜在干预 (ALI)：放弃从历史回放缓存中采样初始状态，改用对抗性生成器 $p_{gen}(\cdot)$ 直接合成非连续的潜在“跳跃”至认知盲区。
2. 定义中继自由能 (R-EFE)：通过最小化该指标引导发现过程，而非仅仅依赖马尔可夫连续性。
3. 构建中继值函数 (RVF) 与中继不确定性函数 (RUF)：通过修正后的 Bellman 方程处理空间断裂处的信度分配问题，并引入二次折扣因子 $\gamma^2$ 解决非连续状态下的不确定性传播。

Result: 在 DeepMind Control Suite 基准测试中，Mind Dreamer 的平均采样效率比 DreamerV3 提升了 1.67 倍，在稀疏奖励任务中效率提升高达 8.8 倍。理论上，该方法能有效扩大流形的谱间隙，减少到达关键瓶颈状态的命中时间。

Conclusion: Mind Dreamer (MD) 通过引入主动潜在干预和中继值函数，成功打破了传统 MBRL 依赖历史轨迹初始化的限制。该框架不仅从理论上证明了在潜在空间非连续跳跃中引入二次折扣因子 $\gamma^2$ 的必要性，还通过实验验证了其在复杂稀疏奖励环境下的高效采样能力，为探索未知状态空间提供了全新的范式。

Abstract: Model-Based Reinforcement Learning (MBRL) leverages latent imagination for sample efficiency, yet remains constrained by Historical Tethering: imagination is typically initialized from observed states. This creates a learning asymmetry, where the world model's manifold discovery outpaces the policy's sparse-reward optimization. We propose Mind Dreamer (MD), a framework that operationalizes Active Latent Intervention (ALI) to transcend Markovian continuity. MD reformulates discovery as the minimization of a global Relay Manifold Expected Free Energy (R-EFE); by sampling initial states from a learned generator $s_0 \sim p_{gen}(\cdot)$ rather than the historical buffer, MD utilizes an adversarial generator to synthesize non-continuous latent jumps to epistemic blind spots that are physically plausible yet cognitively challenging. To resolve the credit assignment paradox across these spatial ruptures, we derive the Relay Value Function (RVF) and Relay Uncertainty Function (RUF). These potentials treat synthesized anchors as counterfactual intermediary states, propagating pragmatic and epistemic value through a principled Bellman-style formulation. Notably, we prove that uncertainty propagation across discontinuities necessitates a quadratic discount $γ^2$, establishing a formal epistemic horizon. Theoretically, MD approximates a variance-minimizing importance sampler that expands the manifold's spectral gap, reducing the hitting time to critical bottleneck states. Empirically, MD achieves a 1.67$\times$ average speedup over DreamerV3 on DeepMind Control Suite, reaching 8.8$\times$ in sparse-reward tasks.

In this paper, we propose a unified framework that explicitly incorporates latent dynamic inference into generative decision-making from minimal yet sufficient observations. We theoretically show that under mild conditions, the latent process can be identified from small temporal blocks of observations. Result: 在 MoleculeNet 的九个基准数据集上进行了测试，MolCHG 在七个数据集上取得了最优性能，在其余任务中也保持了与最强基准模型相当的竞争力。消融实验证实了各层级监督信号的互补性及各组件的贡献。

By introducing a bond graph that operates in parallel with the atom graph, our architecture elevates bond-level information to independently evolving node representations, enabling fragment nodes to aggregate atom-level and bond-level semantics on an equal footing. We design three level-specific pretraining objectives: an atom-bond cross-view contrastive task that aligns the atom-view and bond-view representations within each fragment, a fragment-level functional group prediction task to inject domain-relevant chemical knowledge, and graph-level structure prediction tasks to encode global molecular topology. Experiments on nine MoleculeNet benchmarks demonstrate that MolCHG achieves the best performance on seven datasets across both classification and regression tasks, remaining competitive with the strongest baselines on the rest. ### [116] [ITGPT: Generative Pretraining on Irregular Timeseries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16069)
*Antoine Honoré,Ming Xiao*

TL;DR: ITGPT 是一种新型的 Transformer 架构，无需预处理（如插补或重采样）即可直接从大规模、不规则采样的多模态时间序列中学习，并通过自监督预训练有效解决了数据标注稀缺的问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为 ITGPT 的注意力机制架构，能够直接处理多模态、不规则采样的时间序列。该模型通过结合自监督学习（SSL）和生成式预训练（GPT）目标，在无需重采样、特征融合或显式数据插补的情况下，实现对原始数据的直接建模。

Result: 在 TIHM（医疗）和 CompX（预测性维护）数据集上的实验结果表明，ITGPT 达到了同类方法的最佳性能（SOTA）。此外，该模型在标签稀缺的情况下，通过利用未标注数据进行预训练，显著优于传统的纯监督学习方法。

Conclusion: ITGPT 成功证明了利用大规模未标注多模态时间序列数据进行自监督预训练的有效性，为处理医疗和工业领域中具有挑战性的不规则采样数据提供了强大的通用框架，无需繁琐的预处理步骤。

Abstract: Timeseries regression models often struggle to leverage large volumes of labeled multimodal data, particularly when the data are irregularly sampled or contain missing values. This is common in domains like healthcare and predictive maintenance, where data are collected from unreliable sources, and labeling requires expert knowledge or costly equipments. Transformer-based large language models have proven effective on structured data such as text through self-supervised learning (SSL) and generative pretraining (GPT) frameworks. However, such models lack the flexibility to efficiently process irregularly sampled multimodal timeseries data. In this paper, we introduce ITGPT, an attention-based architecture designed for handling multimodal, irregularly sampled timeseries by allowing training with both SSL losses and GPT-like objectives. We evaluate its performance on a healthcare task with the TIHM dataset, and a predictive maintenance task with the CompX dataset. Our results demonstrate that ITGPT achieves state-of-the-art performance without requiring resampling, feature fusion or explicit data imputation. Furthermore, when labels are scarce, ITGPT effectively leverages unlabeled data through SSL and GPT training, outperforming the purely supervised approach. This represents an important step towards efficiently using large and unstructured timeseries datasets for practical inference tasks.

### [117] [Federated Imputation under Heterogeneous Feature Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16099)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为 FedHF-Impute 的联邦补全框架。该方法区分了结构性特征缺失与一般的随机缺失，构建了一个共享的全局特征图，利用消息传递机制（Message Passing）在统计相关的特征之间进行信息传播，从而实现跨客户端的间接知识迁移。

Result: 在 SECOM 和 AirQuality 数据集上，FedHF-Impute 的补全准确率（RMSE）相比现有联邦学习基准分别提升了 26.9% 和 8.4%；在 PhysioNET 数据集上，其表现与最佳基准相当，仅有 0.3% 的微小差异。

Conclusion: FedHF-Impute 通过引入全局特征图和消息传递机制，成功解决了联邦学习中异构特征空间导致的知识共享受限问题，为处理具有部分重叠特征的联邦数据补全任务提供了一种高效且隐私保护的解决方案。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative training across decentralized clients, but most methods assume aligned feature schemas, an assumption that rarely holds in tabular settings where clients observe only partially overlapping feature subsets. In these heterogeneous feature spaces, parameter-averaging methods (e.g., FedAvg) transfer little information across weakly overlapping or disjoint feature groups, limiting their effectiveness for federated imputation. To overcome this, we propose \textbf{FedHF-Impute}, a federated imputation framework that separates structural feature unavailability from conventional missingness and uses a shared global feature graph to propagate information across statistically related features through message passing. This enables indirect cross-client knowledge transfer, even when features are never jointly observed locally, while preserving standard federated communication. Under simulated partial schema overlap on the SECOM and AirQuality datasets, FedHF-Impute improves imputation accuracy (RMSE) over FL baselines by 26.9\%, and 8.4\% respectively, while achieving comparable performance on PhysioNET, with only a 0.3\% difference relative to the best baseline.

### [118] [MIND: Decoupling Model-Induced Label Noise via Latent Manifold Disentanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16081)
*Dayong Ren*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了MIND框架，通过动态聚类解耦模型诱导的系统性标签噪声，解决了基础模型自动标注中误差与特征流形耦合的难题，有效提升了模型鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在使用预训练专家模型或基础模型进行自动标注时，会引入非随机的“模型诱导标签噪声”。这种噪声源于标注模型的归纳偏见，与局部特征流形紧密耦合。现有的基于全局转移矩阵的方法无法拟合这种结构化错误，而实例级矩阵的学习在数学上又难以实现。

Method: 提出了“模型诱导噪声解耦”（MIND）框架，利用“潜在流形解耦”（Latent Manifold Disentanglement）技术，将高维噪声流形拆解为可处理的子空间相关成分。核心组件“潜在解耦估计器”（LDE）将样本动态投影到具有一致误差模式的潜在结构聚类中，无需真实标签锚点即可实现噪声识别。

Result: 在CIFAR-100（受控噪声）及大规模真实世界3D数据集（S3DIS、ScanNet）上进行了分层评估。实验结果表明，MIND显著超越了现有的先进方法，并能有效纠正视觉-语言模型（如OpenSeg）产生的零样本幻觉。

Conclusion: MIND提供了一个稳健的蒸馏框架，通过解耦模型诱导的噪声，解决了基础模型自动标注中的系统性偏见问题，在复杂基准测试中展现了优于现有SOTA方法的效果，特别是在处理视觉-语言模型的零样本幻觉方面表现出色。

Abstract: The paradigm of learning from automatic annotations driven by pre-trained experts and Foundation Models dominates data-hungry applications. However, it introduces a critical challenge: model-induced label noise. Unlike stochastic noise in classical robust learning, this noise stems from annotator inductive biases, manifesting as systematic errors tightly coupled with local feature manifolds. Existing methods relying on global transition matrices underfit these structural patterns, while learning instance-specific matrices remains mathematically intractable. We propose Model-Induced Noise Decoupling (MIND), a theoretically grounded framework addressing this dilemma. We demonstrate that the high-dimensional noise manifold can be decoupled into tractable, subspace-dependent components via Latent Manifold Disentanglement. Specifically, our Latent Decoupling Estimator (LDE) dynamically projects samples into latent structural clusters with consistent error modes, facilitating noise identifiability without ground-truth anchor points. To rigorously evaluate robustness, we adopt a hierarchical protocol: moving from controlled noise on CIFAR-100 to a structural stress test on large-scale real-world 3D datasets (S3DIS, ScanNet), where error patterns explicitly couple with geometric manifolds. Empirically, MIND significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods on these complex benchmarks and effectively corrects zero-shot hallucinations from Vision-Language Models (e.g., OpenSeg), highlighting its potential as a robust distillation framework for Foundation Models.

### [119] [Attention Dispersion in Dynamic Graph Transformers: Diagnosis and a Transferable Fix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16112)
*Jinhao Zhang,Kangfei Zhao,Qiuhao Zeng,Long-Kai Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本论文针对动态图Transformer在时间分布偏移下注意力分散导致预测性能下降的问题，提出了“差异化注意力（Differential Attention）”机制，通过抑制共性噪音并聚焦关键节点，显著提升了模型在动态图学习任务中的表现，并推出了性能达到SOTA的DiffDyG架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于Transformer的连续时间动态图（CTDG）学习方法在面临数据时间分布偏移（Temporal Distribution Shift）时性能显著下降。研究旨在揭示这种性能衰退背后的深层原因，即“注意力分散（Attention Dispersion）”现象，并寻求一种有效的解决途径以提升模型在分布偏移下的鲁棒性。

Method: 1. 诊断分析：通过对比实验发现模型在面对时间偏移时，无法有效聚焦于携带预测信号的关键节点，导致注意力过于分散。
2. 核心改进：提出将“差异化注意力（Differential Attention）”机制引入Transformer架构，通过差分计算削弱无关的共性信息，突出对关键信息的关注。
3. 模型实现：开发了DiffDyG架构，将该机制应用于现有的各类动态图Transformer基准模型中进行验证。

Result: 1. 差异化注意力机制在三个代表性CTDG基准模型中均能一致提升性能，尤其是在高偏移数据集上增益显著。
2. 实验证明该方法显著降低了注意力熵，并增强了模型对关键节点的注意力权重。
3. 提出的DiffDyG在9个基准测试和三种负采样协议下均达到了SOTA（当前最佳）性能。

Conclusion: 本研究通过诊断发现动态图Transformer在时间分布偏移下存在“注意力分散”的问题，并提出引入“差异化注意力（Differential Attention）”机制。该机制通过抑制共性信号并放大关键节点信号，有效提升了模型在时间分布偏移场景下的鲁棒性和预测准确性，为动态图学习提供了一种通用且高效的优化策略。

Abstract: Transformer-based architectures have become the dominant paradigm for Continuous-Time Dynamic Graph (CTDG) learning, yet their performance remains limited on temporally shifted datasets. In this work, we identify attention dispersion as a shared failure mode of dynamic graph Transformers under temporal distribution shift. Through controlled ablation contrasting structurally and temporally distinguished historical neighbors against random ones, we show that prediction depends on a class of critical nodes that carry consistently more predictive signal than arbitrary neighbors. However, existing Transformers fail to focus on these nodes even when they are present in the input, as temporal shift weakens attention contrast and produces overly dispersed attention distributions. This diagnosis suggests a simple and transferable fix: replace standard attention with differential attention, which suppresses common-mode attention and amplifies distinctive token-level signals. When added to three representative CTDG Transformer baselines, differential attention consistently improves performance, with gains concentrated on high-shift datasets. Attention-level measurements further confirm the mechanism, showing reduced attention entropy and increased attention mass on critical nodes. Building on these findings, we introduce DiffDyG, a reference implementation combining differential attention with standard input encodings. Across 9 benchmarks and three negative sampling protocols, DiffDyG achieves SOTA performance, with especially large gains on the most shifted datasets.

### [120] [Entropy Across the Bridge: Conditional-Marginal Discretization for Flow and Schrödinger Samplers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16126)
*Bruno Trentini,Dejan Stancevic,Michael M. Bronstein,Alexander Tong,Luca Ambrogioni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于熵率的训练后时间调度策略，通过优化采样器在低推理预算下的时间步分配，显著提升了流模型和生成式桥模型的采样质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在小推理预算（NFE）下，生成模型的采样质量高度依赖于采样器函数评估点（网格）的选取。现有的流匹配和薛定谔桥方法通常依赖启发式或从扩散模型继承的网格，缺乏对路径几何形状的深入考量，导致效率低下。

Method: 提出了一种基于条件-边缘熵率（conditional-marginal entropy-rate）的推理时调度方法。该方法通过将端点条件的桥几何结构与边缘流演化分离，从第一性原理推导出一个无需额外训练的离散化目标。对于高斯布朗桥，该目标具有闭式解且呈 U 型，从而引导生成边界加权（boundary-heavy）的非均匀时间网格。

Result: 在多种任务中表现优异：在 2D 模型上，相比线性网格，ODE-Heun 和 SDE-Heun 的 MMD 指标分别提升了 18.1% 和 22.7%；在 CIFAR-10 上，实现了最优的 5 步 FID 分数；在 AlphaFlow 蛋白质生成任务中，在低 NFE 机制下也展现了明显的性能优势。

Conclusion: 熵率调度（entropy-rate scheduling）为各种流模型和扩散模型在低推理预算（低 NFE）下提供了有效的离散化策略，通过优化时间步长分配，显著提升了采样质量，且具备通用性和即插即用的特性。

Abstract: For a fixed flow-based generative model under a small inference budget, sample quality can depend strongly on where the sampler spends its few function evaluations. Flow matching and Schrödinger bridges define probability paths, yet their inference grids are usually heuristic or inherited from one-endpoint diffusion. We derive a conditional-marginal entropy-rate objective for bridge-aware discretization, separating endpoint-conditioned bridge geometry from marginal flow evolution, and use it to build a training-free entropic inference-time scheduler from first principles. For Gaussian Brownian bridges this rate is closed-form and U-shaped, motivating boundary-heavy nonuniform grids. On trained two-dimensional bridge/flow models, the estimated profile recovers the predicted shape and improves 10-step ODE-Heun MMD over linear by 18.1%, with a paired 22.7% SDE-Heun improvement in the same low-NFE sweep. On EDM/CIFAR-10, the entropic time-discretization gives the best tested five-step FID (186.3 \pm 4.0 versus 200.5 \pm 2.9 for linear and 238.0 \pm 5.3 for cosine). On AlphaFlow protein generation, entropic conditional-marginal (cond-marg) scheduling shows advantage in low-NFE regimes on both CAMEO22 and ATLAS benchmarks. These results support entropy-rate scheduling as a practical low-budget allocation signal for high-dimensional bridge and flow samplers.
