### [121] [Entropic Auto-Encoding via Implicit Free-Energy Minimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16164)
*Hazhir Aliahmadi,Irina Babayan,Greg van Anders*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了熵自动编码器（EAE），通过将先验隐式化并引入编码器集成来解决VAE中的后验崩溃问题，从而实现了更高质量、更具结构信息的潜表示学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分自动编码器（VAE）在训练过程中经常面临“后验崩溃”（posterior collapse）问题，即解码器会忽略潜变量，导致潜表示失去信息量。这主要是由于VAE中强制施加的显式先验引导优化过程陷入了无信息的损失平原区域。作者旨在寻找一种能够避免该问题并学习到高质量、多模态潜表示的新范式。

Method: 提出了一种名为“熵自动编码器”（EAE）的新框架。该方法剔除了VAE中显式的先验损失，仅保留重构损失。通过使用一个最小化自由能的编码器集成（ensemble），利用熵隐式地生成潜变量的先验，并通过编码器集成与解码器的相互作用，引导模型搜索高信息量的潜空间表示。

Result: 实验证明，EAE成功缓解了后验崩溃，能够学习到非高斯且具有多模态特征的潜分布。在反应-扩散过程、MNIST数字分类以及CelebA人脸数据集上的实验结果表明，EAE能够生成数据一致且多样化的结果，并能有效提取数据中潜在的层次化结构和分类特征。

Conclusion: 通过引入熵自动编码器（EAE），本文证明了通过隐式生成先验而非显式强加先验，可以有效解决变分自动编码器（VAE）中的后验崩溃问题。EAE框架学习到的非高斯、多模态潜空间能够更好地捕捉复杂数据结构。

Abstract: Despite their ubiquity, variational autoencoders (VAEs) inherently suffer from posterior collapse, a failure mode in which latent variables are effectively ignored. This failure arises because explicit prior imposition drives optimization toward loss landscape regions corresponding to uninformative latent representations. Here, we introduce Entropic Autoencoders (EAEs), a framework in which reconstruction loss is the only explicit objective, and entropy generates the latent variables' prior implicitly through a free energy-minimizing ensemble of encoders. This ensemble biases learning toward high-volume regions of near-optimal solutions, while decoder updates direct the search trajectories toward informative latent representations. We demonstrate that EAEs mitigate posterior collapse by learning non-Gaussian, multimodal latent distributions that yield diverse, data-consistent generations and preserve different forms of underlying structure in the data. As a proof-of-concept, we show that an EAE captures a superposition of the known low-dimensional dynamics of a reaction-diffusion process. Then, we show that an EAE identifies implicit categorical distinctions in MNIST latent representations, and displays a hierarchical understanding of facial structure on the CelebA dataset, from an "all-human" face to individual-dependent features.

### [122] [BAPR: Bayesian amnesic piecewise-robust reinforcement learning for non-stationary continuous control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16170)
*Yifan Zhang,Liang Zheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对分段平稳环境下的鲁棒控制难题，论文提出了BAPR框架，通过结合贝叶斯变化检测与鲁棒强化学习，实现了性能与安全性的动态平衡，并通过Lean 4证明了其数学稳定性和错误边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界的控制系统往往表现为“分段平稳”特性，即系统在经历突发体制转换前会长时间保持稳定。现有的鲁棒强化学习方法难以平衡“全局保守（导致稳定期性能浪费）”与“局部适应（导致体制切换时产生灾难性失效）”之间的矛盾。

Method: 提出了一种名为BAPR（贝叶斯遗忘分段鲁棒SAC）的算法。该方法结合了贝叶斯在线变化检测（BOCD）与鲁棒集成强化学习。通过冻结信念分布对模式条件下的贝尔曼算子进行凸组合，实现了自适应的保守策略，并在策略训练中引入了上下文调节模块以实现模式感知，同时利用Lean 4定理证明器对算法的收缩性及错误边界进行了全量形式化验证。

Result: BAPR在理论上证明了其算子是γ-收缩的，并给出了明确的错误边界。通过Lean 4完成了1145行、22个定理的无错误形式化验证。实验表明，该方法能在检测到变化后迅速调整为最保守策略，并随着置信度提升平滑恢复，检测延迟仅为O(log(1/δ))，无需在部署时提供模式标签。

Conclusion: BAPR通过结合贝叶斯在线变化检测与鲁棒强化学习，成功解决了分段平稳环境下性能与鲁棒性之间的权衡问题。通过Lean 4形式化验证，确保了算子的收缩性质及错误边界，为非平稳动态控制提供了一种既能快速适应变化，又能在未知 regime 转换时保持安全性的可靠框架。

Abstract: Real-world control systems frequently operate under \emph{piecewise stationary} conditions, where dynamics remain stable for extended periods before undergoing abrupt regime changes. Standard robust RL methods face a fundamental dilemma: a globally conservative policy wastes performance during stable periods, while a locally adaptive policy risks catastrophic failure when the regime changes undetected.
  We propose \textbf{BAPR} (Bayesian Amnesic Piecewise-Robust SAC), which unifies Bayesian Online Change Detection (BOCD) with robust ensemble RL. The BAPR operator -- a convex combination of mode-conditional Bellman operators weighted by a frozen belief distribution -- is a $γ$-contraction. A complementary counterexample, machine-verified in Lean~4, establishes a \emph{sharp boundary}: when beliefs depend on the Q-function, the contraction factor becomes $γ+ λΔ$ (where $Δ$ is the mode reward gap), and contraction fails exactly when $γ+ λΔ\geq 1$. We derive a \emph{component-wise} formal error budget for the abstract operator -- every component machine-verified -- bounding post-switch recovery; the budget applies to the abstract mode-mixture operator and inherits to the implemented shared-critic algorithm only through the frozen-parameter design intuition. All results are formally verified with no \texttt{sorry} (1,145 lines across 3 Lean~4 files, 22 machine-verified theorems). BOCD drives an adaptive conservatism mechanism: the policy becomes maximally conservative after detected change-points and smoothly relaxes as confidence grows, with detection delay $O(\log(1/δ))$. A context-conditioning module trained via RMDM loss provides mode-aware representations from simulator-provided mode IDs at training time and requires no mode labels at deployment.

</details>

We find that the TabPFN-based approach consistently outperforms these classical baselines, supporting its use as a strong clinician-behavior baseline for pediatric ECMO decision support.

### [124] [Hypothesis-driven construction of mesoscopic dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16211)
*Zhuoyuan Li,Aiqing Zhu,Qianxiao Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于广义昂萨格原理的学习介观动力学通用框架，通过在假设空间施加物理约束，实现了复杂系统动力学模型的高效学习，并提供了严格的数学保证与物理可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统科学建模依赖于针对特定实例的固定有效方程，在处理复杂多尺度系统时面临严峻挑战。研究旨在通过学习介观动力学并施加物理数学约束，克服传统方法在复杂系统建模中的局限性。

Method: 提出了一种在数学约束假设空间内学习介观动力学的方法。利用广义昂萨格原理构建统一框架，涵盖耗散型与保守型动力学。在学习前建立统一的先验理论保证（全局适定性、渐近稳定性、唯一分解可辨识性及离散能量耗散），并利用特定实例数据进行模型识别。

Result: 通过连续PDE模型验证了该框架的准确性，并在未知精确介观模型的微观链模型中展示了其有效性。该方法不仅实现了精确、稳健的动力学建模，还为揭示潜在物理机制提供了可解释的诊断手段。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于广义昂萨格原理的介观动力学学习范式，证明了在该假设空间内构建的模型具有全局适定性、稳定性及物理一致性，为复杂系统建模提供了一种可解释且稳健的通用框架。

Abstract: Traditional scientific modeling typically begins with fixed, instance-wise effective equations and then carries out equation-specific analysis and computation, a procedure that becomes exceptionally challenging in complex applications such as multiscale systems. We propose an alternative paradigm by learning mesoscopic dynamics within a mathematically constrained hypothesis class. Building upon a generalized Onsager principle, we introduce a unified framework encompassing both dissipative and conservative mesoscopic dynamics. We establish uniform and a priori theoretical guarantees, including global well-posedness, asymptotic stability, unique factorization identifiability, and discrete energy dissipation, applicable to all spatio-temporal evolution equations within this hypothesis class prior to all learning stages. Data from each problem instance is then used to guide the identification of members within our hypothesis class, giving rise to accurate, robust and interpretable dynamical models. We empirically validate this framework on both data from continuum PDE models as a check, and on data arising from microscopic chain models for which exact meso-scale models are unknown. The proposed approach not only acts as an effective dynamics learner, but also offers vital interpretable diagnostics of the underlying physics.

### [125] [The Privacy Price of Tail-Risk Learning: Effective Tail Sample Size in Differentially Private CVaR Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16219)
*El Mustapha Mansouri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了差分隐私CVaR学习的本质：其学习难度由“有效尾部样本量”(nτ)决定，而非总样本量n；隐私开销与 $1/(εnτ)$ 成正比，为该领域的复杂度和算法设计提供了理论基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究在差分隐私约束下，针对尾部风险（CVaR）进行学习时的样本复杂度和隐私开销，解决在处理长尾分布时由于有效样本量减少而带来的隐私与效用权衡问题。

Method: 研究通过将CVaR的超额风险分解为普通尾部风险统计误差与隐私价格，利用标量估计、有限假设空间以及凸Lipschitz学习的上下界缩减方法，推导了在纯DP（及部分近似DP）下的精确收敛率。

Result: 得出CVaR学习的隐私代价项随 1/(εnτ) 缩放。对于标量估计和有限类假设，给出了精确的极小极大收敛率，并证明了CVaR学习的本质难点在于针对 $Θ(nτ)$ 个尾部数据进行普通隐私学习。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了差分隐私（DP）下CVaR学习的基本难度特征，即“有效尾部样本量”（nτ）是决定隐私开销和统计误差的核心指标，证明了在给定尾部概率τ时，CVaR学习的隐私代价与其密切相关。

Abstract: Differential privacy changes the effective sample size governing CVaR learning. For tail mass $τ$, the privacy-relevant sample size is not $n$, but $nτ$; equivalently, the effective private tail sample size is $εnτ$. Private CVaR excess risk decomposes into ordinary tail-risk statistical error and a privacy price. This decomposition is complete for scalar estimation and finite classes: scalar estimation has rate $Θ(B \min\{1,(nτ)^{-1/2}+(εnτ)^{-1}\})$, and finite classes of size $M$ have rate $Θ(B \min\{1,\sqrt{\log(2M)/(nτ)}+\log(2M)/(εnτ)\})$. These complete rates hold under pure DP, and their lower bounds extend to approximate DP in the stated small-$δ$ regimes. For convex Lipschitz learning, modular upper and lower reductions show that the CVaR-specific privacy term necessarily scales as $1/(εnτ)$, with dimension dependence inherited from private stochastic convex optimization. Together, these results identify ordinary private learning on $Θ(nτ)$ informative tail records as the canonical hard subproblem inside private CVaR learning.

</details>


### [126] [Dynamics-Level Watermarking of Flow Matching Models with Random Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16239)
*Shuchan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种直接在流匹配模型的“速度场”中嵌入水印的创新方法，通过密钥控制动力学扰动，实现了生成质量与水印鲁棒性之间的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的水印技术多依赖于修改模型权重或输出像素，容易受到模型微调、剪枝或后处理的攻击。为了提高水印的鲁棒性和隐蔽性，研究者希望开发一种从动力学层面切入的新型水印机制。

Method: 研究者利用流匹配（Flow Matching）模型，将水印直接嵌入其学习到的连续动力学（速度场）中。具体方法是通过在训练过程中引入一个由密钥控制的扰动（随机编码），并构建一个连续通道，使得水印信息能够通过黑盒查询在检测阶段被恢复，同时确保该扰动不会改变生成样本的分布。

Result: 在MNIST和CIFAR-10数据集上的实验证明，该方法实现了可靠的信息恢复，且对生成图像的质量没有负面影响；此外，在没有密钥的情况下，解码准确率处于随机水平，验证了其安全性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种将水印嵌入生成模型动力学层面的创新方案。通过证明在保持生成质量的同时将信息编码至速度场的可行性，该研究为生成式模型的水印技术提供了一个抗鲁棒性强且隐蔽性高的新方向。

Abstract: We introduce a dynamics-level approach to watermarking generative models. Rather than embedding signals into model weights or outputs, we embed the watermark directly into the learned continuous dynamics -- the velocity field of a flow matching model. We formulate this as random coding over a continuous channel: a key-dependent perturbation is added during training, and the message is recovered at detection time from black-box queries. The perturbation is designed to leave the generated distribution unchanged. Experiments on MNIST and CIFAR-10 across different architectures confirm reliable message recovery, preserved generation quality, and chance-level decoding accuracy without the secret key.

</details>

### [127] [Agent4POI: Agentic Context-Conditioned Affordance Reasoning for Multimodal Point-of-Interest Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15203)
*Jinze Wang,Yangchen Zeng,Tiehua Zhang,Lu Zhang,Yuze Liu,Yongchao Liu,Xingjun Ma,Zhu Sun*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Agent4POI 是一种创新的 POI 推荐框架，它放弃了传统的静态嵌入，通过基于 LLM 的智能体在推理时实时生成“上下文相关”的动态表征，从而显著提升了在复杂多变环境下的推荐准确性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态 POI 推荐系统普遍依赖静态的 POI 嵌入，无法捕捉同一地点在不同上下文（如周一工作 vs 周五聚会）下所呈现的差异化功能（可供性）。研究人员从数学上证明了静态编码器无法满足上下文敏感的排序需求，因此提出了一种在推理时根据上下文生成动态表征的框架。

Method: 1. 构建了一个包含四个阶段的 LLM 智能体：第一阶段生成动态、上下文相关的可供性查询；第二阶段执行基于图像、评论和元数据的跨模态思维链（CoT）；第三阶段生成结构化、具有不确定性感知能力的表征；第四阶段通过语义缓存系统将表征与用户偏好对齐，以实现低延迟排序。
2. 摒弃了传统的静态 POI 嵌入，改为在推理时动态生成表征。

Result: 在三个 POI 基准测试及三种评估配置（标准、冷启动、上下文漂移）中，Agent4POI 相比最强基线实现了 23.2% 的相对提升；在上下文漂移场景下，性能下降幅度仅为 7.5%（基线为 16-17%）；在冷启动场景下，性能比最佳内容驱动基线提升了 2.4 倍。

Conclusion: Agent4POI 证明了在推荐系统中，基于上下文的动态表示优于预计算的静态嵌入。通过引入吉布森的“可供性理论”，该框架实现了更具情境感知能力的 POI 推荐，特别是在处理上下文漂移和冷启动问题时展现出显著优势。

Abstract: We introduce Agent4POI, the first POI recommendation framework that generates context-conditioned multimodal representations at recommendation time, rather than relying on static POI embeddings pre-computed independently of context. Existing multimodal systems encode each POI once as a static embedding, a design that precludes reasoning about why the same cafe affords solo work on Monday but group celebration on Friday evening. We formally prove that no pre-computed encoder can satisfy context-sensitive ranking under standard bilinear scoring, motivating inference-time item-side representation. Agent4POI inverts this computation: given a situational context, a four-phase LLM agent generates dynamic, context-specific affordance queries (Phase 1) and executes a five-step cross-modal chain-of-thought over image, review, and metadata evidence (Phase 2). The resulting uncertainty-aware affordance representation is grounded in Gibsonian affordance theory. These cross-modal verdicts form a structured, uncertainty-adjusted affordance representation (Phase 3), which is aligned with user preferences via a semantic caching system for low-latency ranking (Phase 4). On three POI benchmarks and three evaluation configurations (standard, cold-start, context-shift), Agent4POI achieves a 23.2% relative gain over the strongest baseline and degrades by only 7.5% under context-shift versus 16--17\% for the strongest baselines. In cold-start scenarios, Agent4POI outperforms the best content-based baseline by up to 2.4x, whereas ID-based methods fail to generalize.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了一个基于健康饮食指数（HEI）的检索增强生成（RAG）框架。该方法利用NHANES和FPED数据库构建食品嵌入空间，计算基准HEI得分。系统通过检索候选食品，估算替换或增加特定食物对HEI的影响，并利用受限的RAG流水线（结合预训练的OpenAI大模型）生成基于营养特征和HEI贡献的个性化建议。

Abstract: Diet quality is a leading determinant of chronic disease risk. Advances in artificial intelligence (AI) have enabled food recommendation systems to adapt suggestions to user preferences and health goals. However, most current systems rely on loosely curated food databases and provide limited connection to a validated index. In this study, we propose a Healthy Eating Index (HEI) informed retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) framework that combines standardized nutrition databases with large language models (LLMs) for personalized food recommendations. Our proposed method anchors retrieval in the National Health and Nutrition Examination Survey (NHANES) and the Food Patterns Equivalents Database (FPED). A food-level embedding space is constructed from FPED-derived textual descriptions. For each entity, the system computes baseline HEI scores, retrieves candidate foods for intake recommendations, and estimates the HEI impact of simple substitutions or additions. A constrained RAG pipeline instantiated with a pretrained OpenAI LLM generates personalized recommendations and sources based on nutrient profiles and HEI contributions. The simulation results showed a mean HEI improvement of 6.45, with the proportion of users HEI over 50 increasing from 45.12 to 61.26. Quantile analysis revealed consistent improved shifts across the HEI distribution. Our findings suggest that the proposed LLM-RAG-based AI systems can support more precise, explainable, and personalized nutrition guidance to improve diet quality.

### [129] [Fortress: A Case Study in Stabilizing Search Recommendations via Temporal Data Augmentation and Feature Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15299)
*Milind Pandurang Jagre,Jia Huang,Dayvid V. R. Oliveira,Zhinan Cheng,Babak Seyed Aghazadeh,Puja Das,Chris Alvino,Jinda Han,Kailash Thiyagarajan*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Fortress 是一个旨在增强搜索与推荐模型时间稳定性的通用框架，通过识别并剔除会导致模型输出分数剧烈波动的特征，在保持预测准确性的同时，显著提升了系统的鲁棒性和决策一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 搜索与推荐系统中的预测模型常因特定输入特征（如 engagement 类特征）引起输出分数的时间波动，导致系统的不稳定性。这种不稳定性在多阶段系统中会影响决策的一致性，从而降低用户体验。因此，需要一种能够识别并修剪这些不稳定特征的通用框架。

Method: Fortress 框架遵循四个核心步骤：1) 收集模型的历史预测快照；2) 基于历史数据识别导致预测分数波动的样本；3) 通过特征重要性与波动性分析，分离并剔除引起不稳定的特征；4) 使用筛选后的稳定特征子集重新训练模型。该方法旨在在保留 engagement 信号预测能力的同时，抑制其带来的时间波动。

Result: 在大型应用商店的 query-to-app 相关性模型实验中，Fortress 框架显著提升了预测稳定性（变异系数降低）及分类性能（PR-AUC 提升），有效平衡了语义特征与 engagement 特征之间的权衡。

Conclusion: Fortress 框架通过一种系统的特征修剪方法，成功解决了搜索与推荐系统中由于高波动性特征导致的预测不稳定性问题。该方法有效平衡了模型的预测准确性与 temporal 稳定性，在大型应用商店的实验中证明了其在实际工业场景下的实用价值。

Abstract: In search and recommendation systems, predictive models often suffer from temporal instability when certain input features introduce volatility in output scores. This instability can degrade model reliability and user experience especially in multi-stage systems where consistent predictions are critical for downstream decision making. We introduce Fortress, a general framework for enhancing model stability and accuracy by identifying and pruning features that contribute to inconsistent prediction scores over time. Fortress leverages historical snapshots temporally partitioned datasets capturing score fluctuations for the same entity across periods and follows a four-step process: (1) collect historical snapshots, (2) identify samples with unstable predictions, (3) isolate and remove instability-inducing features, and (4) retrain models using only stable features. While semantic features from LLMs and BERT-based models improve generalization, they often lack full query or entity coverage. Engagement-based features offer strong predictive power but tend to introduce temporal instability. Fortress mitigates this trade-off by suppressing the volatility of engagement signals while retaining their predictive value leading to more stable and accurate models. We validate Fortress on a query-to-app relevance model in a large-scale app marketplace. Offline experiments demonstrate notable improvements in prediction stability (measured by Coefficient of Variation) and classification performance (measured by PR-AUC).

</details>


### [130] [Jobs' AI Exposure Should Be Measured from Evidence, Not Model Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15474)
*Luca Mouchel,Pierre Bouquet,Yossi Sheffi*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文批判了当前仅凭大语言模型主观判断评估AI就业影响的方法，提出了一种基于外部证据检索（RAG）的评估框架，以确保AI能力测量的科学性、透明度和可追踪性，从而更好地服务于政策制定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的AI就业暴露度评估方法多依赖大语言模型的零样本推理，缺乏透明的证据链和外部验证，导致其在指导政策制定、资金流向及劳动力规划时存在可靠性风险。研究旨在建立更严谨、更具可解释性的评估标准。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于检索增强生成（RAG）的框架，对O*NET 30.2中的18,796个“职业-任务”对进行评估。该方法利用开源推理模型，结合实时检索到的新闻报道和学术论文摘要作为外部证据，对AI的接触程度进行标注，并将其与传统的零样本（Zero-shot）提示法进行了对比验证。

Result: 相比于传统的零样本基准，该研究提出的证据驱动方法在超过72%的意见不一致案例中表现更优，且评估结果与现实世界中AI的实际应用情况吻合度更高。数据验证了基于证据的测量比单纯模型预测更能准确捕捉AI的实际功能。

Conclusion: 研究强调，衡量人工智能对就业影响的指标不应仅依赖大语言模型的“先验假设”，而必须具备可重复性、外部证据基础和可审查性。随着AI能力的快速演进，基于证据的测量方法能够更准确地反映实际工作任务的AI替代或辅助潜力，政策制定者应将其作为动态工具而非静态真理使用。

Abstract: This position paper argues that job exposure to AI should be measured with grounded, evidence-based methods, not inferred from LLM priors alone. Current theoretical exposure measures use zero-shot prompting to classify task-level AI exposure, generating labels with no explicit evidence, no transparent chain of reasoning, and no external validation. The stakes of these measurements are too high to rely on such methods, as they influence policy making, where public and private funds are directed, and how workers understand their future prospects. We therefore argue that AI capability claims should meet three standards: reproducibility, external grounding, and inspectability. We propose a retrieval-augmented framework that assigns AI exposure labels to all 18,796 occupation--task pairs in O*NET 30.2, using open-weight reasoning and instruct models with retrieved news articles and academic paper abstracts as evidence of current AI capabilities. Relative to a zero-shot baseline, the grounded condition is preferred in over 72\% of disagreement cases under both automatic and human evaluation, and yields scores that align more closely with observed real-world AI usage. Taken together, these findings suggest that evidence-grounded measurement better captures what current AI systems can plausibly do in practice, rather than what a model asserts without external evidence. Because AI capabilities continue to change, the measurements used to inform policy must evolve with them: theoretical AI exposure scores should be periodically reassessed, not inherited as immutable ground truth.

</details>


### [131] [Generative Long-term User Interest Modeling for Click-Through Rate Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15905)
*Jiangli Shao,Kaifu Zheng,Hao Fang,Huimu Ye,Zhiwei Liu,Bo Zhang,Shu Han,Xingxing Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对现有CTR预测模型在处理长序列行为时效率低、兴趣捕获不全的问题，GenLI 通过引入生成式兴趣建模和O(1)复杂度的行为检索，在提升兴趣特征的多样性与完整性的同时，大幅优化了系统的运行效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的两阶段点击率 (CTR) 预测模型（GSU+ESU）存在两个主要缺陷：一是目标中心型的检索方式容易忽略用户的潜在兴趣，导致特征不完整且存在偏差；二是随着历史行为增长，基于配对相似度评分的检索机制计算耗时严重，且未能有效捕捉行为间的关联信息。

Method: 提出了一种生成式长期用户兴趣模型 GenLI，包含三个模块：1. 兴趣生成模块 (IGM)：通过生成多个与目标无关的兴趣分布，整合行为间的交互信息，捕获多样化的用户兴趣；2. 行为检索模块 (BRM)：使用简单的查找操作替代复杂的匹配计算，将时间复杂度降至 O(1)；3. 兴趣融合模块 (IFM)：利用门控机制整合生成的信息，输出最终兴趣特征。

Result: GenLI 能够有效捕获更全面、多样的用户兴趣，同时通过简化检索过程，避免了复杂的配对计算，显著提高了模型在处理海量长序列行为时的在线预测效率。

Conclusion: GenLI 通过将检索过程从传统的基于目标的匹配转向生成式建模，不仅提升了用户兴趣表达的完整性和多样性，还通过简化检索机制显著提升了在线推理的效率，实现了CTR预测在准确性和计算性能之间的良好平衡。

Abstract: Modeling long-term user interests with massive historical user behaviors enhances click-through rate (CTR) prediction performance in advertising and recommendation systems. Typically, a two-stage framework is widely adopted, where a general search unit (GSU) first retrieves top-$k$ relevant behaviors towards the target item, and an exact search unit (ESU) generates interest features via tailored attention. However, current target-centered GSU would ignore other latent user interests, leading to incomplete and biased interest features. Additionally, the matching-based retrieval process in GSUs depends on the pairwise similarity score between target item and each historical behavior, which not only becomes time-consuming for online services as user behaviors continue to grow, but also overlooks the interaction information among user behaviors. To combat these problems, we propose a \textbf{Gen}erative \textbf{L}ong-term user \textbf{I}nterest model named GenLI for CTR prediction. GenLI consists of an interest generation module (IGM), a behavior retrieval module (BRM), and an interest fusion module (IFM). The IGM generates multiple interest distributions to indicate different aspects of real-time user interests, which is target-independent and incorporates interaction information among behaviors, ensuring complete and diverse interest features. The BRM selects related behaviors via a simple lookup operation, reducing the time complexity for weighting each behavior to $O(1)$. Finally, the IFM uses delicate gating mechanisms to generate interest features. Based on the generation process, GenLI improves the diversity of user interests and avoids complex matching-based behavioral retrieval, achieving a better balance between accuracy and efficiency for CTR prediction.

</details>


### [132] [Ascend-RaBitQ: Heterogeneous NPU-CPU Acceleration of Billion-Scale Similarity Search with 1-bit Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16007)
*Fujun He,Chuyue Ye,Huaxiang Cai,Zetao Lv,Baolong Cui,Wenru Yan,Chao Zhan,Zigang Zhang,Hao Yi,Jie Xiang,Xiabing Li,Yuhang Gai,Ziyang Zhang,Pengfei Zheng,Yunfei Du*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Ascend-RaBitQ 是一款针对 NPU 架构优化的十亿级向量搜索系统，通过将粗排序与细排序解耦并分配至 NPU 和 CPU 进行协同计算，成功克服了传统架构下的性能与精度瓶颈，实现了显著的吞吐量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统 CPU 在处理十亿级向量检索时存在计算开销大和内存带宽受限的瓶颈。尽管 NPU 提供更高计算密度，但现有的 1-bit 量化算法（如 RaBitQ）在 NPU 架构上存在硬件不匹配问题，且单一的计算范式难以同时兼顾搜索精度、内存占用与性能。

Method: 提出了一种异构计算流水线，将向量搜索分为三个阶段：1. 利用 NPU 的 AI Core 加速基于 1-bit 量化的粗排序；2. 利用 NPU 的 AI CPU 进行 Top-k 处理；3. 利用主机 CPU 进行全精度向量的细粒度重排序。同时引入了四项 NPU 原生优化：融合算子（AIC-AIV）、计算流重构、细粒度负载均衡以及 AI Core 与 AI CPU 之间的流水线并行。

Result: 实验表明，Ascend-RaBitQ 在构建索引速度上比 CPU 基准快 3.0 到 62.8 倍，吞吐量比最快的 CPU 实现提升了 4.6 倍，比数学等效的 CPU 基准提升了超过 100 倍，并表现出良好的多 NPU 分布式扩展性。

Conclusion: Ascend-RaBitQ 成功证明了通过软硬件协同设计的异构计算架构，可以有效打破在大规模向量搜索中精度、内存和性能之间的权衡。该研究为在 NPU 等专用加速器上部署高效向量检索系统提供了可行的工程范式。

Abstract: Vector similarity search is a critical component of modern AI systems, but traditional CPU-based implementations face fundamental scalability bottlenecks for billion-scale corpora due to prohibitive computational overhead and memory bandwidth limitations. While Neural Processing Units (NPUs) offer orders-of-magnitude higher compute density, existing CPU/GPU-optimized 1-bit RaBitQ quantization implementations cannot be directly ported to NPU architectures due to fundamental hardware mismatches, and homogeneous design paradigms struggle to simultaneously balance accuracy, memory footprint, and performance. This paper presents Ascend-RaBitQ, the first heterogeneous NPU-CPU optimized IVF-RaBitQ system for billion-scale vector search, built on the core insight that decoupling coarse ranking (NPU) from fine ranking (CPU) allows each stage to leverage its optimal hardware, breaking the long-standing accuracy-memory-performance trade-off. We propose a three-stage heterogeneous pipeline comprising AI Core-accelerated coarse ranking on 1-bit quantized vectors, on-device AI CPU Top-k processing, and host CPU fine re-ranking on full-precision vectors. We introduce four NPU architecture-native optimizations: fused AIC-AIV operators for parallel distance computation, computation flow restructuring to exploit rotation orthogonality, fine-grained index block-level load balancing that breaks query boundaries, and intra-NPU pipeline parallelism between AI Core and AI CPU to mask Top-k latency. Evaluation on standard datasets shows that Ascend-RaBitQ achieves 3.0* to 62.8* faster index construction than the CPU baseline, up to 4.6* throughput improvement over the fastest CPU IVF-RaBitQ implementation, and over 100* over the mathematically equivalent CPU baseline, while demonstrating encouraging scalability on distributed multi-NPU systems.

</details>


### [133] [MERVIN: A Unified Framework for Multimodal Event Retrieval in Vietnamese News Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16120)
*Anh-Tai Pham-Nguyen,Tung-Duong Le-Duc,Anh-Duy Le,Trung-Hieu Truong-Le*

TL;DR: MERVIN 是一个针对越南语新闻视频的多模态检索框架，通过 Gemini 1.5 Flash 优化文本质量并整合视觉特征，实现了高效的语义检索，并在权威竞赛中验证了其卓越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着在线视频平台的快速发展，现有的视频检索系统在面对越南语新闻视频时，常受到语音识别噪声、多模态语义对齐不足等问题的困扰，因此急需一套能够有效整合文本、图像及视频总结的语义检索框架。

Method: MERVIN 采用统一的多模态处理流程：使用 Gemini 1.5 Flash 对语音识别文本进行降噪优化；利用 Perception Encoder 提取视觉特征；结合越南语语言模型生成文本嵌入；使用 Milvus 数据库进行高效索引；并配备基于 React 的交互式界面以支持用户进行跨模态查询细化。

Result: MERVIN 在 AI Challenge HCMC 2025 资格赛中获得 79/88 分，并在决赛阶段成功检索到所有查询的预期结果，表现优异。

Conclusion: MERVIN 框架通过整合多模态数据并利用先进的 AI 模型，显著提升了越南语新闻视频的语义检索能力，证明了该方法在处理复杂多模态数据时的有效性与实用性。

Abstract: The growth of online video platforms drives the need for effective, semantically grounded event retrieval. We present MERVIN, a unified multimodal framework for Vietnamese news videos that integrates keyframes, transcripts, and video summaries. Transcript quality is enhanced via Gemini 1.5 Flash, reducing noise from accents, background sounds, and recognition errors. Visual features are extracted with Perception Encoder, while a Vietnamese language model produces textual embeddings; both are indexed in Milvus for efficient similarity-based retrieval. In addition, a React-based interface enables iterative query refinement across modalities, improving semantic alignment. Experimental results on Vietnamese news videos demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed system, with MERVIN achieving 79 out of 88 points in AI Challenge HCMC 2025 qualification phase and successfully retrieved all results for every query in the final round.

### [134] [Does Theory of Mind Improvement Really Benefit Human-AI Interactions? Empirical Findings from Interactive Evaluations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15205)
*Nanxu Gong,Zixin Chen,Haotian Li,Zishu Zhao,Jianxun Lian,Huamin Qu,Yanjie Fu,Xing Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出当前LLM的ToM评估存在局限，提出了新的交互式评估范式，发现静态基准测试的表现并不能有效预测模型在真实动态人机交互中的实际社会认知能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM理论心智（ToM）评估通常基于静态的第三方叙事多选题，忽略了真实人机交互（HAI）中动态、第一人称且开放式的特点，导致评估结果与模型在实际应用中的表现存在脱节。

Method: 提出了一个新的交互式ToM评估范式，该范式通过视角转换（从第三人称转向第一人称）和指标转换（从多选题转向开放式评估）来模拟真实的人机交互。研究对比了四种代表性的ToM增强技术，并在四个真实世界数据集及用户研究中进行了系统性测试。

Result: 研究发现，在传统静态基准测试中表现优异的模型，并不一定能在动态的人机交互场景中表现出更好的ToM能力。评估结果显示，静态基准测试与实际交互表现之间存在明显的鸿沟。

Conclusion: 现有的静态理论心智（ToM）基准测试无法完全衡量LLM在动态交互中的表现。研究强调了转向基于交互的评估范式的必要性，这对于开发具备社会意识的下一代AI系统至关重要。

Abstract: Improving the Theory of Mind (ToM) capability of Large Language Models (LLMs) is crucial for effective social interactions between these AI models and humans. However, the existing benchmarks often measure ToM capability improvement through story-reading, multiple-choice questions from a third-person perspective, while ignoring the first-person, dynamic, and open-ended nature of human-AI (HAI) interactions. To directly examine how ToM improvement techniques benefit HAI interactions, we first proposed the new paradigm of interactive ToM evaluation with both perspective and metric shifts. Next, following the paradigm, we conducted a systematic study of four representative ToM enhancement techniques using both four real-world datasets and a user study, covering both goal-oriented tasks (e.g., coding, math) and experience-oriented tasks (e.g., counseling). Our findings reveal that improvements on static benchmarks do not always translate to better performance in dynamic HAI interactions. This paper offers critical insights into ToM evaluation, showing the necessity of interaction-based assessments in developing next-generation, socially aware LLMs for HAI symbiosis.

### [135] [SkillSmith: Compiling Agent Skills into Boundary-Guided Runtime Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15215)
*Duling Xu,Zheng Chen,Zaifeng Pan,Jiawei Guan,Dong Dong,Jialin Li,Bangzheng Pu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillSmith 是一种针对 LLM 智能体的优化框架，通过离线编译将技能转化为精简的可执行接口，消除了冗余的上下文注入和重复推理，在大幅降低成本和延迟的同时提升了执行效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大语言模型的智能体系统通常将技能作为上下文直接注入推理循环，这导致了两个主要问题：一是引入了大量无关的上下文信息，二是造成了重复的技能特定推理与规划，严重影响了系统的执行效率和资源开销。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SkillSmith 的“边界优先”编译-运行时框架。该框架在离线阶段将技能包编译为最小化的可执行接口，通过提取细粒度的操作边界，实现运行时仅按需加载和执行相关组件，从而减少无效的上下文注入。此外，该框架支持模型间的“编译产物复用”，允许较弱的运行时模型使用由强模型编译出的接口。

Result: 在 SkillsBench 基准测试中，与原始技能执行方式相比，SkillSmith 将求解阶段的 Token 使用量减少了 57.44%，推理迭代次数减少了 42.99%，求解时间缩短了 50.57%（速度提升 2.02 倍），且显著降低了 Token 成本。同时，该框架支持模型间的产物复用，在原始技能理解失效的情况下提升了任务准确率。

Conclusion: SkillSmith 通过引入“边界优先”的编译优化框架，成功解决了大模型智能体在执行技能时存在的上下文冗余和重复推理问题，证明了通过离线编译实现技能精简与接口标准化是提升智能体执行效率和降低成本的有效路径。

Abstract: Recently, skills have been widely adopted in large language model (LLM)-based agent systems across various domains. In existing frameworks, skills are typically injected into the agent reasoning loop as contextual guidance once matched to a runtime task, enabling specialized task-solving capabilities. We find that this execution paradigm introduces two major sources of redundancy: irrelevant context injection and repeated skill-specific reasoning and planning. To this end, we propose SkillSmith, a boundary-first compiler-runtime framework that compiles skill packages offline into minimal executable interfaces. By extracting fine-grained operational boundaries from skills, SkillSmith enables agents to dynamically access and execute only the relevant components at runtime, thereby minimizing unnecessary context injection and redundant reasoning overhead. In the evaluation on SkillsBench benchmark, SkillSmith reduces solve-stage token usage by 57.44%, thinking iterations by 42.99%, solve time by 50.57% (2.02x faster), and token-proportional monetary cost by 57.44% compared with using raw-skills. Moreover, compiled artifacts produced by a stronger model can be reused by a smaller or more efficient runtime model, improving task accuracy in cases where raw skill interpretation fails. The source code and data are available at https://github.com/AetherHeart-AI/Aeloon.

</details>


### [136] [Fair outputs, Biased Internals: Causal Potency and Asymmetry of Latent Bias in LLMs for High-Stakes Decisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15217)
*Jagdish Tripathy,Marcus Buckmann*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究揭示了指令微调模型在“公平输出”下的欺骗性：模型内部深层仍隐藏并放大了种族偏见。这种潜伏偏差可以通过干预被轻易触发，导致决策失衡，因此单纯的输出端审计对于高风险决策场景是不够的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究人员注意到指令微调模型虽然在输出端表现出行为上的公平，但在内部表征中仍保留偏见。研究动机旨在探讨这些被抑制的表征是否会影响模型决策，以及这种因果影响力在不同人口统计学群体间是否具有不对称性。

Method: 研究采用匹配申请（仅姓名种族关联不同）进行抵押贷款承销测试，并结合激活转向（Activation Steering）与创新的跨层干预技术，分析模型内部层级对决策的影响，探究潜在偏差的因果效力及非对称性。

Result: 研究发现模型尽管表现出公平的输出，但内部层级仍保留并放大了种族表征。通过干预，这些潜伏偏见可被重新激活并导致决策逆转。该偏见具有不对称性（对特定群体影响大），且易受提示词工程和微调的干扰。

Conclusion: 仅依靠模型输出的审计不足以评估其公平性，因为模型可能隐藏了潜在的偏见。未来的 AI 治理需要建立结合输出评估与内部表征分析的“双层测试框架”，以应对高风险决策中的隐蔽歧视。

Abstract: Instruction-tuned language models exhibit behavioural fairness in high-stakes decisions while retaining biased associations in their internal representations. However, whether these suppressed representations can affect model outputs - and whether such causal potency is symmetric across demographic groups - remains unknown. We investigate the use of open-weight models for mortgage underwriting using matched applications that differ only in racially-associated names and reveal a critical disconnect: models show no output-level bias, yet retain and amplify demographic representations across model layers. Through activation steering and novel cross-layer interventions, we demonstrate that this suppressed information is decision-relevant: when reinjected at critical layers, it produces near-complete decision reversals. Critically, this latent bias is asymmetric - steering interventions affect decisions in one demographic direction, while producing minimal effects in reverse - and susceptible to adversarial prompt engineering and parameter-efficient fine-tuning. These findings demonstrate that behavioural audits focused on outputs are insufficient: fair outputs can mask exploitable internal biases. They also motivate dual-layer testing frameworks combining output evaluation with representational analysis for AI governance in high-stakes decisions.

</details>


### [137] [NOVA: Fundamental Limits of Knowledge Discovery Through AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15219)
*Salman Avestimehr,Ken Duffy,Muriel Médard*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出NOVA框架，揭示了AI自主发现知识时面临的污染陷阱与成本激增问题，并证明了人类专家在AI探索边界处的关键辅助作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究AI系统通过迭代自我改进是否能发现真正的创新知识，并分析这一过程中潜在的成本、失败模式（如污染、遗忘等）以及系统性的局限性。

Method: 本文采用了理论建模与数学推导的方法，将“生成-验证-积累-重训”循环建模为知识空间上的自适应采样过程，并引入Zipf定律（指数α>1）来量化生成成本的缩放规律。

Result: 研究提出了NOVA框架，识别了导致知识发现失败的四种模式；证明了在不完善的验证机制下，错误知识会加速污染知识库；推导出了发现D个知识点的累积成本缩放律 R_cum(D)=Θ(c_gen*D^α)，揭示了知识发现过程中的收益递减效应。

Conclusion: 本文构建的NOVA框架表明，AI系统的自主知识发现面临严重的“污染陷阱”和边际效应递减规律。随着简单知识被耗尽，维持知识库准确性的难度急剧增加，因此人类专家的介入在突破自主探索瓶颈时具有不可替代的价值。

Abstract: Can AI systems discover genuinely new knowledge through iterative self improvement, and if so, at what cost? We introduce the NOVA framework, which models the common ``generate, verify, accumulate, retrain'' loop as an adaptive sampling process over a knowledge space. We identify sufficient conditions under which accumulated genuine knowledge eventually covers a finite domain, and show how their violations produce distinct failure modes: contamination, forgetting, exploration failure, and acceptance failure. We then analyze imperfect verification and identify a contamination trap: as easy-to-find knowledge is exhausted, the model mass assigned to new valid artifacts shrinks, so even small false-positive rates can cause invalid artifacts to enter the knowledge base faster than genuine discoveries. We clarify that Good--Turing estimation is a local batch-diversity diagnostic, not an estimator of the historically undiscovered valid mass that governs long-term discovery. Under a separate tail-equivalence assumption relating the model's effective discovery distribution to a Zipf law with exponent $α>1$, we prove that the cumulative generation cost required to obtain $D$ distinct genuine discoveries satisfies $R_{\mathrm{cum}}(D)=Θ(c_{\mathrm{gen}}D^α)$, where $c_{\mathrm{gen}}$ is the per-candidate generation cost. This scaling law quantifies asymptotic diminishing returns as the discovery frontier advances. Finally, we formalize human amplification through guidance, generation, and verification, explaining why expert input is most valuable near autonomous exploration barriers.

</details>


### [138] [ICRL: Learning to Internalize Self-Critique with Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15224)
*Jianbo Lin,Xiaomin Yu,Yi Xin,Yifu Guo,Zhuosong Jiang,Zhongqi Yue,Weishi Wang,Heqing Zou,Chengwei Qin,Hui Xiong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ICRL 是一种新型强化学习框架，通过联合训练求解器和批判者，使大模型能够将外部批判转化为自身的内化能力，在无需外部提示的情况下实现推理性能的自主提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大语言模型的智能体在缺乏外部批判时容易重复犯错，说明模型未能真正“内化”批判性指导；同时，固定的 Critic 无法随时间迭代提升反馈质量，限制了模型自我改进的潜力。

Method: 提出了 ICRL（Learning to Internalize Self-Critique with Reinforcement Learning）框架：1. 基于共享骨干模型联合训练 Solver（求解器）和 Critic（批判者）；2. Critic 通过奖励机制学习提供可操作的反馈；3. 引入分布校准重加权比率以解决从“批判条件”到“无批判”状态的分布偏移；4. 采用角色分组优势估计（Role-wise Group Advantage Estimation）以稳定联合优化过程。

Result: 在智能体和数学推理任务的基准测试中，基于 Qwen3-4B/8B 的 ICRL 表现优异。相比 GRPO 基准，在智能体任务上平均提升 6.4 个百分点，数学推理任务上提升 7.0 个百分点。此外，该训练出的 8B Critic 在性能上可与 32B 的 Critic 相媲美，且显著降低了推理开销。

Conclusion: ICRL 框架成功证明了通过联合训练 Solver 和 Critic，模型能够将批判性反馈内化，从而实现无需外部辅助的自我改进。该方法不仅减少了对外部批判的依赖，还通过角色分组优势估计等技术提升了训练稳定性，在保持计算效率的同时显著增强了模型在复杂推理任务中的性能。

Abstract: Large language model-based agents make mistakes, yet critique can often guide the same model toward correct behavior. However, when critique is removed, the model may fail again on the same query, indicating that it has not internalized the critique's guidance into its underlying capability. Meanwhile, a frozen critic cannot improve its feedback quality over time, limiting the potential for iterative self-improvement. To address this, we propose learning to internalize self-critique with reinforcement learning(ICRL), a novel framework that jointly trains a solver and a critic from a shared backbone to convert critique-induced success into unassisted solver ability. The critic is rewarded based on the solver's subsequent performance gain, incentivizing actionable feedback. To address the distribution shift between critique-conditioned and critique-free behavior, ICRL introduces a distribution-calibration re-weighting ratio that selectively transfers critique-guided improvements compatible with the solver's own prompt distribution. Additionally, a role-wise group advantage estimation stabilizes joint optimization across the two roles. Together, these mechanisms ensure that the solver learns to improve itself without external critique, rather than becoming dependent on critique-conditioned behavior. We evaluate ICRL on diverse benchmarks spanning agentic and mathematical reasoning tasks, using Qwen3-4B and Qwen3-8B as backbones. Results show consistent improvements, with average gains of 6.4 points over GRPO on agentic tasks, and 7.0 points on mathematical reasoning. Notably, the learned 8B critic is comparable to 32B critics while using substantially fewer tokens. The code is available at https://github.com/brick-pid/ICRL.

</details>

### [140] [Zero-Shot Goal Recognition with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15333)

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文首次系统评估了大语言模型在目标识别任务中的表现，发现其能力差异不仅源于领域知识，更取决于模型在面对证据积累时进行逻辑推断和一致性评估的实质性整合能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文对前沿大语言模型在经典的PDDL（规划领域定义语言）基准测试上进行了首次系统性的零样本（zero-shot）目标识别评估。研究通过分析模型在不同观察证据量下的推理轨迹，评估其识别准确度与证据整合方式。

Result: 研究发现LLM在目标识别上的能力参差不齐。部分模型能够随着证据量的增加而提升准确率，接近基于地标（landmark）的专家算法；而另一些模型则无论证据如何增加，始终受限于预训练的世界知识先验。定性分析表明，这种差异根源于模型对证据整合机制的不同，而非对领域知识的熟悉程度。

Conclusion: 目标识别任务是评估大语言模型（LLM）规划能力的理想基准。LLM在处理此类任务时，其表现不仅取决于领域知识，更依赖于其对观测证据的整合能力。未来的研究应聚焦于提升模型在证据积累过程中的逻辑推断与一致性评估能力，而非仅仅依赖预训练的先验知识。

Abstract: Large language models have recently reached near-parity with classical planners on well-known planning domains, yet this competence relies on world-knowledge exploitation rather than genuine symbolic reasoning. Goal recognition is a complementary abductive task structurally better suited to LLM strengths: it consists of evaluating consistency with world knowledge rather than generating novel action sequences. This paper provides the first systematic zero-shot evaluation of frontier LLMs as goal recognisers on key classical PDDL benchmarks. Our results show that LLM competence on goal recognition is uneven: some models scale with evidence and approach landmark-based accuracy at full observations, while others remain anchored to world-knowledge priors regardless of how much evidence accumulates. Qualitative analysis of model reasoning traces reveals that this divergence reflects a fundamental difference in evidence integration rather than domain familiarity. These findings position goal recognition as a principled benchmark for the foundational planning knowledge of LLMs.

### [141] [Belief Engine: Configurable and Inspectable Stance Dynamics in Multi-Agent LLM Deliberation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15343)
*Joshua C. Yang,Maurice Flechtner,Damian Dailisan,Michiel A. Bakker*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了“信念引擎”（BE），这是一个为大语言模型智能体设计的可审计信念更新层，通过将立场变化量化为基于证据和锚定的更新过程，解决了现有模型在审议模拟中立场变化原因不明的“黑箱”问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前基于大语言模型的智能体常用于模拟谈判、冲突解决等审议互动，但其产生的对话记录往往无法揭示立场变化的深层原因（如是基于证据更新、锚定效应、角色漂移还是提示词影响）。缺乏这种可解释性限制了对智能体决策逻辑的深入研究。

Method: 该研究引入了一个名为“信念引擎”（Belief Engine, BE）的可审计信念更新层。该方法将信念视为命题上的证据状态，并将其表示为标量立场。具体做法包括：1. 将论点提取为结构化记忆；2. 使用受证据摄取（u）和先验锚定（a）控制的对数几率规则（log-odds rule）来更新立场；3. 对多个基础大模型进行参数扫描，以验证该控制机制在保持证据更新轨迹的同时塑造立场动态的能力。

Result: 在人类审议数据集DEBATE上的测试表明，BE能够有效地重建那些立场随提取证据而变化的参与者过程。对于立场稳定或与证据背道而驰的情况，该引擎也能识别出锚定效应或其他外部因素的影响。相比于隐式的提示词效应，BE提供了一种可配置的基础设施来量化开放性、承诺、收敛和分歧等审议行为。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的“信念引擎”（BE）为研究大语言模型智能体在审议过程中的立场变化提供了可解释的框架。它表明，通过将信念建模为结构化的证据更新过程，研究人员可以更有效地解构智能体立场转变的内在机理，从而区分是基于证据的理性变化还是由提示词或锚定效应引起的非理性波动。

Abstract: LLM-based agents are increasingly used to simulate deliberative interactions such as negotiation, conflict resolution, and multi-turn opinion exchange. Yet generated transcripts often do not reveal why an agent's stance changes: movement may reflect evidence uptake, anchoring, role drift, echoing, or changed prompt and retrieval context. We introduce the Belief Engine (BE), an auditable belief-update layer that treats "belief" as an evidential state over a proposition and exposes it as scalar stance. BE extracts arguments into structured memory and updates stance with a log-odds rule controlled by evidence uptake u and prior anchoring a. Across multiple base LLMs, parameter sweeps show that these controls reliably shape stance dynamics while preserving an evidence-level update trail. On DEBATE, a human deliberation dataset with pre/post opinions, BE best reconstructs participants whose final stance follows extracted evidence; stable and evidence-opposed cases instead point to anchoring or factors outside the extracted evidence stream. BE provides configurable infrastructure for studying evidence-grounded deliberation, where openness, commitment, convergence, and disagreement can be tied to explicit update assumptions rather than hidden prompt effects.

### [142] [Ensemble Monitoring for AI Control: Diverse Signals Outweigh More Compute](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15377)
*Eugene Koran,Yejun Yun,Samantha Tetef,Benjamin Arnav,Pablo Bernabeu-Pérez*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究人员构建了12个基于GPT-4.1-Mini的监控模型，采用了提示工程（prompting）和微调（fine-tuning）两种策略，并在通过标准测试但面对对抗性输入时会失败的编码任务上进行了评估。通过计算不同模型组合的性能，分析模型多样性、个体性能和相关性对检测能力的影响。

Result: 研究发现，多样化的集成模型显著优于个体监控模型和同质集成模型。最优的3模型集成方案比同质模型组合性能提升了2.4倍。此外，包含微调模型的集成系统表现最佳，且在分布外攻击类型中保持了稳定性，证明微调能带来提示工程无法企及的检测能力。

Conclusion: 多样性而非单纯的规模扩大是提升AI智能体监控性能的关键。通过组合低相关性、高质量（特别是包含微调）的监控模型，构建集成系统是一种在合理推理成本下实现有效AI安全管控的实用策略。

Abstract: As AI systems are increasingly deployed in autonomous agentic settings at scale, it is important to ensure the actions they take are safe and aligned with user intent. Monitoring agent actions is a key safety mechanism, yet reliable monitors remain difficult to build and the scale of these systems makes human oversight impractical. We show that combining signals from diverse monitors into an ensemble improves detection of misaligned actions. We build 12 GPT-4.1-Mini monitors using both prompting and fine-tuning strategies. We evaluate them on coding tasks where candidate solutions pass standard tests but fail on adversarial inputs. In this setting, diverse ensembles outperform both individual monitors and homogeneous ensembles. Our best 3-monitor ensemble achieves 2.4x greater detection performance gain compared to an ensemble composed of three identical monitors, with the same ensemble performing strongly on an independent dataset. We contend that these results show that diversity - not scale - drives gains. The best ensembles combine strong individual performance with low correlation between monitors. Furthermore, fine-tuned monitors appear in every top-performing ensemble and maintain this advantage on out-of-distribution attack types, suggesting that fine-tuning enables detection capabilities that prompting alone does not elicit. These results support ensemble monitoring as a practical AI control strategy for safety gains at reasonable inference costs.

### [143] [From LLM-Generated Conjectures to Lean Formalizations: Automated Polynomial Inequality Proving via Sum-of-Squares Certificates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15445)
*Ruobing Zuo,Hanrui Zhao,Gaolei He,Zhengfeng Yang,Jianlin Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NSPI 是一种神经符号框架，通过“LLM 提出猜想 + 符号计算精炼 + Lean 形式化验证”的三段式流程，有效解决了大规模多项式不等式自动证明中的扩展性难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纯符号方法在处理变量增多或次数增加的多项式不等式时，面临计算复杂度过高和扩展性差的问题；现有 LLM 方法虽在小型不等式上表现出色，但在处理更具挑战性的复杂问题时仍存在局限性，需要一种兼具启发式搜索效率与符号计算确定性的方法。

Method: 提出了一种神经符号框架 NSPI：首先利用大语言模型（LLM）生成多项式平方和（SOS）分解的近似猜想；随后通过符号计算对该猜想进行精炼，将其转化为精确的 SOS 表示以证明不等式；最后在 Lean 交互式定理证明器中进行证明的机器校验。

Result: 实验结果表明，NSPI 能够有效处理多达 10 个变量的复杂多项式不等式证明任务，展现了优于单一方法的高效性和更好的扩展性。

Conclusion: NSPI 通过结合 LLM 的启发式搜索能力与符号计算的严谨性，成功构建了一个端到端的自动化多项式不等式证明流水线，不仅提升了处理复杂问题的规模，还通过 Lean 提供了形式化验证保证。

Abstract: Automated proving of polynomial inequalities is a fundamental challenge in automated mathematical reasoning, where rich algebraic structure and a rapidly growing certificate search space hinder scalability. Purely symbolic approaches provide strong guarantees but often scale poorly as the number of variables or the degree increases, due to expensive algebraic manipulations and rapidly growing intermediate expressions. In parallel, LLM-guided methods have made notable progress, particularly on competition-style inequalities with a small number of variables. To address the remaining scalability challenges, we propose NSPI, a neuro-symbolic framework that combines the complementary strengths of LLMs and symbolic computation for polynomial-inequality proving. Concretely, an LLM proposes a conjecture in the form of an approximate polynomial Sum-Of-Squares (SOS) decomposition; we refine it via symbolic computation to obtain an exact polynomial SOS representation, which directly proves the target inequality, and we further certify the proof in Lean, yielding an end-to-end pipeline from heuristic discovery to machine-checked proof. Experiments on challenging benchmarks involving polynomials with up to 10 variables demonstrate the effectiveness and scalability of the proposed method.

### [144] [CAPS: Cascaded Adaptive Pairwise Selection for Efficient Parallel Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15513)
*Fangzhou Lin,Shuo Xing,Peiran Li,Siyuan Yang,Qianwen Ge,Kazunori Yamada,Ziming Zhang,Haichong Zhang,Zhengzhong Tu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CAPS 是一种新型推理框架，通过动态分配验证计算资源（根据证据需求和比较优先级），在显著降低验证成本的同时，提升了多候选解生成中的最佳答案筛选准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的并行推理验证方法（如全量配对验证）存在极高的计算成本，且无论候选解质量如何均消耗相同的资源。研究旨在解决如何在大规模推理中高效分配验证计算预算的问题，以实现更经济、更高效的解选择。

Method: 提出 CAPS（级联自适应配对选择）框架，该方法主要包含两个维度的计算优化：一是“证据轴”，即根据验证难度动态调整模型读取候选解的程度（部分或全部）；二是“分布轴”，即自适应地分配比较次数。在此基础上构建了四阶段级联流程，通过关闭无信息增量的比较来降低验证成本。

Result: 在四种模型和五个数学/编程基准测试中，CAPS 在 14 个测试集上优于现有的领先配对验证方法，且在代码任务中仅使用了原计算预算的 25.4%，同时在所有 20 个测试集上均表现优于点对点（pointwise）自我验证。

Conclusion: CAPS 通过引入基于证据深度和比较分布的非均匀计算分配机制，证明了在大规模语言模型推理阶段，无需全量读取候选解即可实现高效的自我验证，从而显著提升了测试时缩放（test-time scaling）的效率与经济性。

Abstract: Parallel reasoning, where a generator samples many candidate solutions and an aggregator selects the best, is one of the most effective forms of test-time scaling in large language models, and pairwise self-verification has become its strongest aggregation primitive. Yet pairwise verification carries a heavy cost: each judgment reads two complete solutions in full, and existing methods perform tens of such judgments per problem regardless of whether the comparison is informative. We introduce CAPS (Cascaded Adaptive Pairwise Selection), an inference-only framework that allocates verifier compute non-uniformly along two orthogonal axes: an evidence axis that adapts how much of each candidate the judge sees, and a distribution axis that adapts how comparisons are spread across the pool. CAPS instantiates these into a four-stage cascade with an optional rescue subroutine, and admits a closed-form verifier-token cost in which the per-candidate marginal cost is roughly halved relative to uniform full-evidence schedules. On four self-verifying models (Qwen3-14B, GPT-OSS-20B, Qwen3-4B-Instruct/Thinking) and five reasoning benchmarks spanning code (LiveCodeBench-v5/v6, CodeContests) and math (AIME 2025, HMMT 2025), CAPS outperforms the leading pairwise verifier on 14 of 20 suites while using 25.4% of its verifier-token budget on code, and outperforms pointwise self-verification on all 20. The trade-off suites admit an interpretable diagnostic in terms of the verifier's accuracy at partial versus full evidence, providing a concrete pre-deployment check for cascade suitability.

Abstract: This paper introduces RTL-BenchMT, an agentic framework for dynamically maintaining RTL generation benchmarks. However, current RTL benchmarks face two critical challenges: (1) flawed cases in the benchmarks and (2) overfitting to the benchmarks. Both challenges are difficult to resolve purely by manual engineering effort. To address these issues and systematically reduce human maintenance costs, we propose an automated agentic framework, RTL-BenchMT. RTL-BenchMT focuses on two key applications: (1) automatically identifying and revising flawed benchmark cases and (2) automatically detecting and updating overfitting cases. With the assistance of RTL-BenchMT, we conduct a thorough, in-depth analysis of flawed and overfitting cases and produce a refined benchmark suite that will be open-sourced to the community.

### [146] [DRS-GUI: Dynamic Region Search for Training-Free GUI Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15542)
*Yichao Liu,Huawen Shen,Liu Yu,Shiyu Liu,Zeyu Chen,Yu Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DRS-GUI 是一项为 GUI 智能体设计的无训练框架，通过模拟人类视觉的“聚焦、移动、分散”策略，结合蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）动态筛选界面元素，显著解决了高分辨率屏幕下的精准定位难题，性能提升 14%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于多模态大模型（MLLM）的 GUI 智能体在处理高分辨率、包含大量无关组件的复杂界面时，难以精准定位与指令相关的元素。该研究旨在解决这一“定位难”的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 DRS-GUI 的无需训练的动态区域搜索框架，包含：1. UI Perceptor：执行“聚焦（Focus）”、“移动（Shift）”和“分散（Scatter）”三种感知动作以探索界面；2. Action Planner：基于蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）动态调度感知动作，并利用区域质量奖励来筛选最相关的 UI 元素。

Result: 在 ScreenSpot-Pro 基准测试中，DRS-GUI 使通用和 GUI 专用多模态大模型（如 Qwen2.5-VL-7B 和 UGround-V1-7B）的定位性能提升了 14%，有效增强了模型在复杂 GUI 环境下的泛化能力和定位精度。

Conclusion: DRS-GUI 证明了通过模仿人类视觉感知策略，即使在训练自由（training-free）的约束下，也能有效利用蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）来优化 GUI 界面中的任务相关元素定位，显著提升了多模态大模型的交互准确性。

Abstract: GUI agents powered by Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated impressive capability in understanding and executing user instructions. However, accurately grounding instruction-relevant elements from high-resolution screenshots cluttered with irrelevant UI components remains challenging for existing approaches. Inspired by how humans dynamically adjust their perceptual scope to locate task-related regions on complex screens, we propose DRS-GUI, a training-free dynamic region search framework for GUI grounding that can be seamlessly integrated into existing MLLMs. DRS-GUI introduces a lightweight UI Perceptor that performs three human-like perceptual actions (Focus, Shift, and Scatter) to progressively explore the interface and generate region proposals. To dynamically schedule these actions, we further design an Action Planner based on Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS). A region quality reward is employed to evaluate and select the highly instruction-relevant region, efficiently pruning redundant UI elements. Experiments demonstrate that DRS-GUI yields a 14\% improvement on ScreenSpot-Pro for general and GUI-specific MLLMs (Qwen2.5-VL-7B and UGround-V1-7B), significantly enhancing grounding performance and generalization.

</details>

Result: 通过在联邦学习（Federated Learning）案例中的应用，验证了元认知策略能显著提升学习效率、模型效果及安全性。此外，作者开源的软件框架为社区提供了一个实现和验证元认知AI设计的工具，推动了该研究方向的实践进程。

Conclusion: 元认知是构建更准确、安全和高效人工智能系统的核心设计原则。通过赋予AI系统自我监控和资源分配的能力，可以有效应对复杂环境中的不确定性。作者提供的框架不仅为研究提供了理论支持，也为元认知在实际应用（如联邦学习）中的落地提供了可行性路径。

Abstract: This position paper argues for metacognition as a general design principle for creating more accurate, secure, and efficient AI. The metacognitive solution involves systems monitoring their own states and judiciously allocating resources depending on each problem instance's difficulty or cost of mistakes. Drawing inspiration both from past work on resource-rational AI and from well-documented metacognitive strategies in psychology and cognitive science, we identify specific challenges in embedding these strategies into AI design and highlight open theoretical and implementation problems. We showcase these principles through a tangible example of improved learning efficiency, effectiveness, and security in a Federated Learning (FL) case study. We show how these principles can be translated into practice with a novel software framework developed specifically to allow the community to design, deploy, and experiment with metacognition-enabled AI applications.

### [148] [See Before You Code: Learning Visual Priors for Spatially Aware Educational Animation Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15585)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型生成的教育动画代码常出现元素重叠、对齐错误及动画连续性中断等视觉缺陷。由于这些问题仅在代码执行渲染后才能发现，现有的代码生成模型难以直接解决，因此需要一种具备渲染反馈意识的生成机制。

Method: 提出OmniManim框架，包含四个核心部分：1) 共享场景状态管理；2) 显式视觉规划（利用Vision Agent进行关键帧布局预测和边界框去噪）；3) 结构化渲染后诊断；4) 基于反馈的局部代码修复。此外，通过引入插值感知目标函数来优化中间帧的渲染效果。

Result: 在EduRequire-500数据集上，OmniManim在渲染质量、指令遵循和可执行性方面均优于现有的单模型和多智能体基准框架。消融实验证实，视觉规划中的粗略空间先验和边界框细化是提升质量的关键。

Conclusion: OmniManim通过引入显式视觉规划、渲染反馈机制以及局部修复策略，有效解决了大模型在生成教育动画时存在的视觉缺陷问题，为高质量、可执行的动画代码生成提供了可靠的框架和评估基准。

Abstract: Large language models can generate executable code for educational animations, but the resulting renders often exhibit visual defects, including element overlap, misalignment, and broken animation continuity. These defects cannot be reliably detected from the code alone and become apparent only after execution. We formalize this problem as render-feedback-aware constrained code generation: given a natural language specification, the model must generate executable code whose rendered output satisfies structured quality criteria that can be evaluated only after rendering. To address this problem, we introduce OmniManim, a render-feedback-aware educational animation generation framework built around a shared scene state, explicit visual planning, structured post-render diagnostics, and localized repair. Within OmniManim, the Vision Agent is a task-specific visual planning module: it predicts sparse keyframe layouts with coarse-to-fine bounding-box denoising and optimizes an interpolation-aware objective to reduce intermediate-frame failures induced by downstream animation interpolation. We further construct two datasets, ManimLayout-1K and EduRequire-500, and provide a reproducible evaluation protocol covering executability, instructional quality, visual quality, and efficiency. On EduRequire-500, OmniManim improves measured render quality over both single-model baselines and existing multi-agent frameworks. Systematic ablation studies further verify that explicit visual planning, especially its coarse spatial prior, bounding-box refinement, and interpolation-aware optimization, is central to these gains.

Abstract: We introduce ColPackAgent, an agent framework that autonomously runs Monte Carlo simulations of colloidal packing through a Model Context Protocol (MCP) tool server and an agent skill, whether as a standalone agent or inside an existing agent system. By harnessing the MCP server and agent skill, ColPackAgent executes a structured workflow for colloidal packing simulations, which are central to studies of phase behavior, self-assembly, and materials design. Without dedicated simulation tools and workflow instructions, general-purpose Large Language Model (LLM) agents tend to describe such workflows rather than execute them reliably. The MCP server exposes a custom-built colpack Python package that wraps HOOMD-blue hard-particle Monte Carlo, and the skill encodes a four-stage workflow contract. ColPackAgent can carry out the workflow interactively with human feedback, autonomously from an end-to-end prompt, or as autoresearch following a provided program file. We demonstrate the system in different modes with several colloidal packing simulation examples such as cube particles in 3D, a binary system of disks and capsules in 2D, and the 2D hard-disk freezing transition using autoresearch. We also compare model performance on this workflow across a panel of LLMs with 17 stage-specific prompts. This benchmark provides a stage-level check of how reliably different models follow the setup, planning, and analysis workflow. Together, these results show that pairing a domain Python package with MCP tools and a portable agent skill provides a practical route for turning a simulation toolkit into an agent-assisted research workflow.

### [150] [Nudging Beyond the Comfort Zone: Efficient Strategy-Guided Exploration for RLVR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15726)
*Chanuk Lee,Sangwoo Park,Minki Kang,Sung Ju Hwang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NudgeRL 是一种用于大语言模型推理任务的新型强化学习框架，通过引入结构化的“策略引导”和分解奖励优化目标，实现了高效的多样性探索，在显著降低计算资源消耗的同时超越了大规模采样和基于预言机的强化学习方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习中带有可验证奖励（RLVR）的方法受限于探索效率，传统的暴力增加采样数量代价昂贵，而现有的优化目标修改方法对探索过程的控制力有限。本研究旨在通过引入结构化和多样性驱动的探索，解决 RLVR 中的探索效率瓶颈。

Method: 提出 NudgeRL 框架，包含两个核心部分：1. 策略引导（Strategy Nudging）：通过轻量级的策略级语境（context）引导采样，促进推理路径的多样性；2. 统一优化目标：将奖励信号分解为跨语境和语境内部组件，并引入蒸馏目标，将发现的优质策略行为迁移回基础模型。

Result: 在五个具有挑战性的数学基准测试中，NudgeRL 的表现优于标准的 GRPO（即使后者使用了 8 倍的采样预算），同时也优于基于预言机指导的强化学习基线，证明了其在计算效率和性能提升上的优势。

Conclusion: NudgeRL 证明了结构化、基于语境的探索是应对强化学习中探索瓶颈的有效且可扩展的方案，无需依赖昂贵的预言机监督即可超越大规模暴力采样，为提升大语言模型的推理能力提供了一种高效的新途径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a scalable paradigm for improving the reasoning capabilities of large language models. However, its effectiveness is fundamentally limited by exploration: the policy can only improve on trajectories it has already sampled. While increasing the number of rollouts alleviates this issue, such brute-force scaling is computationally expensive, and existing approaches that modify the optimization objective provide limited control over what is explored. In this work, we propose NudgeRL, a framework for structured and diversity-driven exploration in RLVR. Our approach introduces Strategy Nudging, which conditions each rollout on lightweight, strategy-level contexts to induce diverse reasoning trajectories without relying on expensive oracle supervision. To effectively learn from such structured exploration, we further propose a unified objective, which decomposes the reward signal into inter- and intra-context components and incorporates a distillation objective to transfer discovered behaviors back to the base policy. Empirically, NudgeRL outperforms standard GRPO with up to 8 times larger rollout budgets, while outperforming oracle-guided RL baseline on average across five challenging math benchmarks. These results demonstrate that structured, context-driven exploration can serve as an efficient and scalable alternative to both brute-force rollout scaling and feasibility-oriented methods based on privileged information. Our code is available at https://github.com/tally0818/NudgeRL.

</details>


### [151] [Can We Trust AI-Inferred User States. A Psychometric Framework for Validating the Reliability of Users States Classification by LLMs in Operational Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15734)
*Izabella Krzeminska,Michal Butkiewicz,Ewa Komkowska*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究通过实证评估发现，大语言模型评估用户状态的指标在个体层面大多缺乏可靠性，仅少数指标适用于实时自适应系统，并为此提出了一个可复制的指标评估框架以促进AI设计的负责任应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前利用大语言模型评估用户状态的自适应系统，往往基于“评估指标在个体层面具有稳定性和可解释性”这一假设。研究者旨在通过实证手段检验这一假设，揭示人工智能测量用户状态时的心理测量学可靠性问题。

Method: 研究采用了复制评估程序，对三种双模态大语言模型（GPT-4o audio, Gemini 2.0 Flash, Gemini 2.5 Flash）在广泛指标集上的可重复性进行了实证评估。分析涵盖了单个分数可靠性和聚合可靠性，并提出了一个可复制的评估框架，用于衡量指标的适用性。

Result: 研究发现指标可靠性并非普遍存在，213个指标中仅有31个符合可靠性标准。个体分数层面的不稳定性限制了其在实时自适应系统中的应用，但这些指标在经过聚合后或在事后分析（post-hoc studies）中仍具有识别交互规律和用户体验参数的相关价值。

Conclusion: 在大规模语言模型驱动的自适应系统中，不能将指标稳定性视为默认属性。个体层面的分数缺乏可靠性，这意味着在实时自适应系统中直接应用这些指标存在风险。开发者在设计系统时，必须对指标的可靠性进行明确的验证，并监控随时间产生的偏差，以实现更负责任的AI设计。

Abstract: The use of large language models to assess user states in conversational and adaptive systems is based on the assumption that the metrics used for such assessment are stable and interpretable at the level of individual scores. This paper empirically tests this assumption, focusing on the psychometric reliability of artificial intelligence (AI) measures of user states.
  This study employed replication evaluation procedures to assess the repeatability of a broad set of metrics across three different bimodal large language models (GPT-4o audio, Gemini 2.0 Flash, Gemini 2.5 Flash). Analyses include both individual score reliability and aggregated reliability, allowing us to distinguish metrics potentially useful for real-time adaptation from those that retain their value only in aggregated analyses.
  The results demonstrate that metric reliability cannot be considered a default property in interpretive domains. The lack of stability at the level of individual scores precludes the interpretation of such scores as indicators of user state in real-time adaptive systems, even if these metrics demonstrate stability after aggregation. At the same time, the study indicates that individually unstable metrics can retain analytical utility in post-hoc studies, identifying rules governing interactions and their relationships with user experience parameters such as satisfaction, trust, and engagement.
  The main contribution of this work, besides quantifying the severity of the problem (only 31 of 213 metrics met the criteria), is the proposal of a replicable evaluation framework, enabling measurable evaluations of metric applicability. This approach supports more responsible AI design of adaptive systems, in which the interpretation of results requires explicit validation of reliability and monitoring for violations over time.

</details>

*Kean Shi,Zihang Li,Tianyi Ma,Zengji Tu,Jialong Wu,Xinbo Xu,Qingyao Yang,Ruoyu Wu,Weichu Xie,Ming Wu,Jason Zeng,Michael Heinrich,Elvis Zhang,Liang Chen,Kuan Li,Baobao Chang*

Abstract: Computer-Using Agents (CUAs) are rapidly extending large language models (LLMs) beyond text-based reasoning toward action execution in more complex environments, such as web browsers and graphical user interfaces (GUIs). However, existing web and GUI agent benchmarks often rely on simplified settings, isolated tasks, or short-horizon interactions, making it difficult to assess capabilities of agents in realistic professional workflows. Software-as-a-Service (SaaS) environments are a natural choice for CUA evaluation, as they host a large share of modern digital work and naturally involve dynamic system states, cross-application coordination, domain-specific knowledge, and long-horizon dependencies. To this end, we introduce SaaS-Bench, a benchmark built on 23 deployable SaaS systems across six professional domains, containing 106 tasks grounded in realistic work scenarios. These tasks require long-horizon execution, cover both text-only and multimodal settings, and are evaluated with weighted verification checkpoints that measure strict task completion and partial progress. Experiments show that representative LLM-based agents struggle on SaaS-Bench, with even the strongest model completing fewer than 4% of tasks end-to-end, exposing limitations in planning, state tracking, cross-application context maintenance, and error recovery. Code are available at https://github.com/UniPat-AI/SaaS-Bench for reproduction.

### [153] [Agentic Discovery of Neural Architectures: AIRA-Compose and AIRA-Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15871)
*Alberto Pepe,Chien-Yu Lin,Despoina Magka,Bilge Acun,Yannan Nellie Wu,Anton Protopopov,Carole-Jean Wu,Yoram Bachrach*

TL;DR: 该论文提出了AIRA双框架，利用多智能体协作自主设计并优化基础模型架构，成功开发出在性能和扩展效率上均超越主流模型（如Llama 3.2）的新架构，验证了AI驱动递归自我改进的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一个双框架方法：AIRA-Compose（用于高层架构搜索）和AIRA-Design（用于底层机制实现）。AIRA-Compose利用11个智能体在24小时内搜索计算原语，并将设计扩展至不同规模；AIRA-Design利用20个智能体编写新型注意力机制和训练脚本。

Result: AIRA系列模型（AIRAformers和AIRAhybrids）在1B规模预训练中表现优于Llama 3.2；下游任务中，AIRAformer-D和AIRAhybrid-D精度分别提升2.4%和3.8%；在扩展效率上，AIRA-C系列模型较Llama 3.2、Nemotron-2等基准有显著提升；在长序列任务及基准测试中，表现接近或超过人类顶尖水平。

Conclusion: 研究证明，AI智能体能够自主发现架构和算法优化，其性能可达到甚至超越人类专家设计的基准。这为发现下一代基础模型提供了一种强大的新范式，是迈向递归自我改进的重要一步。

Abstract: Toward recursive self-improvement, we investigate LLM agents autonomously designing foundation models beyond standard Transformers. We introduce a dual-framework approach: AIRA-Compose for high-level architecture search, and AIRA-Design for low-level mechanistic implementation. AIRA-Compose uses 11 agents to explore fundamental computational primitives under a 24-hour budget. Agents evaluate million-parameter candidates, extrapolating top designs to 350M, 1B, and 3B scales. This yields 14 architectures across two families: AIRAformers (Transformer-based) and AIRAhybrids (Transformer-Mamba). Pre-trained at 1B scale, these consistently outperform Llama 3.2 and Composer-found baselines. On downstream tasks, AIRAformer-D and AIRAhybrid-D improve accuracy by 2.4% and 3.8% over Llama 3.2. Furthermore, AIRA-Compose finds models with highly efficient scaling frontiers: AIRAformer-C scales 54% and 71% faster than Llama 3.2 and Composer's best Transformer, while AIRAhybrid-C outscales Nemotron-2 by 23% and Composer's best hybrid by 37%. AIRA-Design tasks 20 agents with writing novel attention mechanisms for long-range dependencies and high-performing training scripts. On the Long Range Arena benchmark, agent-designed architectures reach within 2.3% and 2.6% of human state-of-the-art on document matching and text classification. On the Autoresearch benchmark, Greedy Opus 4.5 achieves 0.968 validation bits-per-byte under a fixed time budget, surpassing the published minimum. Together, these frameworks show AI agents can autonomously discover architectures and algorithmic optimizations matching or surpassing hand-designed baselines. This establishes a powerful paradigm for discovering next-generation foundation models, marking a clear step toward recursive self-improvement.

### [154] [Imperfect World Models are Exploitable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15960)
*Logan Mondal Bhamidipaty,Esmeralda S. Whitammer,David Abel,Mykel J. Kochenderfer,Subramanian Ramamoorthy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种量化强化学习中“模型开发”的新理论，证明了该现象在大型策略空间中不可避免，并为模型驱动的强化学习指出了安全规划的理论边界与适用范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习中的模型开发（即模型对环境的错误建模导致策略评估偏差）是一个严峻挑战。研究旨在形式化定义“模型开发”，探索其与“奖励操纵”的联系，并回答在世界模型中进行安全规划是否具有理论上的必然限制。

Method: 提出了模型开发（model exploitation）的新定义，将其与奖励操纵（reward hacking）类比；构建了关于这两者的通用理论，通过数学推导证明了在大规模策略集中开发行为的必然性；探讨了有限策略集中避免操纵的条件，并引入了松弛化的开发定义以推导出安全规划的有效范围。

Result: 证明了模型开发在大规模策略集中是必然存在的；发现有限策略集中防止奖励操纵的条件无法直接推广至防止模型开发；通过松弛化定义，计算出了一个能够规避模型开发的“安全视界（safe horizon）”。

Conclusion: 本研究通过建立奖励操纵与模型开发之间的理论关联，揭示了在大型策略集中模型开发是不可避免的。研究指出了安全规划的局限性，并提供了一个基于松弛定义的安全时间范围，为理解强化学习中的模型不确定性与安全性提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We propose a novel definition of model exploitation in reinforcement learning. Informally, a world model is exploitable if it implies that one policy should be strictly preferred over another while the environment's true transition model implies the reverse. We analogize our definition with a prior characterization of reward hacking but show that the associated proof of inevitability does not transfer to exploitation. To overcome this obstruction, we develop a general theory of reward hacking and model exploitation that proves that exploitation is essentially unavoidable on large policy sets and yields the corresponding claim for hacking as a special case. Unfortunately, we also find that the conditions that guarantee unhackability in finite policy sets have no counterpart that precludes exploitation. Consequently, we introduce a relaxed notion of exploitation and derive a safe horizon within which it can be avoided. Taken together, our results establish a formal bridge between reward hacking and model exploitation and elucidate the limits of safe planning in world models.

</details>


### [155] [Petri Net Induced Heuristic Search for Resource Constrained Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15983)
*Ido Lublin,Dor Atzmon,Izack Cohen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于带资源时间变迁Petri网（TTPN）的RCPSP求解方法，利用启发式A*搜索在可达图上进行最优决策，在PSPLIB基准测试中展现出比传统MIP求解器更优的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统求解RCPSP的方法（如混合整数线性规划MIP）在处理大规模或特定约束条件下的问题时效率有限，研究者希望通过探索状态空间搜索（Petri网方法）来寻找更高效的求解路径。

Method: 1. 将RCPSP建模为带资源时间变迁Petri网（TTPN）的可达图搜索问题，引入“相对延迟令牌”使调度决策与状态空间中的变迁触发对应；
2. 采用A*搜索算法求解，并设计了一种结合关键路径和基于资源下界的启发式函数；
3. 证明了该启发式在所提出的令牌时间语义下的相容性。

Result: 在PSPLIB基准测试中，该方法在成功率和求解时间上均优于主流的MIP求解器（SCIP, CBC）；分析表明，A*搜索与MIP的性能退化分别受资源紧缺度和问题规模大小影响，且资源强度决定了哪种求解器更具优势。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用带资源时间变迁Petri网（TTPN）对RCPSP进行建模，并结合特定的启发式A*算法，能够有效处理资源受限的项目调度问题，特别是在资源紧缺的场景下表现优于传统MIP求解器。

Abstract: We formulate the Resource-Constrained Project Scheduling Problem (RCPSP) as optimal search over the reachability graph of a Timed Transition Petri Net with Resources, using relative-delay tokens so that scheduling decisions correspond to transition firings in the induced state space. We solve the resulting problem with $A^*$ guided by a heuristic that combines Critical Path and resource-based lower bounds, and prove that it is consistent under our token-based time semantics. Experiments on the PSPLIB benchmarks show that the approach outperforms strong exact Mixed-Integer Linear Programming (MIP) baselines (SCIP, CBC) in both success rate and solve time. Per-instance analysis shows that heuristic search and MIP degrade along independent axes, resource tightness for $A^*$ and formulation size for MIP, with resource strength mediating which solver benefits from scale.

### [156] [ScreenSearch: Uncertainty-Aware OS Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16024)
*Michael Solodko,Justin Wagle*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ScreenSearch是一个针对桌面GUI智能体的探索框架，通过状态去重和引入基于动作结果离散度的歧义感知机制，解决了桌面任务中视觉相似但状态不同的难题，实现了更高效的大规模状态探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 桌面GUI智能体面临部分可观测性挑战，即外观相似的屏幕可能代表不同的任务状态。现有的探索方法往往无法有效处理这种歧义，导致智能体在类似屏幕上采取错误的动作，因此需要一种能主动区分状态并高效探索桌面环境的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为ScreenSearch的系统，包含两个核心模块：1. 基于结构化特征和UIA树的屏幕检索与去重机制，用于跨VM构建共享的状态图；2. 基于PUCT图老虎机的探索策略，通过引入“匹配动作结果离散度”作为歧义信号，驱动智能体主动探测易混淆的状态，而非盲目进行探索。

Result: 在11个桌面应用程序上成功采集了超过100万张截图和3万个去重状态。实验表明，该系统能有效识别歧义状态，通过引入歧义信号与前沿奖励的协同，实现了对桌面环境的大规模探索，并揭示了 novelty（新颖性）与 ambiguity（歧义性）之间的权衡关系。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在桌面GUI智能体的探索任务中，状态识别、动作建议质量以及对歧义的感知（ambiguity-aware search）是构建鲁棒智能体的三个核心要素。单纯追求降低歧义不足以实现充分探索，必须在探索新前沿与消除状态歧义之间取得平衡。

Abstract: Desktop GUI agents operate under partial observability: visually similar screens can correspond to different underlying workflow states, so locally plausible actions can lead to sharply different outcomes. We frame this as a problem of computer/OS state exploration, where effective behavior requires both expanding the reachable frontier and reducing ambiguity before committing. We present ScreenSearch, a system that combines structural screen retrieval and deduplication with an ambiguity-aware PUCT graph-bandit for large-scale desktop exploration. The retrieval layer converts UIA trees into location-aware structural features, indexes related screens through sparse token search and metadata filters, and maintains a shared deduplicated state graph across VM workers. On top of this graph, we define a scalable ambiguity signal based on matched-action outcome dispersion. If similar screens produce different next states under the same action signature, the state should be probed further rather than treated as resolved. We use this signal together with frontier rewards to drive large-scale exploration and replay-start policy evaluation over the shared graph. Across 11 desktop applications, ScreenSearch collects over 1M screenshots and over 30K deduplicated states, yielding large exploration corpora with substantial cross-application and within-application diversity. On a fixed replay-start slice, we observe a clear novelty--ambiguity trade-off: some policies reduce ambiguity quickly while discovering little frontier. Ambiguity reduction alone is therefore not a sufficient exploration objective. Appendix ablations show that stronger proposal priors can materially improve unique-state discovery during corpus building. These results suggest that state identity, proposal quality, and ambiguity-aware search all matter when deciding when to probe and when to commit.

Abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have significantly enhanced automated legal reasoning. Yet, it remains unclear whether their performance reflects genuine legal reasoning ability or artifacts of data contamination. We present a comprehensive empirical study of tax law reasoning approaches and implement a contamination detection protocol to rigorously assess LLM reliability. We show that performance can be inflated by contamination. Building on this analysis, we conduct a systematic evaluation, comparing monolithic LLMs with hybrid systems that translate statutory text into formal representations and delegate inference to symbolic solvers. We build a novel test suite designed to probe generalization to unseen documents via case and rule variations. Our findings indicate that legal reasoning is inherently compositional and that neuro-symbolic frameworks offer a more reliable and robust foundation for legal AI, as well as improved generalization to unobserved situations.

### [158] [Sign-Separated Finite-Time Error Analysis of Q-Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16103)
*Donghwan Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过将Q学习误差分解为正负两部分，揭示了贝尔曼最大化操作导致的“误差不对称性”，从理论上解释了过估计现象，并推导出恒定步长Q学习的有限时间收敛界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决现有Q学习误差分析中对过估计现象理解不足的问题，通过深入剖析恒定步长Q学习的有限时间误差动态，探究其非对称性误差演化机制，从而弥补以往对Q学习收敛特性分析的局限性。

Method: 采用了基于切换系统（switching-system）的表示法，将Q学习的误差分解为正、负分量。针对负向分量，构建了由最优策略主导的下界比较线性时不变（LTI）系统；针对正向分量，构建了线性切换系统进行分析，并推导了确定性和随机恒定步长递归下的有限时间误差界。

Result: 研究结果表明，Q学习的负向误差项受到比正向切换项更强的约束，可能呈现更快的指数衰减。该分析精确地识别出由贝尔曼算子（Bellman maximum）传播正向误差带来的非对称性，并为常数步长Q学习在不同噪声设置下提供了严谨的有限时间收敛边界。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了Q学习中误差动态的“最大值诱导不对称性”（max-induced asymmetry），并论证了这种不对称性是导致过估计现象的根源。通过将误差分解为正负部分，研究表明负向误差受最优策略下的线性时不变系统约束，而正向误差则受到切换系统的影响，进而证明了正负误差在收敛速率上的本质差异。

Abstract: This paper develops a sign-separated finite-time error analysis for constant step-size Q-learning. Starting from the switching-system representation, the error is decomposed into its componentwise negative and positive parts. The negative part is dominated by a lower comparison linear time-invariant (LTI) system associated with a fixed optimal policy, whereas the positive part is controlled by a linear switching system. The resulting bounds show that the negative-side LTI certificate is no slower than the positive-side switching certificate and may produce a faster exponential envelope. The analysis identifies a max-induced asymmetry in Q-learning error dynamics. This asymmetry is connected to overestimation: positive action-wise errors can be selected and propagated by the Bellman maximum, whereas negative errors admit an optimal-policy lower comparison. Finite-time bounds are provided for both deterministic and stochastic constant-step-size recursions.

</details>


### [159] [ShopGym: An Integrated Framework for Realistic Simulation and Scalable Benchmarking of E-Commerce Web Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16116)
*Chinmay Savadikar,Mingyu Zhao,Yuanzheng Zhu,Han Li,Shuang Xie,Alberto Castelo,Tianfu Wu,Lingyun Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了 ShopGym 框架，包含两个核心模块：1. ShopArena：通过分阶段、经过验证的生成过程，将实时电商平台转换为包含匿名规范的自包含沙盒商店；2. ShopGuru：在这些模拟商店基础上，结合目录、导航结构和交互功能，合成涵盖七个技能类别的基准任务。

Abstract: Developing and evaluating e-commerce web agents requires environments that preserve meaningful task structure while enabling controllable, reproducible, and scalable scientific comparison. Existing methodologies force a tradeoff: live storefronts provide realism but are non-stationary, difficult to inspect, and irreproducible, while hand-built sandbox benchmarks provide control but cover only a narrow range of layouts, catalogs, policies, and interaction patterns. We argue that the core bottleneck is methodological: the field lacks a scalable way to construct evaluation settings that are simultaneously realistic, diverse, controllable, inspectable, and reproducible. We introduce ShopGym, an integrated framework for realistic simulation and scalable benchmarking of e-commerce web agents. ShopGym is a framework for constructing e-commerce simulation environments and grounded benchmark tasks. Its simulation layer, ShopArena, converts live seed storefronts into self-contained sandbox shops through anonymized shop specifications and a staged, validated generation process. On top of these simulated storefronts, ShopGuru synthesizes benchmark tasks across seven skill categories, grounding each task in the shop's catalog, navigation structure, policies, and interaction affordances. Together, ShopArena and ShopGuru produce self-contained, resettable, inspectable, and stable evaluation artifacts that preserve structural properties and agent-evaluation signals relevant to shopping tasks. We validate the framework through graph-based structural analysis and agent-based behavioral evaluation with 224 generated tasks across six sandbox shops: three constructed with synthetic data and three with real data. Our results show that the synthetic shops preserve key structural properties of live storefronts, with agent performance on synthetic shops positively correlated with performance on live storefronts.
